    1  import logging
    2  import threading
    3  import time
    4  from dotenv import load_dotenv
    5  load_dotenv()
    6  
    7  import config
    8  from broker import AlpacaBroker
    9  from risk import RiskManager
   10  from agent import TradingAgent
   11  from memory import TradingMemory
   12  from analyzer import TradeAnalyzer
   13  from dashboard import start_dashboard
   14  from notifier import TradingNotifier
   15  
   16  logging.basicConfig(
   17      level=logging.INFO,
   18      format='%(asctime)s %(levelname)s %(message)s'
   19  )
   20  logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
   21  
   22  WATCHDOG_INTERVAL_SECONDS = 60
   23  
   24  
   25  def _make_fast_thread(agent: TradingAgent) -> threading.Thread:
   26      """Create (but do not start) a new fast loop daemon thread."""
   27      def _run():
   28          logger.info("[FAST] ⚡ Fast loop thread started — 30s tick")
   29          while True:
   30              try:
   31                  agent.fast_loop_tick()
   32              except Exception as e:
   33                  logger.error(f"[FAST] loop error: {e}")
   34              time.sleep(config.FAST_LOOP_INTERVAL_SECONDS)
   35  
   36      return threading.Thread(target=_run, daemon=True, name="FastLoop")
   37  
   38  
   39  def _run_watchdog(agent: TradingAgent, thread_ref: list):
   40      """
   41      Daemon thread — wakes every 60 seconds.
   42      Checks whether the fast loop thread is still alive.
   43      If dead, spawns a fresh replacement and updates thread_ref[0].
   44      """
   45      while True:
   46          time.sleep(WATCHDOG_INTERVAL_SECONDS)
   47          t = thread_ref[0]
   48          if t.is_alive():
   49              logger.info("[WATCHDOG] fast loop alive ✅")
   50          else:
   51              logger.warning("[WATCHDOG] fast loop dead — restarting 🔄")
   52              new_thread = _make_fast_thread(agent)
   53              new_thread.start()
   54              thread_ref[0] = new_thread
   55              logger.info("[WATCHDOG] fast loop restarted successfully ✅")
   56  
   57  
   58  def main():
   59      logger.info("🚀 Trading Agent starting...")
   60  
   61      memory   = TradingMemory("trading_memory.db")
   62      broker   = AlpacaBroker()
   63      risk     = RiskManager(broker)
   64      agent    = TradingAgent(broker, risk, memory)
   65      analyzer = TradeAnalyzer(memory)
   66      notifier = TradingNotifier(memory, analyzer)
   67  
   68      start_dashboard(memory, analyzer, scanner=agent.scanner, regime=agent.regime, agent=agent, port=5000)
   69      notifier.start_scheduler(daily_hour_utc=20)
   70  
   71      # ── Start the fast loop ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
   72      fast_thread = _make_fast_thread(agent)
   73      fast_thread.start()
   74  
   75      # thread_ref is a mutable list so the watchdog can swap in a replacement
   76      thread_ref = [fast_thread]
   77  
   78      # ── Start the watchdog ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   79      watchdog_thread = threading.Thread(
   80          target=_run_watchdog,
   81          args=(agent, thread_ref),
   82          daemon=True,
   83          name="Watchdog",
   84      )
   85      watchdog_thread.start()
   86  
   87      logger.info(
   88          f"✅ All systems running — "
   89          f"fast loop: {config.FAST_LOOP_INTERVAL_SECONDS}s | "
   90          f"slow loop: {config.LOOP_INTERVAL_SECONDS}s | "
   91          f"watchdog: {WATCHDOG_INTERVAL_SECONDS}s"
   92      )
   93  
   94      # ── Slow loop (main thread) ───────────────────────────────────────────────
   95      cycle = 0
   96      while True:
   97          try:
   98              cycle += 1
   99              logger.info(f"[SLOW] --- Cycle {cycle} ---")
  100  
  101              if risk.check_global_stop_loss():
  102                  logger.error("🔴 GLOBAL STOP LOSS — shutting down")
  103                  broker.close_all_positions()
  104                  notifier.send_stop_loss_alert(
  105                      broker.get_portfolio_value()
  106                  )
  107                  break
  108  
  109              # Hand off symbols the fast loop already triggered this cycle
  110              skip_symbols = agent.consume_fast_triggered()
  111              if skip_symbols:
  112                  logger.info(
  113                      f"[SLOW] ⏭ Fast loop triggered {len(skip_symbols)} symbol(s) "
  114                      f"this cycle — skipping in slow scan: {sorted(skip_symbols)}"
  115                  )
  116  
  117              agent.run_cycle(skip_symbols=skip_symbols)
  118              analyzer.run_pending_analyses()
  119  
  120              anomalies = analyzer.detect_performance_anomalies()
  121              if anomalies:
  122                  logger.warning(f"[SLOW] {len(anomalies)} anomalie(s) detected")
  123  
  124              time.sleep(config.LOOP_INTERVAL_SECONDS)
  125  
  126          except KeyboardInterrupt:
  127              logger.info("⛔ Agent stopped by user")
  128              break
  129          except Exception as e:
  130              logger.error(f"[SLOW] Cycle error: {e}")
  131              time.sleep(30)
  132  
  133  
  134  if __name__ == "__main__":
  135      main()
