    1  import json
    2  import logging
    3  import threading
    4  import uuid
    5  from datetime import datetime, timezone, time as dtime
    6  import anthropic
    7  import config
    8  import pytz
    9  from correlations import CorrelationIntelligence
   10  from geometry import GeometryAnalysis
   11  from regime import MarketRegime
   12  from synthesis import SynthesisEngine
   13  from scanner import MarketScanner
   14  from strategy import (
   15      compute_indicators,
   16      compute_opportunity_score,
   17      detect_patterns,
   18      get_session_context,
   19      build_strategy_prompt,
   20      rank_symbols,
   21      is_good_stock_window,
   22      is_crypto_good_hours,
   23  )
   24  
   25  SCORE_LONG_MIN  = 60   # Score above this → bullish signal → call Claude (long candidate)
   26  SCORE_SHORT_MAX = 30   # Score below this → bearish signal → call Claude (short candidate)
   27  # Scores between 30–60 = ambiguous, no clear signal → skip Claude entirely
   28  
   29  SHORT_TRAIL_PCT = 0.03   # Short positions: trailing stop 3% above lowest price reached
   30  
   31  logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
   32  
   33  class TradingAgent:
   34      def __init__(self, broker, risk_manager, memory=None):
   35          self.broker = broker
   36          self.risk = risk_manager
   37          self.memory = memory
   38          self.client = anthropic.Anthropic(api_key=config.ANTHROPIC_API_KEY)
   39          self.scanner       = MarketScanner()
   40          self.regime        = MarketRegime()
   41          self.correlations  = CorrelationIntelligence()
   42          self.geometry      = GeometryAnalysis()
   43          self.synthesis     = SynthesisEngine(
   44              self.regime, self.correlations, self.geometry, self.scanner
   45          )
   46          # Tracks highest price seen per LONG position (for trailing stop)
   47          self._high_water: dict = {}
   48          # Tracks lowest price seen per SHORT position (for trailing stop)
   49          self._low_water: dict = {}
   50          # Symbols for which partial profit has already been taken this session
   51          self._partial_taken: set = set()
   52          # Score-based trailing stop % per symbol (set at entry, read during management)
   53          self._trail_pcts: dict = {}
   54          # Daily dedup: date string (YYYY-MM-DD ET) when cash liberation last fired
   55          self._cash_lib_last_date: str = ""
   56          # Two-speed loop: dedup + cross-loop coordination
   57          self._last_analyzed: dict  = {}  # symbol → UTC datetime of last Claude call
   58          self._fast_triggered: set  = set()  # symbols triggered by fast loop this cycle
   59          self._lock = threading.Lock()      # guards _last_analyzed, _fast_triggered
   60          # Pre-close: date (YYYY-MM-DD ET) when stock pre-close already fired today
   61          self._preclose_done_date: str = ""
   62  
   63      def _sync_orphan_positions(self):
   64          """Detect Alpaca positions with no matching open SQLite record and create them."""
   65          if not self.memory:
   66              return
   67          try:
   68              alpaca_positions = self.broker.get_positions()
   69              if not alpaca_positions:
   70                  return
   71              open_trades = self.memory.get_open_trades()
   72              open_symbols = {t["symbol"].replace("/", "").upper(): t for t in open_trades}
   73              synced = 0
   74              for pos in alpaca_positions:
   75                  sym_normalized = pos.symbol.replace("/", "").upper()
   76                  if sym_normalized in open_symbols:
   77                      continue
   78                  # Determine proper display symbol (crypto: "BTCUSD" → "BTC/USD")
   79                  display_symbol = pos.symbol
   80                  for crypto in config.CRYPTO_SYMBOLS:
   81                      if crypto.replace("/", "").upper() == sym_normalized:
   82                          display_symbol = crypto
   83                          break
   84                  side        = "buy" if getattr(pos, "side", "long") == "long" else "sell"
   85                  qty         = abs(float(pos.qty))
   86                  entry_price = float(pos.avg_entry_price)
   87                  trade_id    = str(uuid.uuid4())
   88                  logger.info(
   89                      f"🔄 SYNC orphan: {display_symbol} {side} qty={qty:.6g} "
   90                      f"entry=${entry_price:.4f} — writing to SQLite"
   91                  )
   92                  self.memory.log_trade_open(
   93                      trade_id=trade_id,
   94                      symbol=display_symbol,
   95                      side=side,
   96                      qty=qty,
   97                      entry_price=entry_price,
   98                      alpaca_order_id=f"orphan_{sym_normalized}",
   99                      market_context={"source": "alpaca_sync",
  100                                      "synced_at": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()},
  101                  )
  102                  synced += 1
  103              if synced:
  104                  logger.info(f"✅ Orphan sync complete: {synced} position(s) added to SQLite")
  105          except Exception as e:
  106              logger.error(f"_sync_orphan_positions error: {e}")
  107  
  108      def _pre_market_cash_liberation(self):
  109          """
  110          9:25 AM ET weekdays — per-position rules to free cash for stock market open:
  111            • Negative position          → skip (let trailing stop manage it)
  112            • Profitable but < +2% gain  → sell 100% (weak overnight, free all capital)
  113            • Profitable and >= +2% gain → sell 50%  (keep half running with trailing stop)
  114          """
  115          ET = pytz.timezone("America/New_York")
  116          now_et = datetime.now(ET)
  117  
  118          # Weekdays only
  119          if now_et.weekday() >= 5:
  120              return
  121  
  122          # Window: 9:23 – 9:28 AM ET (covers any 5-min cycle that straddles 9:25)
  123          t = now_et.time()
  124          if not (dtime(9, 23) <= t <= dtime(9, 28)):
  125              return
  126  
  127          # Daily dedup — fire at most once per calendar day
  128          today_str = now_et.strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
  129          if self._cash_lib_last_date == today_str:
  130              return
  131  
  132          # Mark immediately to prevent double-fire if an error occurs mid-loop
  133          self._cash_lib_last_date = today_str
  134  
  135          # Fetch all open positions from Alpaca
  136          try:
  137              positions = self.broker.get_positions()
  138          except Exception as e:
  139              logger.error(f"_pre_market_cash_liberation: cannot fetch positions: {e}")
  140              return
  141  
  142          if not positions:
  143              logger.info("💤 PRE-MARKET LIBERATION (9:25 ET): no open positions")
  144              return
  145  
  146          # Filter to long crypto positions only
  147          crypto_positions = []
  148          for pos in positions:
  149              if not self._is_crypto(pos.symbol):
  150                  continue
  151              try:
  152                  if getattr(pos, "side", "long") != "long" or float(pos.qty) <= 0:
  153                      continue
  154                  crypto_positions.append(pos)
  155              except Exception:
  156                  continue
  157  
  158          if not crypto_positions:
  159              logger.info("💤 PRE-MARKET LIBERATION (9:25 ET): no open crypto positions")
  160              return
  161  
  162          logger.info(
  163              f"⏰ PRE-MARKET LIBERATION triggered (9:25 ET) — "
  164              f"evaluating {len(crypto_positions)} crypto position(s)"
  165          )
  166  
  167          freed_total = 0.0
  168  
  169          for pos in crypto_positions:
  170              try:
  171                  current_price = float(pos.current_price)
  172                  avg_entry     = float(pos.avg_entry_price)
  173                  qty_total     = float(pos.qty)
  174  
  175                  # Resolve display symbol (e.g. "BTCUSD" → "BTC/USD")
  176                  display_sym = pos.symbol
  177                  for crypto in config.CRYPTO_SYMBOLS:
  178                      if crypto.replace("/", "").upper() == pos.symbol.replace("/", "").upper():
  179                          display_sym = crypto
  180                          break
  181  
  182                  # Position gain %
  183                  if avg_entry <= 0:
  184                      continue
  185                  pos_gain_pct = (current_price - avg_entry) / avg_entry * 100
  186  
  187                  # ── Rule 1: Negative → skip ──────────────────────────────────
  188                  if pos_gain_pct < 0:
  189                      logger.info(
  190                          f"  ↳ PRE-MARKET LIBERATION: {display_sym} "
  191                          f"{pos_gain_pct:+.2f}% — HOLDING (negative, trailing stop managing)"
  192                      )
  193                      continue
  194  
  195                  # ── Rule 2: Profitable < +2% → sell 100% ────────────────────
  196                  # ── Rule 3: Profitable >= +2% → sell 50% ────────────────────
  197                  if pos_gain_pct < 2.0:
  198                      sell_ratio = 1.00
  199                      sell_pct_label = "100%"
  200                  else:
  201                      sell_ratio = 0.50
  202                      sell_pct_label = "50%"
  203  
  204                  sell_qty = round(qty_total * sell_ratio, 8)
  205                  if sell_qty <= 0:
  206                      continue
  207  
  208                  freed = sell_qty * current_price
  209                  freed_total += freed
  210  
  211                  logger.info(
  212                      f"💵 PRE-MARKET LIBERATION: {display_sym} "
  213                      f"{pos_gain_pct:+.2f}% — selling {sell_pct_label} "
  214                      f"— freeing ${freed:.2f} for market open"
  215                  )
  216  
  217                  order = self.broker.place_order(display_sym, sell_qty, "sell")
  218  
  219                  # Update SQLite memory
  220                  if order and self.memory:
  221                      try:
  222                          open_trades = self.memory.get_open_trades()
  223                          match = next(
  224                              (t for t in open_trades
  225                               if t.get("symbol", "").replace("/", "").upper()
  226                                  == pos.symbol.replace("/", "").upper()
  227                               and t.get("status") == "open"),
  228                              None,
  229                          )
  230                          if match:
  231                              pnl     = (current_price - float(match["entry_price"])) * sell_qty
  232                              pnl_pct = (current_price - float(match["entry_price"])) / float(match["entry_price"]) * 100
  233                              self.memory.log_trade_close(
  234                                  match["trade_id"],
  235                                  exit_price=current_price,
  236                                  close_reason="pre_market_cash_liberation",
  237                                  pnl=round(pnl, 4),
  238                                  pnl_pct=round(pnl_pct, 4),
  239                              )
  240                      except Exception as me:
  241                          logger.warning(f"Memory update after liberation ({display_sym}): {me}")
  242  
  243              except Exception as e:
  244                  logger.error(f"Cash liberation error for {pos.symbol}: {e}")
  245  
  246          if freed_total > 0:
  247              logger.info(
  248                  f"✅ PRE-MARKET LIBERATION complete — "
  249                  f"${freed_total:.2f} total freed ahead of 9:30 open"
  250              )
  251          else:
  252              logger.info(
  253                  "💤 PRE-MARKET LIBERATION complete — "
  254                  "no positions sold (all negative or zero qty)"
  255              )
  256  
  257      def _is_crypto(self, alpaca_symbol: str) -> bool:
  258          """Alpaca returns crypto as 'BTCUSD'; our config uses 'BTC/USD'."""
  259          normalized = alpaca_symbol.replace("/", "")
  260          return any(normalized == s.replace("/", "") for s in config.CRYPTO_SYMBOLS)
  261  
  262      # ── Two-speed loop helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
  263  
  264      def _was_recently_analyzed(self, symbol: str, window_seconds: int = 180) -> bool:
  265          """Return True if Claude was called for this symbol within the last N seconds."""
  266          with self._lock:
  267              last = self._last_analyzed.get(symbol)
  268          if last is None:
  269              return False
  270          return (datetime.now(timezone.utc) - last).total_seconds() < window_seconds
  271  
  272      def _mark_analyzed(self, symbol: str):
  273          """Record the UTC time of the most recent Claude call for this symbol."""
  274          with self._lock:
  275              self._last_analyzed[symbol] = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
  276  
  277      def consume_fast_triggered(self) -> set:
  278          """Return (and clear) the set of symbols triggered by the fast loop since last slow cycle."""
  279          with self._lock:
  280              triggered = set(self._fast_triggered)
  281              self._fast_triggered.clear()
  282          return triggered
  283  
  284      def _check_hard_stops(self, positions):
  285          """[FAST] Close any LONG position whose loss exceeds TRADE_STOP_LOSS_PCT."""
  286          for pos in (positions or []):
  287              try:
  288                  if getattr(pos, "side", "long") == "short":
  289                      continue
  290                  current_price = float(pos.current_price)
  291                  avg_entry     = float(pos.avg_entry_price)
  292                  if avg_entry <= 0:
  293                      continue
  294                  loss_pct = (avg_entry - current_price) / avg_entry
  295                  if loss_pct >= config.TRADE_STOP_LOSS_PCT:
  296                      symbol = pos.symbol
  297                      logger.info(
  298                          f"[FAST] 🛑 FAST STOP: {symbol} hard stop hit at {current_price:.6g} "
  299                          f"— loss capped at {loss_pct*100:.1f}%"
  300                      )
  301                      closed = self.broker.close_position(symbol)
  302                      if closed:
  303                          self._high_water.pop(symbol, None)
  304                          self._trail_pcts.pop(symbol, None)
  305                          self._partial_taken.discard(symbol)
  306                          if self.memory:
  307                              try:
  308                                  open_trades = self.memory.get_recent_trades(limit=50)
  309                                  match = next(
  310                                      (t for t in open_trades
  311                                       if t.get("symbol", "").replace("/", "") == symbol.replace("/", "")
  312                                       and t.get("status") == "open"),
  313                                      None,
  314                                  )
  315                                  if match:
  316                                      qty_m   = float(match["qty"])
  317                                      pnl     = (current_price - float(match["entry_price"])) * qty_m
  318                                      pnl_pct = -round(loss_pct * 100, 4)
  319                                      self.memory.log_trade_close(
  320                                          match["trade_id"],
  321                                          exit_price=current_price,
  322                                          close_reason="hard_stop_loss",
  323                                          pnl=round(pnl, 4),
  324                                          pnl_pct=pnl_pct,
  325                                      )
  326                              except Exception as me:
  327                                  logger.warning(f"[FAST] Memory update after hard stop ({symbol}): {me}")
  328              except Exception as e:
  329                  logger.error(f"[FAST] Hard stop check error: {e}")
  330  
  331      def _preclose_stocks(self, positions: list, today_str: str) -> None:
  332          """
  333          Close all equity (non-crypto) positions at 15:55 ET to avoid overnight
  334          exposure.  Fires at most once per calendar day (guarded by _preclose_done_date).
  335          """
  336          if self._preclose_done_date == today_str:
  337              return
  338          self._preclose_done_date = today_str
  339          stock_positions = [p for p in positions if "/" not in p.symbol]
  340          if not stock_positions:
  341              logger.info("[Pre-close] No equity positions to close before 16:00 ET")
  342              return
  343          for pos in stock_positions:
  344              symbol = pos.symbol
  345              try:
  346                  current_price = float(pos.current_price)
  347                  closed = self.broker.close_position(symbol)
  348                  if closed:
  349                      logger.info(f"[Pre-close] ✅ Closed {symbol} before 16:00 ET")
  350                      # Clean up in-memory state
  351                      self._high_water.pop(symbol, None)
  352                      self._low_water.pop(symbol, None)
  353                      self._trail_pcts.pop(symbol, None)
  354                      self._partial_taken.discard(symbol)
  355                      # Update SQLite record
  356                      if self.memory:
  357                          try:
  358                              open_trades = self.memory.get_recent_trades(limit=50)
  359                              match = next(
  360                                  (t for t in open_trades
  361                                   if t.get("symbol", "") == symbol
  362                                   and t.get("status") == "open"),
  363                                  None,
  364                              )
  365                              if match:
  366                                  qty_m   = float(match["qty"])
  367                                  pnl     = (current_price - float(match["entry_price"])) * qty_m
  368                                  pnl_pct = round(pnl / (float(match["entry_price"]) * qty_m) * 100, 4)
  369                                  self.memory.log_trade_close(
  370                                      match["trade_id"],
  371                                      exit_price=current_price,
  372                                      close_reason="pre_market_close",
  373                                      pnl=round(pnl, 4),
  374                                      pnl_pct=pnl_pct,
  375                                  )
  376                          except Exception as me:
  377                              logger.warning(f"[Pre-close] Memory update for {symbol}: {me}")
  378              except Exception as e:
  379                  logger.error(f"[Pre-close] ❌ Failed to close {symbol}: {e}")
  380  
  381      def _close_dust_positions(self, positions: list, threshold: float = 5.0) -> None:
  382          """
  383          Close any open position whose absolute market value is below `threshold`
  384          (default $5).  These 'dust' positions tie up a slot without meaningful
  385          upside.
  386          """
  387          for pos in positions:
  388              symbol = pos.symbol
  389              try:
  390                  market_value = abs(float(pos.market_value))
  391                  if market_value >= threshold:
  392                      continue
  393                  current_price = float(pos.current_price)
  394                  closed = self.broker.close_position(symbol)
  395                  if closed:
  396                      logger.info(
  397                          f"[Dust] 🧹 Closed dust position: {symbol} "
  398                          f"(market_value=${market_value:.2f} < ${threshold:.0f})"
  399                      )
  400                      self._high_water.pop(symbol, None)
  401                      self._low_water.pop(symbol, None)
  402                      self._trail_pcts.pop(symbol, None)
  403                      self._partial_taken.discard(symbol)
  404                      if self.memory:
  405                          try:
  406                              open_trades = self.memory.get_recent_trades(limit=50)
  407                              match = next(
  408                                  (t for t in open_trades
  409                                   if t.get("symbol", "") == symbol
  410                                   and t.get("status") == "open"),
  411                                  None,
  412                              )
  413                              if match:
  414                                  qty_m   = float(match["qty"])
  415                                  pnl     = (current_price - float(match["entry_price"])) * qty_m
  416                                  pnl_pct = round(pnl / (float(match["entry_price"]) * qty_m) * 100, 4)
  417                                  self.memory.log_trade_close(
  418                                      match["trade_id"],
  419                                      exit_price=current_price,
  420                                      close_reason="dust_cleanup",
  421                                      pnl=round(pnl, 4),
  422                                      pnl_pct=pnl_pct,
  423                                  )
  424                          except Exception as me:
  425                              logger.warning(f"[Dust] Memory update for {symbol}: {me}")
  426              except Exception as e:
  427                  logger.error(f"[Dust] Failed to close {symbol}: {e}")
  428  
  429      def fast_loop_tick(self):
  430          """
  431          FAST LOOP — called every 30 seconds from a background thread.
  432          0. Pre-close stocks at 15:55 ET (weekdays only, once per day)
  433          1. Trailing stop check  → FAST EXIT log
  434          2. Hard stop check      → FAST STOP log
  435          3. Dust cleanup: close positions with market_value < $5
  436          4. RSI/MACD/volume scan → compute raw opportunity score
  437          5. Score > 60 or < 30  → FAST TRIGGER → call Claude immediately
  438          6. Volume > 5× average → VOLUME SPIKE log
  439          Never calls Claude directly; triggers analyze_market() when threshold crossed.
  440          """
  441          # ── 0: Pre-close equity positions at 15:55 ET ─────────────────────────
  442          now_et    = datetime.now(pytz.timezone("America/New_York"))
  443          today_str = now_et.strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
  444          if now_et.weekday() < 5 and now_et.hour == 15 and now_et.minute >= 55:
  445              try:
  446                  preclose_positions = self.broker.get_positions() or []
  447              except Exception:
  448                  preclose_positions = []
  449              self._preclose_stocks(preclose_positions, today_str)
  450  
  451          # ── 1 & 2: Position management ────────────────────────────────────────
  452          try:
  453              positions = self.broker.get_positions() or []
  454          except Exception as e:
  455              logger.error(f"[FAST] Cannot fetch positions: {e}")
  456              positions = []
  457  
  458          self._manage_trailing_stops(loop_tag="FAST")
  459          self._manage_short_trailing_stops(loop_tag="FAST")
  460          self._check_hard_stops(positions)
  461          self._close_dust_positions(positions)
  462  
  463          # ── 4-6: Technical scan (no movers refresh — uses cached data) ────────
  464          session_ctx = get_session_context()
  465          session     = session_ctx["session"]
  466  
  467          # Build fast watchlist from session rules + cached movers
  468          fast_watchlist: list[str] = []
  469          if is_good_stock_window():
  470              fast_watchlist.extend(config.BLUECHIP_SYMBOLS)
  471          if is_crypto_good_hours():
  472              fast_watchlist.extend(config.CRYPTO_SYMBOLS)
  473          cached_movers = self.scanner._movers_cache.get("symbols", [])
  474          for m in cached_movers[:5]:
  475              sym = m.get("symbol")
  476              if sym and sym not in fast_watchlist:
  477                  fast_watchlist.append(sym)
  478  
  479          for symbol in fast_watchlist:
  480              # Skip symbols recently analyzed (3-min window)
  481              if self._was_recently_analyzed(symbol, window_seconds=180):
  482                  continue
  483  
  484              try:
  485                  bars = self.broker.get_bars(symbol)
  486                  if bars is None or bars.empty:
  487                      continue
  488                  bars50  = bars.tail(50)
  489                  prices  = bars50["close"].tolist()
  490                  volumes = bars50["volume"].tolist()
  491                  if len(prices) < 20:
  492                      continue
  493  
  494                  indicators = compute_indicators(prices, volumes)
  495                  if "error" in indicators:
  496                      continue
  497                  opens50  = bars50["open"].tolist()
  498                  highs50  = bars50["high"].tolist()
  499                  lows50   = bars50["low"].tolist()
  500                  patterns = detect_patterns(indicators, session)
  501                  score    = compute_opportunity_score(indicators, patterns)
  502  
  503                  # ── 5: Volume spike ───────────────────────────────────────────
  504                  sample   = volumes[-20:] if len(volumes) >= 20 else volumes
  505                  avg_vol  = sum(sample) / len(sample) if sample else 1
  506                  last_vol = volumes[-1] if volumes else 0
  507                  ratio    = last_vol / avg_vol if avg_vol > 0 else 1.0
  508                  if ratio >= 5.0:
  509                      logger.info(
  510                          f"[FAST] ⚡ VOLUME SPIKE: {symbol} {ratio:.1f}x average — monitoring"
  511                      )
  512  
  513                  # ── 4: Score threshold → synthesis gate → Claude ─────────────
  514                  if score > 60 or score < 30:
  515                      _side = "long" if score > 60 else "short"
  516  
  517                      # Run full synthesis before calling Claude — same gate as slow loop
  518                      try:
  519                          open_pos_syms = [p.symbol for p in positions]
  520                          synth = self.synthesis.run(
  521                              symbol=symbol,
  522                              base_score=score,
  523                              opens=opens50, highs=highs50, lows=lows50,
  524                              closes=prices, volumes=volumes,
  525                              open_positions=open_pos_syms,
  526                              side=_side,
  527                          )
  528                      except Exception as synth_err:
  529                          logger.warning(f"[FAST] Synthesis error on {symbol}: {synth_err}")
  530                          synth = {
  531                              "final_score": score, "should_call_claude": True,
  532                              "full_context": "", "stop_loss": None, "take_profit": None,
  533                              "stop_pct": None, "target_pct": None, "risk_reward": None,
  534                              "size_multiplier": 1.0,
  535                          }
  536  
  537                      final_score = synth["final_score"]
  538  
  539                      # Hard gate: synthesis must approve before Claude is called
  540                      if not synth.get("should_call_claude", True):
  541                          reason = synth.get("decision_reason", "synthesis score below threshold")
  542                          logger.info(
  543                              f"[FAST] ⛔ SYNTHESIS SKIP {symbol}: {reason} "
  544                              f"(raw={score:.0f} → synth={final_score:.0f})"
  545                          )
  546                          if self.memory:
  547                              self.memory.log_decision(
  548                                  decision="hold",
  549                                  reasoning=(
  550                                      f"[FAST] Synthesis blocked Claude call — {reason}. "
  551                                      f"Breakdown: {synth.get('score_breakdown', '')}"
  552                                  ),
  553                                  symbol=symbol,
  554                                  confidence=0.0,
  555                              )
  556                          continue
  557  
  558                      logger.info(
  559                          f"[FAST] 🎯 FAST TRIGGER: {symbol} score={score:.0f} "
  560                          f"→ synth={final_score:.0f} → calling Claude now"
  561                      )
  562                      self._mark_analyzed(symbol)
  563                      with self._lock:
  564                          self._fast_triggered.add(symbol)
  565  
  566                      market_context = self.scanner.build_market_context()
  567                      synth_ctx      = synth.get("full_context", "")
  568                      try:
  569                          decision = self.analyze_market(
  570                              symbol, bars,
  571                              market_context=f"{market_context}\n\n{synth_ctx}" if synth_ctx else market_context,
  572                          )
  573                      except Exception as e:
  574                          logger.error(f"[FAST] analyze_market error {symbol}: {e}")
  575                          continue
  576  
  577                      if not decision:
  578                          continue
  579  
  580                      action     = decision.get("decision", "hold")
  581                      confidence = decision.get("confidence", 0)
  582                      logger.info(
  583                          f"[FAST] {symbol}: {action.upper()} conf={confidence:.0%} — "
  584                          f"{decision.get('reasoning', '')[:120]}"
  585                      )
  586  
  587                      if self.memory:
  588                          self.memory.log_decision(
  589                              decision=action,
  590                              reasoning=f"[FAST TRIGGER] {decision.get('reasoning', '')}",
  591                              symbol=symbol,
  592                              confidence=confidence,
  593                          )
  594  
  595                      regime_params = self.regime.get_params()
  596                      min_conf      = regime_params["confidence_threshold"] / 100
  597                      current_price = float(bars["close"].iloc[-1])
  598  
  599                      if action == "buy" and confidence >= min_conf:
  600                          if self.risk.can_trade():
  601                              qty, pct, trail_pct = self.risk.get_position_size_by_score(
  602                                  symbol, current_price, final_score
  603                              )
  604                              # Prefer ATR-anchored stop/target from synthesis geometry layer
  605                              geo_sl = synth.get("stop_loss")
  606                              geo_tp = synth.get("take_profit")
  607                              sl     = geo_sl if geo_sl else self.risk.calculate_stop_loss(current_price, "buy")
  608                              if geo_sl and synth.get("stop_pct"):
  609                                  stop_pct = synth["stop_pct"] / 100
  610                                  if stop_pct < trail_pct:
  611                                      trail_pct = stop_pct
  612                              amount = qty * current_price
  613                              rr_str = f" | R:R={synth.get('risk_reward', 0):.1f}x" if synth.get("risk_reward") else ""
  614                              tp_str = f" | target=${geo_tp:.4f}" if geo_tp else ""
  615                              logger.info(
  616                                  f"[FAST] TRADE ENTRY: {symbol} buy | score={final_score:.0f} "
  617                                  f"| position={pct*100:.0f}% = ${amount:,.2f} "
  618                                  f"| stop=${sl:.4f}{tp_str}{rr_str}"
  619                              )
  620                              order = self.broker.place_order(symbol, qty, "buy", sl, take_profit=geo_tp)
  621                              self._trail_pcts[symbol] = trail_pct
  622                              if order and self.memory:
  623                                  try:
  624                                      self.memory.log_trade_open(
  625                                          trade_id=str(uuid.uuid4()),
  626                                          symbol=symbol,
  627                                          side="buy",
  628                                          qty=qty,
  629                                          entry_price=current_price,
  630                                          stop_loss=sl,
  631                                          market_context={
  632                                              "source": "fast_loop_trigger",
  633                                              "score": final_score,
  634                                          },
  635                                      )
  636                                  except Exception as me:
  637                                      logger.warning(f"[FAST] Memory log entry ({symbol}): {me}")
  638  
  639                      elif action == "sell" and confidence >= min_conf:
  640                          logger.info(
  641                              f"[FAST] TRADE EXIT: {symbol} sell signal | conf={confidence:.0%}"
  642                          )
  643                          self.broker.close_position(symbol)
  644  
  645              except Exception as e:
  646                  logger.error(f"[FAST] Scan error {symbol}: {e}")
  647  
  648      # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  649  
  650      def _manage_trailing_stops(self, loop_tag: str = ""):
  651          """Check every open LONG position against its score-based trailing stop."""
  652          try:
  653              positions = self.broker.get_positions()
  654          except Exception as e:
  655              logger.error(f"_manage_trailing_stops: could not fetch positions: {e}")
  656              return
  657  
  658          for pos in positions:
  659              try:
  660                  if getattr(pos, "side", "long") == "short" or float(pos.qty) < 0:
  661                      continue
  662              except Exception:
  663                  continue
  664  
  665              symbol = pos.symbol
  666              try:
  667                  current_price = float(pos.current_price)
  668                  current_qty   = abs(float(pos.qty))
  669                  # Use score-based trailing %; fall back to 5% if position pre-dates session
  670                  trail_pct = self._trail_pcts.get(symbol, 0.05)
  671  
  672                  # ── Partial profit taking (+5% → sell 50%) ─────────────────
  673                  unrealised_pct = float(getattr(pos, "unrealized_plpc", 0))
  674                  if (unrealised_pct >= config.PARTIAL_PROFIT_PCT
  675                          and symbol not in self._partial_taken
  676                          and current_qty > 0):
  677                      sell_qty = round(current_qty * config.PARTIAL_PROFIT_RATIO, 4)
  678                      if sell_qty > 0:
  679                          remaining_qty  = current_qty - sell_qty
  680                          remaining_val  = remaining_qty * current_price
  681                          secured_val    = sell_qty * current_price
  682                          logger.info(
  683                              f"💰 PARTIAL PROFIT: {symbol} sold 50% at "
  684                              f"+{unrealised_pct*100:.1f}% — "
  685                              f"${secured_val:,.2f} secured — "
  686                              f"remaining 50% running with {trail_pct*100:.0f}% trailing stop"
  687                          )
  688                          order = self.broker.place_order(symbol, sell_qty, "sell")
  689                          self._partial_taken.add(symbol)
  690  
  691                          # ── Update SQLite: close old record, reopen with remaining qty ──
  692                          if self.memory:
  693                              try:
  694                                  open_trades = self.memory.get_open_trades()
  695                                  match = next(
  696                                      (t for t in open_trades
  697                                       if t.get("symbol", "").replace("/", "").upper()
  698                                          == symbol.replace("/", "").upper()
  699                                       and t.get("status") == "open"),
  700                                      None,
  701                                  )
  702                                  if match:
  703                                      entry_p = float(match["entry_price"])
  704                                      pnl     = (current_price - entry_p) * sell_qty
  705                                      pnl_pct = (current_price - entry_p) / entry_p * 100 if entry_p > 0 else 0
  706                                      # Close the original record (for the sold portion)
  707                                      self.memory.log_trade_close(
  708                                          match["trade_id"],
  709                                          exit_price=current_price,
  710                                          close_reason="partial_profit",
  711                                          pnl=round(pnl, 4),
  712                                          pnl_pct=round(pnl_pct, 4),
  713                                      )
  714                                      # Reopen a new record for the remaining 50%
  715                                      if remaining_qty > 0:
  716                                          self.memory.log_trade_open(
  717                                              trade_id=str(uuid.uuid4()),
  718                                              symbol=match["symbol"],
  719                                              side="buy",
  720                                              qty=remaining_qty,
  721                                              entry_price=entry_p,
  722                                              stop_loss=match.get("stop_loss"),
  723                                              alpaca_order_id=match.get("alpaca_order_id"),
  724                                              market_context={"source": "partial_profit_remainder"},
  725                                          )
  726                              except Exception as me:
  727                                  logger.warning(f"Memory update after partial profit ({symbol}): {me}")
  728  
  729                  # Initialise high-water mark on first sight (or after restart)
  730                  if symbol not in self._high_water:
  731                      self._high_water[symbol] = current_price
  732                      logger.info(
  733                          f"📈 Trailing stop init: {symbol} "
  734                          f"high={current_price:.6g} trail={trail_pct*100:.0f}%"
  735                      )
  736                      continue
  737  
  738                  new_high = max(self._high_water[symbol], current_price)
  739                  self._high_water[symbol] = new_high
  740                  stop_level = new_high * (1 - trail_pct)
  741  
  742                  logger.debug(
  743                      f"  {symbol}: price={current_price:.6g} "
  744                      f"high={new_high:.6g} stop={stop_level:.6g} trail={trail_pct*100:.0f}%"
  745                  )
  746  
  747                  if current_price <= stop_level:
  748                      if loop_tag:
  749                          logger.info(
  750                              f"[{loop_tag}] FAST EXIT: {symbol} trailing stop hit at "
  751                              f"{current_price:.6g} (peak={new_high:.6g}, -{trail_pct*100:.0f}%)"
  752                          )
  753                      else:
  754                          logger.info(
  755                              f"[SLOW] 🔴 TRAILING STOP HIT: {symbol} "
  756                              f"price={current_price:.6g} < stop={stop_level:.6g} "
  757                              f"(peak={new_high:.6g}, -{trail_pct*100:.0f}%)"
  758                          )
  759                      closed = self.broker.close_position(symbol)
  760                      if closed:
  761                          self._high_water.pop(symbol, None)
  762                          self._trail_pcts.pop(symbol, None)
  763                          self._partial_taken.discard(symbol)
  764                          if self.memory:
  765                              try:
  766                                  open_trades = self.memory.get_recent_trades(limit=50)
  767                                  match = next(
  768                                      (t for t in open_trades
  769                                       if t.get("symbol", "").replace("/", "") == symbol.replace("/", "")
  770                                       and t.get("status") == "open"),
  771                                      None
  772                                  )
  773                                  if match:
  774                                      entry  = float(match["entry_price"])
  775                                      qty_m  = float(match["qty"])
  776                                      pnl    = (current_price - entry) * qty_m
  777                                      pnl_pct = (current_price - entry) / entry * 100
  778                                      logger.info(
  779                                          f"TRADE EXIT: {symbol} | reason=trailing_stop "
  780                                          f"| pnl=${pnl:+.2f} ({pnl_pct:+.2f}%)"
  781                                      )
  782                                      self.memory.log_trade_close(
  783                                          match["trade_id"],
  784                                          exit_price=current_price,
  785                                          close_reason="trailing_stop",
  786                                          pnl=pnl,
  787                                      )
  788                              except Exception as me:
  789                                  logger.warning(f"Memory update after trailing stop: {me}")
  790              except Exception as e:
  791                  logger.error(f"Trailing stop error for {symbol}: {e}")
  792  
  793      def _manage_short_trailing_stops(self, loop_tag: str = ""):
  794          """Check every SHORT position — trailing stop 3% above the lowest price reached."""
  795          try:
  796              positions = self.broker.get_positions()
  797          except Exception as e:
  798              logger.error(f"_manage_short_trailing_stops: could not fetch positions: {e}")
  799              return
  800  
  801          for pos in positions:
  802              try:
  803                  side    = getattr(pos, "side", "long")
  804                  qty_val = float(pos.qty)
  805                  if side != "short" and qty_val >= 0:
  806                      continue
  807              except Exception:
  808                  continue
  809  
  810              symbol = pos.symbol
  811              try:
  812                  current_price = float(pos.current_price)
  813                  current_qty   = abs(qty_val)
  814                  trail_pct     = SHORT_TRAIL_PCT   # always 3% for shorts
  815  
  816                  # ── Partial profit taking (+5% → cover 50%) ────────────────
  817                  short_key      = f"short:{symbol}"
  818                  unrealised_pct = float(getattr(pos, "unrealized_plpc", 0))
  819                  if (unrealised_pct >= config.PARTIAL_PROFIT_PCT
  820                          and short_key not in self._partial_taken
  821                          and current_qty > 0):
  822                      cover_qty     = round(current_qty * config.PARTIAL_PROFIT_RATIO, 4)
  823                      if cover_qty > 0:
  824                          remaining_qty = current_qty - cover_qty
  825                          remaining_val = remaining_qty * current_price
  826                          secured_val   = cover_qty * current_price
  827                          logger.info(
  828                              f"💰 PARTIAL PROFIT: {symbol} sold 50% at "
  829                              f"+{unrealised_pct*100:.1f}% — "
  830                              f"${secured_val:,.2f} secured — "
  831                              f"remaining 50% running with {trail_pct*100:.0f}% trailing stop"
  832                          )
  833                          self.broker.place_order(symbol, cover_qty, "buy")
  834                          self._partial_taken.add(short_key)
  835  
  836                          # ── Update SQLite: close old record, reopen with remaining qty ──
  837                          if self.memory:
  838                              try:
  839                                  open_trades = self.memory.get_open_trades()
  840                                  match = next(
  841                                      (t for t in open_trades
  842                                       if t.get("symbol", "").replace("/", "").upper()
  843                                          == symbol.replace("/", "").upper()
  844                                       and t.get("status") == "open"
  845                                       and t.get("side") == "sell"),
  846                                      None,
  847                                  )
  848                                  if match:
  849                                      entry_p = float(match["entry_price"])
  850                                      pnl     = (entry_p - current_price) * cover_qty
  851                                      pnl_pct = (entry_p - current_price) / entry_p * 100 if entry_p > 0 else 0
  852                                      self.memory.log_trade_close(
  853                                          match["trade_id"],
  854                                          exit_price=current_price,
  855                                          close_reason="partial_profit",
  856                                          pnl=round(pnl, 4),
  857                                          pnl_pct=round(pnl_pct, 4),
  858                                      )
  859                                      if remaining_qty > 0:
  860                                          self.memory.log_trade_open(
  861                                              trade_id=str(uuid.uuid4()),
  862                                              symbol=match["symbol"],
  863                                              side="sell",
  864                                              qty=remaining_qty,
  865                                              entry_price=entry_p,
  866                                              stop_loss=match.get("stop_loss"),
  867                                              alpaca_order_id=match.get("alpaca_order_id"),
  868                                              market_context={"source": "partial_profit_remainder"},
  869                                          )
  870                              except Exception as me:
  871                                  logger.warning(f"Memory update after short partial profit ({symbol}): {me}")
  872  
  873                  # Initialise low-water mark on first sight (or after restart)
  874                  if symbol not in self._low_water:
  875                      self._low_water[symbol] = current_price
  876                      logger.info(
  877                          f"📉 Short trailing stop init: {symbol} "
  878                          f"low={current_price:.6g} trail={trail_pct*100:.0f}%"
  879                      )
  880                      continue
  881  
  882                  new_low    = min(self._low_water[symbol], current_price)
  883                  self._low_water[symbol] = new_low
  884                  stop_level = new_low * (1 + trail_pct)
  885  
  886                  logger.debug(
  887                      f"  SHORT {symbol}: price={current_price:.6g} "
  888                      f"low={new_low:.6g} stop={stop_level:.6g} trail={trail_pct*100:.0f}%"
  889                  )
  890  
  891                  if current_price >= stop_level:
  892                      if loop_tag:
  893                          logger.info(
  894                              f"[{loop_tag}] FAST EXIT: {symbol} short trailing stop hit at "
  895                              f"{current_price:.6g} (trough={new_low:.6g}, +{trail_pct*100:.0f}%)"
  896                          )
  897                      else:
  898                          logger.info(
  899                              f"[SLOW] 🟢 SHORT TRAILING STOP HIT: {symbol} "
  900                              f"price={current_price:.6g} >= stop={stop_level:.6g} "
  901                              f"(trough={new_low:.6g}, +{trail_pct*100:.0f}%) — covering short"
  902                          )
  903                      cover_qty = abs(qty_val)
  904                      covered   = self.broker.place_order(symbol, cover_qty, "buy")
  905                      if covered:
  906                          self._low_water.pop(symbol, None)
  907                          self._partial_taken.discard(f"short:{symbol}")
  908                          if self.memory:
  909                              try:
  910                                  open_trades = self.memory.get_recent_trades(limit=50)
  911                                  match = next(
  912                                      (t for t in open_trades
  913                                       if t.get("symbol", "").replace("/", "") == symbol.replace("/", "")
  914                                       and t.get("status") == "open"
  915                                       and t.get("side") == "sell"),
  916                                      None
  917                                  )
  918                                  if match:
  919                                      entry   = float(match["entry_price"])
  920                                      pnl     = (entry - current_price) * cover_qty
  921                                      pnl_pct = (entry - current_price) / entry * 100
  922                                      logger.info(
  923                                          f"TRADE EXIT: {symbol} | reason=short_trailing_stop "
  924                                          f"| pnl=${pnl:+.2f} ({pnl_pct:+.2f}%)"
  925                                      )
  926                                      self.memory.log_trade_close(
  927                                          match["trade_id"],
  928                                          exit_price=current_price,
  929                                          close_reason="short_trailing_stop",
  930                                          pnl=pnl,
  931                                      )
  932                              except Exception as me:
  933                                  logger.warning(f"Memory update after short trailing stop: {me}")
  934              except Exception as e:
  935                  logger.error(f"Short trailing stop error for {symbol}: {e}")
  936  
  937      def analyze_market(self, symbol, bars, market_context: str = ""):
  938          if bars is None or bars.empty:
  939              return None
  940  
  941          recent = bars.tail(50)
  942          prices = recent['close'].tolist()
  943          volumes = recent['volume'].tolist()
  944  
  945          if len(prices) < 20:
  946              return None
  947  
  948          indicators = compute_indicators(prices, volumes)
  949          if "error" in indicators:
  950              return None
  951  
  952          session_ctx = get_session_context()
  953          patterns = detect_patterns(indicators, session_ctx["session"])
  954  
  955          memory_context = ""
  956          if self.memory:
  957              memory_context = self.memory.get_context_for_agent(symbol)
  958  
  959          regime_context = self.regime.build_regime_context()
  960          combined_context = f"{market_context}\n\n{regime_context}" if market_context else regime_context
  961  
  962          prompt = build_strategy_prompt(
  963              symbol=symbol,
  964              indicators=indicators,
  965              patterns=patterns,
  966              session_ctx=session_ctx,
  967              memory_context=memory_context,
  968              market_context=combined_context,
  969          )
  970  
  971          try:
  972              response = self.client.messages.create(
  973                  model="claude-sonnet-4-20250514",
  974                  max_tokens=500,
  975                  messages=[{"role": "user", "content": prompt}]
  976              )
  977              raw = response.content[0].text.strip()
  978              if raw.startswith("```"):
  979                  raw = raw.split("```")[1]
  980                  if raw.startswith("json"):
  981                      raw = raw[4:]
  982              result = json.loads(raw.strip())
  983              result["_indicators"] = indicators
  984              result["_patterns"] = patterns
  985              result["_session"] = session_ctx["session"]
  986              return result
  987          except Exception as e:
  988              logger.error(f"analyze_market error: {e}")
  989              return None
  990  
  991      def run_cycle(self, skip_symbols: set = None):
  992          """
  993          SLOW LOOP — called every 5 minutes from the main thread.
  994          skip_symbols: set of symbols already triggered+analyzed by the fast loop this cycle.
  995          """
  996          # 9:25 ET weekdays: free crypto cash ahead of stock market open
  997          self._pre_market_cash_liberation()
  998  
  999          # Sync any Alpaca positions that have no SQLite record (e.g. manual trades)
 1000          self._sync_orphan_positions()
 1001  
 1002          # NOTE: Trailing stop management is handled exclusively by the fast loop (every 30s).
 1003          # No trailing stop call here to avoid double-firing on simultaneous startup.
 1004  
 1005          if not self.risk.can_trade():
 1006              logger.warning("[SLOW] ⚠️ Trading paused by risk manager")
 1007              return
 1008  
 1009          session_ctx = get_session_context()
 1010          session = session_ctx["session"]
 1011          logger.info(
 1012              f"[SLOW] 📅 Session: {session} ({session_ctx['time_et']}) — "
 1013              f"stocks: {session_ctx['good_for_stocks']} | crypto: {session_ctx['good_for_crypto']}"
 1014          )
 1015  
 1016          # ── Regime-driven dynamic parameters ─────────────────────────────────
 1017          regime_params   = self.regime.get_params()
 1018          _regime         = regime_params["regime"]
 1019          score_long_min  = regime_params["score_long_threshold"]
 1020          score_short_max = regime_params["score_short_threshold"]
 1021          size_mult       = regime_params["position_size_multiplier"]
 1022          regime_conf_min = regime_params["confidence_threshold"] / 100
 1023          logger.info(
 1024              f"[SLOW] 🎯 Regime: {_regime.upper()} | "
 1025              f"long_min={score_long_min} | short_max={score_short_max} | "
 1026              f"size={size_mult}x | conf_min={regime_conf_min:.0%}"
 1027          )
 1028  
 1029          _skip = skip_symbols or set()
 1030          dynamic_watchlist = self.scanner.get_dynamic_watchlist()
 1031          symbols_to_scan = []
 1032          for symbol in dynamic_watchlist:
 1033              is_crypto = "/" in symbol
 1034              if is_crypto and not is_crypto_good_hours():
 1035                  continue
 1036              if not is_crypto and not is_good_stock_window():
 1037                  continue
 1038              # Skip symbols the fast loop already analyzed this cycle
 1039              if symbol in _skip:
 1040                  logger.info(f"[SLOW] ⏭ Skipping {symbol} — already triggered by fast loop")
 1041                  continue
 1042              symbols_to_scan.append(symbol)
 1043  
 1044          if not symbols_to_scan:
 1045              logger.info("[SLOW] 😴 No symbols to scan in current session — crypto off-hours and market closed")
 1046              return
 1047  
 1048          # Build market context once per cycle (news sentiment + top movers + calendar + earnings)
 1049          market_context = self.scanner.build_market_context()
 1050  
 1051          # ── Correlation intelligence — refresh prices once per cycle ──────────
 1052          corr_changes    = self.correlations.refresh_prices(symbols_to_scan)
 1053          dxy_trend       = self.regime._cache.get("dxy") or "neutral"
 1054          try:
 1055              _open_pos_list  = self.broker.get_positions() or []
 1056              open_pos_symbols = [p.symbol for p in _open_pos_list]
 1057          except Exception:
 1058              open_pos_symbols = []
 1059  
 1060          # Build earnings alert map: symbol → {type, days_away}
 1061          earnings_alerts_map = {ea["symbol"]: ea for ea in self.scanner.get_earnings_alerts()}
 1062  
 1063          symbols_data = {}
 1064          for symbol in symbols_to_scan:
 1065              try:
 1066                  bars = self.broker.get_bars(symbol)
 1067                  if bars is None or bars.empty:
 1068                      continue
 1069                  bars50  = bars.tail(50)
 1070                  prices  = bars50['close'].tolist()
 1071                  volumes = bars50['volume'].tolist()
 1072                  opens   = bars50['open'].tolist()
 1073                  highs   = bars50['high'].tolist()
 1074                  lows    = bars50['low'].tolist()
 1075                  if len(prices) < 20:
 1076                      continue
 1077                  indicators = compute_indicators(prices, volumes)
 1078                  patterns   = detect_patterns(indicators, session)
 1079                  symbols_data[symbol] = {
 1080                      "indicators": indicators, "patterns": patterns, "bars": bars,
 1081                      "opens": opens, "highs": highs, "lows": lows,
 1082                      "prices": prices, "volumes": volumes,
 1083                  }
 1084              except Exception as e:
 1085                  logger.error(f"Pre-scan error on {symbol}: {e}")
 1086  
 1087          ranked = rank_symbols({s: d for s, d in symbols_data.items()})
 1088          logger.info(f"[SLOW] 🔍 Scanning {len(ranked)} symbols — top: {ranked[:3]}")
 1089  
 1090          # Pre-filter: two-band score gate
 1091          #   score > 60 → bullish signal   → Claude evaluates for long
 1092          #   score < 30 → bearish signal   → Claude evaluates for short
 1093          #   30 ≤ score ≤ 60 → ambiguous   → skip (no API cost)
 1094          passed_long, passed_short, skipped, no_short_crypto = [], [], [], []
 1095          cached_movers_list = self.scanner._movers_cache.get("symbols", [])
 1096  
 1097          for symbol in ranked:
 1098              data      = symbols_data[symbol]
 1099              is_crypto = "/" in symbol
 1100              base_score = compute_opportunity_score(data["indicators"], data["patterns"])
 1101              _side      = "short" if base_score < 45 else "long"
 1102  
 1103              # ── Synthesis: all intelligence layers → one final score ─────────
 1104              try:
 1105                  synth = self.synthesis.run(
 1106                      symbol=symbol,
 1107                      base_score=base_score,
 1108                      opens=data["opens"], highs=data["highs"], lows=data["lows"],
 1109                      closes=data["prices"], volumes=data["volumes"],
 1110                      open_positions=open_pos_symbols,
 1111                      side=_side,
 1112                  )
 1113              except Exception as synth_err:
 1114                  logger.warning(f"Synthesis error on {symbol}: {synth_err}")
 1115                  synth = {
 1116                      "final_score": base_score, "should_call_claude": True,
 1117                      "full_context": "", "stop_loss": None, "take_profit": None,
 1118                      "stop_pct": None, "target_pct": None, "risk_reward": None,
 1119                      "size_multiplier": 1.0,
 1120                  }
 1121  
 1122              data["synthesis"] = synth
 1123              opp_score = synth["final_score"]
 1124              data["opportunity_score"] = opp_score
 1125  
 1126              # ── Earnings day: hard skip (stocks only) ──────────────────────
 1127              sym_base = symbol  # stocks use bare ticker; crypto keeps "BTC/USD"
 1128              ea = earnings_alerts_map.get(sym_base)
 1129              if ea and ea["type"] == "earnings_day" and not is_crypto:
 1130                  logger.info(f"EARNINGS DAY: skipping {symbol} — too risky to enter")
 1131                  if self.memory:
 1132                      self.memory.log_decision(
 1133                          decision="hold",
 1134                          reasoning=f"EARNINGS DAY: {symbol} reports today — no entry, volatility risk too high.",
 1135                          symbol=symbol,
 1136                          confidence=0.0,
 1137                      )
 1138                  continue
 1139  
 1140              # ── Post-earnings gapper: boost score if gap >5% ───────────────
 1141              if ea and ea["type"] == "post_earnings" and not is_crypto:
 1142                  mover_info = next((m for m in cached_movers_list if m["symbol"] == sym_base), None)
 1143                  if mover_info and mover_info.get("change_pct", 0) >= 5:
 1144                      logger.info(
 1145                          f"📈 POST-EARNINGS GAPPER: {symbol} +{mover_info['change_pct']:.1f}% "
 1146                          f"— boosting score to 90 (was {opp_score})"
 1147                      )
 1148                      opp_score = 90
 1149                      data["opportunity_score"] = 90
 1150  
 1151              if opp_score > score_long_min:
 1152                  passed_long.append(symbol)
 1153              elif opp_score < score_short_max:
 1154                  if is_crypto:
 1155                      no_short_crypto.append(symbol)
 1156                      logger.info(f"BEARISH CRYPTO {symbol}: no short on Alpaca")
 1157                      # Log bearish hold so dashboard shows current state
 1158                      if self.memory:
 1159                          self.memory.log_decision(
 1160                              decision="hold",
 1161                              reasoning=f"Bearish signal (score={opp_score}/100) but crypto shorts not supported on Alpaca. Monitoring for reversal.",
 1162                              symbol=symbol,
 1163                              confidence=round(max(0.1, (30 - opp_score) / 30), 2),
 1164                          )
 1165                  else:
 1166                      passed_short.append(symbol)
 1167              else:
 1168                  skipped.append(symbol)
 1169                  logger.info(f"SKIPPED {symbol}: neutral signal score {opp_score}")
 1170                  # For crypto: always log HOLD so the dashboard shows current status
 1171                  if is_crypto and self.memory:
 1172                      neutral_conf = round(abs(opp_score - 45) / 45 * 0.4, 2)  # max 0.4 for neutral
 1173                      self.memory.log_decision(
 1174                          decision="hold",
 1175                          reasoning=f"Neutral signal (score={opp_score}/100) — no clear directional bias. Monitoring.",
 1176                          symbol=symbol,
 1177                          confidence=neutral_conf,
 1178                      )
 1179  
 1180          passed = passed_long + passed_short
 1181          if no_short_crypto:
 1182              logger.info(
 1183                  f"📉 Bearish crypto skipped ({len(no_short_crypto)}): {', '.join(no_short_crypto)}"
 1184              )
 1185          if skipped:
 1186              logger.info(
 1187                  f"⚡ Pre-filter: {len(skipped)} neutral score (30≤score≤60) skipped"
 1188              )
 1189          logger.info(
 1190              f"🤖 Calling Claude for {len(passed)}/{len(ranked)} symbols — "
 1191              f"long candidates: {passed_long or 'none'} | "
 1192              f"short candidates (stocks/ETF only): {passed_short or 'none'}"
 1193          )
 1194  
 1195          claude_confidences: dict = {}  # populated during Claude pass, consumed in short pass
 1196  
 1197          for symbol in passed:
 1198              try:
 1199                  data  = symbols_data[symbol]
 1200                  bars  = data["bars"]
 1201                  synth = data.get("synthesis", {})
 1202  
 1203                  # ── Hard gate: only call Claude when synthesis says go ────────
 1204                  if not synth.get("should_call_claude", True):
 1205                      reason = synth.get("decision_reason", "synthesis score below threshold")
 1206                      logger.info(f"⛔ SYNTHESIS SKIP {symbol}: {reason}")
 1207                      if self.memory:
 1208                          self.memory.log_decision(
 1209                              decision="hold",
 1210                              reasoning=(
 1211                                  f"Synthesis engine blocked Claude call — {reason}. "
 1212                                  f"Breakdown: {synth.get('score_breakdown', '')}"
 1213                              ),
 1214                              symbol=symbol,
 1215                              confidence=0.0,
 1216                          )
 1217                      continue
 1218  
 1219                  synth_ctx = synth.get("full_context", "")
 1220                  decision = self.analyze_market(
 1221                      symbol, bars,
 1222                      market_context=f"{market_context}\n\n{synth_ctx}"
 1223                  )
 1224                  if not decision:
 1225                      continue
 1226  
 1227                  current_price = float(bars['close'].iloc[-1])
 1228                  confidence = decision.get("confidence", 0)
 1229                  action = decision.get("decision", "hold")
 1230                  strategy = decision.get("strategy_used", "NONE")
 1231                  urgency = decision.get("urgency", "low")
 1232  
 1233                  logger.info(
 1234                      f"{symbol}: {action.upper()} | {strategy} | "
 1235                      f"conf={confidence:.0%} | urgency={urgency} — {decision.get('reasoning','')}"
 1236                  )
 1237  
 1238                  if self.memory:
 1239                      self.memory.log_decision(
 1240                          decision=action,
 1241                          reasoning=decision.get("reasoning", ""),
 1242                          symbol=symbol,
 1243                          confidence=confidence,
 1244                      )
 1245  
 1246                  # Store for short selling pass
 1247                  claude_confidences[symbol] = confidence
 1248  
 1249                  # Regime sets the base bar; session can only raise it, never lower
 1250                  if session in ("mid_day", "after_hours", "closed"):
 1251                      min_confidence = max(regime_conf_min, 0.85)
 1252                  elif session == "weekend":
 1253                      min_confidence = max(regime_conf_min, 0.70)
 1254                  else:
 1255                      min_confidence = regime_conf_min
 1256  
 1257                  if action == "buy" and confidence >= min_confidence:
 1258                      # Look up daily volume from scanner cache (movers only; None for crypto)
 1259                      cached_movers = self.scanner._movers_cache.get("symbols", [])
 1260                      mover_info    = next((m for m in cached_movers if m["symbol"] == symbol), None)
 1261                      daily_volume  = mover_info["volume"] if mover_info else None
 1262  
 1263                      opp_score = data["opportunity_score"]
 1264                      qty, pct, trail_pct = self.risk.get_position_size_by_score(
 1265                          symbol, current_price, opp_score, volume=daily_volume
 1266                      )
 1267  
 1268                      # ── Correlation conflict check — hard block if ≥80% overlap ──
 1269                      corr_check = self.correlations.check_correlation_conflict(
 1270                          symbol, open_pos_symbols
 1271                      )
 1272                      if corr_check["conflict"] and corr_check.get("score_adjustment", 0) <= -20:
 1273                          logger.info(
 1274                              f"🚫 CORRELATION BLOCK: {symbol} entry skipped — "
 1275                              f"{corr_check['reason']}"
 1276                          )
 1277                          if self.memory:
 1278                              self.memory.log_decision(
 1279                                  decision="hold",
 1280                                  reasoning=f"Correlation conflict blocked entry: {corr_check['reason']}",
 1281                                  symbol=symbol,
 1282                                  confidence=confidence,
 1283                              )
 1284                          continue
 1285  
 1286                      # ── Regime size multiplier ──────────────────────────────────
 1287                      if size_mult != 1.0:
 1288                          orig_qty = qty
 1289                          qty  = max(1, round(qty * size_mult, 8))
 1290                          pct  = pct * size_mult
 1291                          logger.info(
 1292                              f"  ↳ Regime {_regime} size_mult={size_mult}x: "
 1293                              f"qty {orig_qty} → {qty} | position={pct*100:.0f}%"
 1294                          )
 1295  
 1296                      # ── Beta-adjusted size (correlations module) ────────────────
 1297                      beta_pct = self.correlations.get_beta_adjusted_size(
 1298                          symbol, pct * 100, _regime
 1299                      )
 1300                      if abs(beta_pct - pct * 100) > 0.5:
 1301                          ratio    = beta_pct / (pct * 100) if pct > 0 else 1.0
 1302                          orig_qty = qty
 1303                          qty      = max(1, round(qty * ratio, 8))
 1304                          pct      = beta_pct / 100
 1305                          logger.info(
 1306                              f"  ↳ Beta adj: {symbol} → {beta_pct:.0f}% of portfolio "
 1307                              f"| qty {orig_qty} → {qty}"
 1308                          )
 1309  
 1310                      # ── Pre-earnings cap: limit to 10% of portfolio ─────────────
 1311                      ea_buy = earnings_alerts_map.get(symbol)
 1312                      if ea_buy and ea_buy["type"] == "pre_earnings":
 1313                          try:
 1314                              account = self.broker.api.get_account()
 1315                              portfolio_value = float(account.portfolio_value)
 1316                              max_qty = int((0.10 * portfolio_value) / current_price)
 1317                              if qty > max_qty:
 1318                                  logger.info(
 1319                                      f"⚠️ PRE-EARNINGS cap: {symbol} qty {qty}→{max_qty} "
 1320                                      f"(10% limit, reports in {ea_buy['days_away']}d)"
 1321                                  )
 1322                                  qty = max_qty
 1323                                  pct = 0.10
 1324                          except Exception as cap_err:
 1325                              logger.warning(f"Pre-earnings cap error: {cap_err}")
 1326  
 1327                      amount = qty * current_price
 1328                      # Prefer ATR-anchored stop/target from synthesis (geometry layer)
 1329                      geo_sl = synth.get("stop_loss")
 1330                      geo_tp = synth.get("take_profit")
 1331                      sl     = geo_sl if geo_sl else self.risk.calculate_stop_loss(current_price, "buy")
 1332                      if geo_sl:
 1333                          geo_stop_pct = synth.get("stop_pct", 0)
 1334                          if geo_stop_pct and geo_stop_pct / 100 < trail_pct:
 1335                              trail_pct               = geo_stop_pct / 100
 1336                              self._trail_pcts[symbol] = trail_pct
 1337  
 1338                      rr_str = f" | R:R={synth.get('risk_reward', 0):.1f}x" if synth.get("risk_reward") else ""
 1339                      tp_str = f" | target=${geo_tp:.4f}" if geo_tp else ""
 1340                      logger.info(
 1341                          f"TRADE ENTRY: {symbol} buy | score={opp_score} "
 1342                          f"| position={pct*100:.0f}% = ${amount:,.2f} "
 1343                          f"| stop={trail_pct*100:.0f}%{tp_str}{rr_str}"
 1344                      )
 1345  
 1346                      # Store trail_pct so _manage_trailing_stops uses the correct %
 1347                      self._trail_pcts[symbol] = trail_pct
 1348  
 1349                      self.broker.place_order(symbol, qty, "buy", sl, take_profit=geo_tp)
 1350  
 1351                  elif action == "sell" and confidence >= min_confidence:
 1352                      self.broker.close_position(symbol)
 1353  
 1354              except Exception as e:
 1355                  logger.error(f"Error on {symbol}: {e}")
 1356  
 1357          # ── SHORT SELLING PASS ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
 1358          # Separate pass over ALL scanned symbols (incl. pre-filtered ones).
 1359          # Short only stocks/ETFs — Alpaca spot does NOT support crypto shorts.
 1360          # Entry conditions: RSI > 70 AND MACD bearish AND price below SMA20
 1361          #   + if Claude was called for this symbol: confidence < SHORT_ENTRY_CONF_MAX
 1362          try:
 1363              open_positions = {
 1364                  p.symbol.replace("/", ""): p
 1365                  for p in self.broker.get_positions()
 1366              }
 1367          except Exception as e:
 1368              logger.error(f"Short entry: could not fetch positions: {e}")
 1369              open_positions = {}
 1370  
 1371          short_candidates = 0
 1372          for symbol, data in symbols_data.items():
 1373              is_crypto = "/" in symbol
 1374              if is_crypto:
 1375                  continue  # Alpaca spot = no crypto shorts
 1376  
 1377              ind = data["indicators"]
 1378              rsi          = ind.get("rsi", 50)
 1379              macd_bullish = ind.get("macd_bullish", True)
 1380              above_sma20  = ind.get("above_sma20", True)
 1381              current_price = ind.get("current_price", 0)
 1382  
 1383              # Technical gate
 1384              if not (rsi > config.SHORT_ENTRY_RSI_MIN
 1385                      and not macd_bullish
 1386                      and not above_sma20):
 1387                  continue
 1388  
 1389              # Confidence gate: if Claude was called, require conf < threshold
 1390              if symbol in passed:
 1391                  conf = claude_confidences.get(symbol, 1.0)
 1392                  if conf >= config.SHORT_ENTRY_CONF_MAX:
 1393                      logger.debug(f"SHORT skip {symbol}: Claude conf={conf:.0%} >= {config.SHORT_ENTRY_CONF_MAX:.0%}")
 1394                      continue
 1395  
 1396              # No existing position in this symbol
 1397              sym_key = symbol.replace("/", "")
 1398              if sym_key in open_positions:
 1399                  pos_side = getattr(open_positions[sym_key], "side", "long")
 1400                  logger.debug(f"SHORT skip {symbol}: already in {pos_side} position")
 1401                  continue
 1402  
 1403              if current_price <= 0:
 1404                  continue
 1405  
 1406              short_candidates += 1
 1407              qty, short_pct = self.risk.get_short_position_size(symbol, current_price)
 1408              amount = qty * current_price
 1409              sl     = self.risk.calculate_stop_loss(current_price, "sell")
 1410              opp_score_short = symbols_data[symbol]["opportunity_score"]
 1411  
 1412              logger.info(
 1413                  f"TRADE ENTRY: {symbol} sell | score={opp_score_short} "
 1414                  f"| position={short_pct*100:.0f}% = ${amount:,.2f} "
 1415                  f"| stop={SHORT_TRAIL_PCT*100:.0f}%"
 1416              )
 1417              order = self.broker.place_order(symbol, qty, "sell", sl)
 1418              if order and self.memory:
 1419                  try:
 1420                      trade_id = str(uuid.uuid4())
 1421                      alpaca_id = getattr(order, "id", None)
 1422                      self.memory.log_trade_open(
 1423                          trade_id=trade_id,
 1424                          symbol=symbol,
 1425                          side="sell",
 1426                          qty=qty,
 1427                          entry_price=current_price,
 1428                          stop_loss=sl,
 1429                          alpaca_order_id=alpaca_id,
 1430                      )
 1431                  except Exception as me:
 1432                      logger.warning(f"Memory log short entry: {me}")
 1433  
 1434          if short_candidates == 0:
 1435              logger.debug("SHORT PASS: no candidates met entry conditions")
