    1  import sqlite3
    2  import json
    3  import logging
    4  from datetime import datetime, timezone
    5  from typing import Optional
    6  from contextlib import contextmanager
    7  
    8  logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
    9  
   10  SCHEMA = """
   11  CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS trades (
   12      id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
   13      trade_id TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
   14      alpaca_order_id TEXT,
   15      symbol TEXT NOT NULL,
   16      side TEXT NOT NULL,
   17      qty REAL NOT NULL,
   18      entry_price REAL,
   19      exit_price REAL,
   20      stop_loss REAL,
   21      take_profit REAL,
   22      status TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'open',
   23      pnl REAL,
   24      pnl_pct REAL,
   25      entry_at TEXT NOT NULL,
   26      exit_at TEXT,
   27      hold_duration_min REAL,
   28      close_reason TEXT,
   29      market_context TEXT,
   30      created_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime('now'))
   31  );
   32  CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS agent_decisions (
   33      id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
   34      trade_id TEXT,
   35      symbol TEXT,
   36      decision TEXT NOT NULL,
   37      confidence REAL,
   38      reasoning TEXT NOT NULL,
   39      market_data TEXT,
   40      decided_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime('now'))
   41  );
   42  CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS trade_analyses (
   43      id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
   44      trade_id TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
   45      symbol TEXT NOT NULL,
   46      outcome TEXT NOT NULL,
   47      pnl REAL,
   48      analysis TEXT NOT NULL,
   49      lessons TEXT,
   50      mistakes TEXT,
   51      strategy_adj TEXT,
   52      analyzed_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime('now'))
   53  );
   54  CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS agent_memory (
   55      id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
   56      key TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
   57      value TEXT NOT NULL,
   58      category TEXT NOT NULL,
   59      updated_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime('now'))
   60  );
   61  """
   62  
   63  class TradingMemory:
   64      def __init__(self, db_path="trading_memory.db"):
   65          self.db_path = db_path
   66          self._init_db()
   67          logger.info(f"✅ TradingMemory ready: {db_path}")
   68  
   69      def _init_db(self):
   70          with self._conn() as conn:
   71              conn.executescript(SCHEMA)
   72  
   73      @contextmanager
   74      def _conn(self):
   75          conn = sqlite3.connect(self.db_path, timeout=30)
   76          conn.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
   77          conn.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
   78          try:
   79              yield conn
   80              conn.commit()
   81          except Exception as e:
   82              conn.rollback()
   83              raise
   84          finally:
   85              conn.close()
   86  
   87      def log_trade_open(self, trade_id, symbol, side, qty, entry_price,
   88                         stop_loss=None, take_profit=None,
   89                         alpaca_order_id=None, market_context=None):
   90          try:
   91              with self._conn() as conn:
   92                  conn.execute(
   93                      "INSERT INTO trades (trade_id,alpaca_order_id,symbol,side,qty,entry_price,stop_loss,take_profit,status,entry_at,market_context) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,'open',?,?)",
   94                      (trade_id, alpaca_order_id, symbol, side, qty, entry_price,
   95                       stop_loss, take_profit,
   96                       datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
   97                       json.dumps(market_context) if market_context else None)
   98                  )
   99              return True
  100          except Exception as e:
  101              logger.error(f"log_trade_open error: {e}")
  102              return False
  103  
  104      def log_trade_close(self, trade_id, exit_price, close_reason, pnl=None, pnl_pct=None):
  105          try:
  106              with self._conn() as conn:
  107                  row = conn.execute(
  108                      "SELECT entry_at, entry_price, qty, side FROM trades WHERE trade_id=?",
  109                      (trade_id,)
  110                  ).fetchone()
  111                  if not row:
  112                      return False
  113                  exit_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
  114                  entry_at = datetime.fromisoformat(row["entry_at"])
  115                  duration = (exit_at - entry_at).total_seconds() / 60
  116                  if pnl is None:
  117                      m = 1 if row["side"] == "buy" else -1
  118                      pnl = (exit_price - row["entry_price"]) * row["qty"] * m
  119                  if pnl_pct is None and row["entry_price"] > 0:
  120                      pnl_pct = (pnl / (row["entry_price"] * row["qty"])) * 100
  121                  conn.execute(
  122                      "UPDATE trades SET exit_price=?,exit_at=?,hold_duration_min=?,close_reason=?,pnl=?,pnl_pct=?,status='closed' WHERE trade_id=?",
  123                      (exit_price, exit_at.isoformat(), duration, close_reason,
  124                       round(pnl,4), round(pnl_pct,4) if pnl_pct else None, trade_id)
  125                  )
  126              return True
  127          except Exception as e:
  128              logger.error(f"log_trade_close error: {e}")
  129              return False
  130  
  131      def get_open_trades(self):
  132          with self._conn() as conn:
  133              rows = conn.execute("SELECT * FROM trades WHERE status='open' ORDER BY entry_at DESC").fetchall()
  134              return [dict(r) for r in rows]
  135  
  136      def get_recent_trades(self, limit=20, symbol=None):
  137          with self._conn() as conn:
  138              if symbol:
  139                  rows = conn.execute("SELECT * FROM trades WHERE symbol=? ORDER BY entry_at DESC LIMIT ?", (symbol, limit)).fetchall()
  140              else:
  141                  rows = conn.execute("SELECT * FROM trades ORDER BY entry_at DESC LIMIT ?", (limit,)).fetchall()
  142              return [dict(r) for r in rows]
  143  
  144      def get_closed_trades_unanalyzed(self):
  145          with self._conn() as conn:
  146              rows = conn.execute(
  147                  "SELECT t.* FROM trades t LEFT JOIN trade_analyses ta ON t.trade_id=ta.trade_id WHERE t.status='closed' AND ta.trade_id IS NULL ORDER BY t.exit_at DESC"
  148              ).fetchall()
  149              return [dict(r) for r in rows]
  150  
  151      def log_decision(self, decision, reasoning, symbol=None, trade_id=None, confidence=None, market_data=None):
  152          try:
  153              with self._conn() as conn:
  154                  conn.execute(
  155                      "INSERT INTO agent_decisions (trade_id,symbol,decision,confidence,reasoning,market_data) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?)",
  156                      (trade_id, symbol, decision, confidence, reasoning,
  157                       json.dumps(market_data) if market_data else None)
  158                  )
  159              return True
  160          except Exception as e:
  161              logger.error(f"log_decision error: {e}")
  162              return False
  163  
  164      def get_recent_decisions(self, limit=10, symbol=None):
  165          with self._conn() as conn:
  166              if symbol:
  167                  rows = conn.execute("SELECT * FROM agent_decisions WHERE symbol=? ORDER BY decided_at DESC LIMIT ?", (symbol, limit)).fetchall()
  168              else:
  169                  rows = conn.execute("SELECT * FROM agent_decisions ORDER BY decided_at DESC LIMIT ?", (limit,)).fetchall()
  170              return [dict(r) for r in rows]
  171  
  172      def save_trade_analysis(self, trade_id, symbol, outcome, pnl, analysis, lessons=None, mistakes=None, strategy_adj=None):
  173          try:
  174              with self._conn() as conn:
  175                  conn.execute(
  176                      "INSERT OR REPLACE INTO trade_analyses (trade_id,symbol,outcome,pnl,analysis,lessons,mistakes,strategy_adj) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)",
  177                      (trade_id, symbol, outcome, pnl, analysis,
  178                       json.dumps(lessons) if lessons else None,
  179                       json.dumps(mistakes) if mistakes else None,
  180                       strategy_adj)
  181                  )
  182              return True
  183          except Exception as e:
  184              logger.error(f"save_trade_analysis error: {e}")
  185              return False
  186  
  187      def get_analyses(self, limit=10):
  188          with self._conn() as conn:
  189              rows = conn.execute("SELECT * FROM trade_analyses ORDER BY analyzed_at DESC LIMIT ?", (limit,)).fetchall()
  190              return [dict(r) for r in rows]
  191  
  192      def compute_performance_stats(self, symbol=None):
  193          with self._conn() as conn:
  194              q = "SELECT * FROM trades WHERE status='closed'"
  195              params = []
  196              if symbol:
  197                  q += " AND symbol=?"
  198                  params.append(symbol)
  199              rows = conn.execute(q, params).fetchall()
  200              trades = [dict(r) for r in rows]
  201          if not trades:
  202              return {"total_trades": 0}
  203          pnls = [t["pnl"] for t in trades if t["pnl"] is not None]
  204          wins = [p for p in pnls if p > 0]
  205          losses = [p for p in pnls if p < 0]
  206          gross_win = sum(wins) if wins else 0
  207          gross_loss = abs(sum(losses)) if losses else 0
  208          pf = gross_win / gross_loss if gross_loss > 0 else 999
  209          cumulative = peak = max_dd = 0
  210          for p in pnls:
  211              cumulative += p
  212              if cumulative > peak:
  213                  peak = cumulative
  214              dd = peak - cumulative
  215              if dd > max_dd:
  216                  max_dd = dd
  217          by_asset = {}
  218          for t in trades:
  219              s = t["symbol"]
  220              if t["pnl"] is not None:
  221                  by_asset.setdefault(s, []).append(t["pnl"])
  222          asset_pnl = {s: sum(v) for s, v in by_asset.items()}
  223          return {
  224              "total_trades": len(pnls),
  225              "winning_trades": len(wins),
  226              "losing_trades": len(losses),
  227              "win_rate": round(len(wins)/len(pnls)*100, 2) if pnls else 0,
  228              "total_pnl": round(sum(pnls), 2),
  229              "avg_win": round(sum(wins)/len(wins), 2) if wins else 0,
  230              "avg_loss": round(sum(losses)/len(losses), 2) if losses else 0,
  231              "profit_factor": round(pf, 2),
  232              "max_drawdown": round(max_dd, 2),
  233              "best_asset": max(asset_pnl, key=asset_pnl.get) if asset_pnl else None,
  234              "worst_asset": min(asset_pnl, key=asset_pnl.get) if asset_pnl else None,
  235              "asset_pnl": {k: round(v,2) for k,v in asset_pnl.items()},
  236          }
  237  
  238      def set_memory(self, key, value, category="strategy"):
  239          try:
  240              with self._conn() as conn:
  241                  conn.execute(
  242                      "INSERT INTO agent_memory (key,value,category,updated_at) VALUES (?,?,?,?) ON CONFLICT(key) DO UPDATE SET value=excluded.value,category=excluded.category,updated_at=excluded.updated_at",
  243                      (key, json.dumps(value), category, datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat())
  244                  )
  245              return True
  246          except Exception as e:
  247              logger.error(f"set_memory error: {e}")
  248              return False
  249  
  250      def get_memory(self, key, default=None):
  251          with self._conn() as conn:
  252              row = conn.execute("SELECT value FROM agent_memory WHERE key=?", (key,)).fetchone()
  253              if row:
  254                  try:
  255                      return json.loads(row["value"])
  256                  except:
  257                      return row["value"]
  258              return default
  259  
  260      def get_all_memory(self, category=None):
  261          with self._conn() as conn:
  262              if category:
  263                  rows = conn.execute("SELECT key,value,category,updated_at FROM agent_memory WHERE category=?", (category,)).fetchall()
  264              else:
  265                  rows = conn.execute("SELECT key,value,category,updated_at FROM agent_memory").fetchall()
  266              result = {}
  267              for row in rows:
  268                  try:
  269                      result[row["key"]] = {"value": json.loads(row["value"]), "category": row["category"]}
  270                  except:
  271                      result[row["key"]] = {"value": row["value"], "category": row["category"]}
  272              return result
  273  
  274      def get_context_for_agent(self, symbol=None):
  275          stats = self.compute_performance_stats(symbol)
  276          recent = self.get_recent_trades(limit=5, symbol=symbol)
  277          memory = self.get_all_memory()
  278          lines = ["=== AGENT MEMORY ==="]
  279          if stats.get("total_trades", 0) > 0:
  280              lines.append(f"Performance: {stats['total_trades']} trades | Win rate: {stats['win_rate']}% | P&L: ${stats['total_pnl']}")
  281          if recent:
  282              lines.append("Recent trades:")
  283              for t in recent:
  284                  pnl_str = f"${t['pnl']:.2f}" if t.get("pnl") else "open"
  285                  lines.append(f"  {t['symbol']} {t['side']} | {pnl_str}")
  286          strategy = {k: v["value"] for k,v in memory.items() if v.get("category") == "strategy"}
  287          if strategy:
  288              lines.append("Strategy insights:")
  289              for k,v in list(strategy.items())[:3]:
  290                  lines.append(f"  • {k}: {v}")
  291          return "\n".join(lines)

   96  @app.route("/api/regime")
   97  def api_regime():
   98      if not _regime:
   99          return jsonify({"regime": "UNKNOWN", "vix": None, "dxy": None, "score_long_threshold": 60, "score_short_threshold": 30})
  100      try:
  101          import re as _re
  102          params  = _regime.get_params()
  103          context = _regime.build_regime_context()
  104          # Inject VIX into params if present in context string
  105          vix_m = _re.search(r"VIX:\s*([\d.]+)", context)
  106          if vix_m:
  107              params = dict(params)
  108              params["vix"] = float(vix_m.group(1))
  109          return jsonify({
  110              "regime":   params.get("regime", "UNKNOWN"),
  111              "params":   params,
  112              "context":  context,
  113          })
  114      except Exception as e:
  115          return jsonify({"regime": "UNKNOWN", "error": str(e)})
  116  
  117  def _period_start(period: str) -> str | None:
  118      now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
  119      if period == "today":
  120          return now.date().isoformat()
  121      if period == "week":
  122          monday = now.date() - __import__('datetime').timedelta(days=now.weekday())
  123          return monday.isoformat()
  124      if period == "month":
  125          return now.date().replace(day=1).isoformat()
  126      if period == "ytd":
  127          return now.date().replace(month=1, day=1).isoformat()
  128      return None  # all
  129  
  130  @app.route("/api/closed-today")
  131  def api_closed_today():
  132      from flask import request as flask_req
  133      if not _memory:
  134          return jsonify({"closed": [], "date": ""})
  135      try:
  136          period    = flask_req.args.get("period", "today")
  137          since     = _period_start(period)
  138          today     = datetime.now(timezone.utc).date().isoformat()
  139          conn      = sqlite3.connect(_memory.db_path, timeout=10)
  140          c         = conn.cursor()
  141          if since:
  142              c.execute("""
  143                  SELECT symbol,
  144                         SUM(pnl)         AS total_pnl,
  145                         COUNT(*)         AS trade_count,
  146                         SUM(qty)         AS total_qty_sold,
  147                         MAX(exit_at)     AS last_exit_at,
  148                         GROUP_CONCAT(DISTINCT close_reason) AS reasons
  149                  FROM trades
  150                  WHERE status = 'closed' AND exit_at >= ?
  151                  GROUP BY symbol
  152                  ORDER BY total_pnl DESC
  153              """, (since,))
  154          else:
  155              c.execute("""
  156                  SELECT symbol,
  157                         SUM(pnl)         AS total_pnl,
  158                         COUNT(*)         AS trade_count,
  159                         SUM(qty)         AS total_qty_sold,
  160                         MAX(exit_at)     AS last_exit_at,
  161                         GROUP_CONCAT(DISTINCT close_reason) AS reasons
  162                  FROM trades
  163                  WHERE status = 'closed'
  164                  GROUP BY symbol
  165                  ORDER BY total_pnl DESC
  166              """)
  167          rows = c.fetchall()
  168          conn.close()
  169          closed = [
  170              {
  171                  "symbol":      r[0],
  172                  "pnl":         round(r[1], 6) if r[1] is not None else 0,
  173                  "trade_count": r[2],
  174                  "qty_sold":    round(r[3], 8) if r[3] is not None else 0,
  175                  "last_exit":   r[4] or "",
  176                  "reasons":     r[5] or "",
  177              }
  178              for r in rows
  179          ]
  180          return jsonify({"closed": closed, "date": today, "period": period})
  181      except Exception as e:
  182          logger.error(f"api_closed_today error: {e}")
  183          return jsonify({"closed": [], "error": str(e)})
  184  
  185  @app.route("/api/analysis")
  186  def api_analysis():
  187      if not _memory:
  188          return jsonify({})
  189      try:
  190          conn = sqlite3.connect(_memory.db_path, timeout=10)
  191          c    = conn.cursor()
  192  
  193          # ── All closed trades ──────────────────────────────────────────
  194          c.execute("""
  195              SELECT symbol, pnl, pnl_pct, hold_duration_min, close_reason, exit_at
  196              FROM trades WHERE status='closed'
  197              ORDER BY exit_at
  198          """)
  199          trades = c.fetchall()
  200  
  201          # ── Daily P&L (last 30 days) ───────────────────────────────────
  202          c.execute("""
  203              SELECT DATE(exit_at) AS day, SUM(pnl) AS day_pnl, COUNT(*) AS cnt
  204              FROM trades WHERE status='closed'
  205              GROUP BY day ORDER BY day DESC LIMIT 30
  206          """)
  207          daily_rows = c.fetchall()
  208  
  209          # ── P&L by asset ───────────────────────────────────────────────
  210          c.execute("""
  211              SELECT symbol, SUM(pnl) AS total, COUNT(*) AS cnt,
  212                     AVG(pnl) AS avg_pnl, AVG(hold_duration_min) AS avg_hold
  213              FROM trades WHERE status='closed'
  214              GROUP BY symbol ORDER BY total DESC
  215          """)
  216          asset_rows = c.fetchall()
  217  
  218          # ── Close reason breakdown ─────────────────────────────────────
  219          c.execute("""
  220              SELECT close_reason, COUNT(*) AS cnt, SUM(pnl) AS total_pnl
  221              FROM trades WHERE status='closed'
  222              GROUP BY close_reason ORDER BY cnt DESC
  223          """)
  224          reason_rows = c.fetchall()
  225  
  226          conn.close()
  227  
  228          # ── Compute core metrics ───────────────────────────────────────
  229          total  = len(trades)
  230          wins   = [t for t in trades if (t[1] or 0) > 0]
  231          losses = [t for t in trades if (t[1] or 0) < 0]
  232          pnls   = [t[1] or 0 for t in trades]
  233          holds  = [t[3] or 0 for t in trades if t[3]]
  234  
  235          gross_win  = sum(t[1] for t in wins)  if wins   else 0
  236          gross_loss = sum(t[1] for t in losses) if losses else 0
  237          win_rate   = (len(wins) / total * 100) if total else 0
  238          loss_rate  = 100 - win_rate
  239          avg_win    = (gross_win / len(wins))   if wins   else 0
  240          avg_loss   = (gross_loss / len(losses)) if losses else 0
  241          pf         = (gross_win / abs(gross_loss)) if gross_loss else 999
  242          expectancy = (win_rate/100 * avg_win) + (loss_rate/100 * avg_loss)
  243  
  244          best_trade  = max(trades, key=lambda t: t[1] or 0) if trades else None
  245          worst_trade = min(trades, key=lambda t: t[1] or 0) if trades else None
  246          avg_hold    = (sum(holds) / len(holds)) if holds else 0
  247  
  248          # ── Streak calculation ─────────────────────────────────────────
  249          streak, max_win_streak, max_loss_streak = 0, 0, 0
  250          cur_streak_type = None
  251          for t in trades:
  252              is_win = (t[1] or 0) >= 0
  253              if cur_streak_type is None or is_win == cur_streak_type:
  254                  streak += 1
  255                  cur_streak_type = is_win
  256              else:
  257                  if cur_streak_type:
  258                      max_win_streak  = max(max_win_streak, streak)
  259                  else:
  260                      max_loss_streak = max(max_loss_streak, streak)
  261                  streak = 1
  262                  cur_streak_type = is_win
  263          if cur_streak_type is True:
  264              max_win_streak  = max(max_win_streak, streak)
  265          elif cur_streak_type is False:
  266              max_loss_streak = max(max_loss_streak, streak)
  267          current_streak      = {"type": "win" if cur_streak_type else "loss", "count": streak} if trades else None
  268  
  269          # ── Avg trades per active day ──────────────────────────────────
  270          active_days = len(set(t[5][:10] for t in trades if t[5])) if trades else 1
  271          avg_trades_per_day = total / active_days if active_days else 0
  272  
  273          return jsonify({
  274              "total_trades":      total,
  275              "winning_trades":    len(wins),
  276              "losing_trades":     len(losses),
  277              "win_rate":          round(win_rate, 1),
  278              "profit_factor":     round(pf, 2) if pf != 999 else 999,
  279              "expectancy":        round(expectancy, 4),
  280              "gross_win":         round(gross_win, 4),
  281              "gross_loss":        round(gross_loss, 4),
  282              "total_pnl":         round(sum(pnls), 4),
  283              "avg_win":           round(avg_win, 4),
  284              "avg_loss":          round(avg_loss, 4),
  285              "avg_hold_min":      round(avg_hold, 1),
  286              "avg_trades_per_day": round(avg_trades_per_day, 1),
  287              "best_trade":  {"symbol": best_trade[0],  "pnl": round(best_trade[1],4),  "reason": best_trade[4]} if best_trade  else None,
  288              "worst_trade": {"symbol": worst_trade[0], "pnl": round(worst_trade[1],4), "reason": worst_trade[4]} if worst_trade else None,
  289              "current_streak":    current_streak,
  290              "max_win_streak":    max_win_streak,
  291              "max_loss_streak":   max_loss_streak,
  292              "daily_pnl":  [{"date": r[0], "pnl": round(r[1],4), "trades": r[2]} for r in daily_rows],
  293              "by_asset":   [{"symbol": r[0], "pnl": round(r[1],4), "trades": r[2], "avg_pnl": round(r[3],4), "avg_hold_min": round(r[4] or 0,1)} for r in asset_rows],
  294              "by_reason":  [{"reason": r[0], "trades": r[1], "pnl": round(r[2],4)} for r in reason_rows],
  295          })
  296      except Exception as e:
  297          logger.error(f"api_analysis error: {e}")
  298          return jsonify({"error": str(e)})
  299  
  300  @app.route("/api/account")
  301  def api_account():
  302      if not _agent:
  303          return jsonify({"equity": 0, "cash": 0, "buying_power": 0, "portfolio_value": 0})
  304      try:
  305          account = _agent.broker.get_account()
  306          return jsonify({
  307              "equity":          float(account.equity),
  308              "cash":            float(account.cash),
  309              "buying_power":    float(account.buying_power),
  310              "portfolio_value": float(account.portfolio_value),
  311              "last_equity":     float(account.last_equity),
  312          })
  313      except Exception as e:
  314          logger.error(f"api_account error: {e}")
  315          return jsonify({"equity": 0, "cash": 0, "buying_power": 0, "portfolio_value": 0, "error": str(e)})
  316  
  317  @app.route("/api/stops")
  318  def api_stops():
  319      """Return trailing stop prices per symbol from agent's in-memory state."""
  320      if not _agent:
  321          return jsonify({"stops": {}})
  322      try:
  323          stops = {}
  324          high   = getattr(_agent, "_trailing_high", {})
  325          trail  = getattr(_agent, "_score_trail_pct", {})
  326          low    = getattr(_agent, "_trailing_low",  {})
  327          s_trail = getattr(_agent, "_short_score_trail_pct", {})
  328          for sym, h in high.items():
  329              pct = trail.get(sym, 0.05)
  330              stops[sym] = round(h * (1 - pct), 4)
  331          for sym, l in low.items():
  332              pct = s_trail.get(sym, 0.03)
  333              stops[sym] = round(l * (1 + pct), 4)
  334          return jsonify({"stops": stops})
  335      except Exception as e:
  336          return jsonify({"stops": {}, "error": str(e)})
  337  
  338  @app.route("/api/health")
  339  def api_health():
  340      return jsonify({"status":"ok","timestamp":datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()})
  341  
  342  @app.route("/")
  343  def dashboard():
  344      return render_template_string(DASHBOARD_HTML)
  345  
  346  def start_dashboard(memory, analyzer, scanner=None, regime=None, agent=None, port=8080):
  347      init_dashboard(memory, analyzer, scanner=scanner, regime=regime, agent=agent)
  348      def run():
  349          app.run(host="0.0.0.0", port=port, debug=False, use_reloader=False)
  350      thread = threading.Thread(target=run, daemon=True)
  351      thread.start()
  352      logger.info(f"🌐 Dashboard running on port {port}")
  353      return thread
  354

  459  <script>
  460  const REFRESH=15000;
  461  function fmt(v,p='$',d=2){if(v===null||v===undefined||isNaN(v))return'—';return p+parseFloat(v).toFixed(d)}
  462  function fmtPct(v){if(v===null||v===undefined||isNaN(v))return'—';const n=parseFloat(v);return(n>0?'+':'')+n.toFixed(2)+'%'}
  463  function pnlCls(v){if(!v||isNaN(v))return'';return parseFloat(v)>=0?'pos':'neg'}
  464  function fmtDur(m){if(!m)return'—';const n=Math.round(m);return n<60?n+'min':Math.floor(n/60)+'h'+(n%60>0?n%60+'min':'')}
  465  async function fetchJSON(url){try{const r=await fetch(url);return await r.json()}catch(e){return null}}
  466  function updateClock(){document.getElementById('clock').textContent=new Date().toUTCString().split(' ')[4]+' UTC'}
  467  setInterval(updateClock,1000);updateClock();
  468  async function updateStats(){
  469    const s=await fetchJSON('/api/stats');
  470    if(!s||s.total_trades===0)return;
  471    const pnl=s.total_pnl||0;
  472    const el=document.getElementById('kpi-pnl');
  473    el.textContent=(pnl>=0?'+':'')+' $'+Math.abs(pnl).toFixed(2);
  474    el.className='stat-value '+(pnl>=0?'pos':'neg');
  475    document.getElementById('kpi-wr').textContent=(s.win_rate||0).toFixed(1)+'%';
  476    document.getElementById('kpi-trades').textContent=s.total_trades;
  477    const pf=document.getElementById('kpi-pf');
  478    pf.textContent=s.profit_factor>=999?'∞':(s.profit_factor||0).toFixed(2);
  479    pf.className='stat-value '+((s.profit_factor||0)>=1?'pos':'neg');
  480    document.getElementById('kpi-dd').textContent='-$'+(s.max_drawdown||0).toFixed(2);
  481    renderAssetBars(s.asset_pnl||{});
  482  }
  483  async function updateOpenTrades(){
  484    const trades=await fetchJSON('/api/trades/open');
  485    const el=document.getElementById('open-trades-container');
  486    document.getElementById('kpi-open').textContent=trades?trades.length:0;
  487    if(!trades||trades.length===0){el.innerHTML='<div class="empty">Aucune position ouverte</div>';return}
  488    el.innerHTML='<table class="data-table"><thead><tr><th>Symbol</th><th>Dir.</th><th>Entrée</th><th>SL</th><th>TP</th></tr></thead><tbody>'+
  489      trades.map(t=>`<tr><td><strong>${t.symbol}</strong></td><td><span class="tag tag-${t.side}">${t.side.toUpperCase()}</span></td><td>${fmt(t.entry_price)}</td><td style="color:var(--red)">${fmt(t.stop_loss)}</td><td style="color:var(--green)">${fmt(t.take_profit)}</td></tr>`).join('')+
  490      '</tbody></table>';
  491  }
  492  function renderAssetBars(ap){
  493    const c=document.getElementById('asset-bars');
  494    const e=Object.entries(ap);
  495    if(!e.length){c.innerHTML='<div class="empty">Pas de données</div>';return}
  496    const max=Math.max(...e.map(([,v])=>Math.abs(v)),1);
  497    c.innerHTML=e.sort(([,a],[,b])=>b-a).map(([s,p])=>{
  498      const pct=Math.abs(p)/max*100;const cls=p>=0?'pos':'neg';
  499      return`<div class="asset-row"><div class="asset-name">${s}</div><div class="bar-wrap"><div class="bar-fill ${cls}" style="width:${pct}%"></div></div><div class="asset-pnl ${cls}">${p>=0?'+':''} $${Math.abs(p).toFixed(2)}</div></div>`;
  500    }).join('');
  501  }
  502  async function updateTradesHistory(){
  503    const trades=await fetchJSON('/api/trades/recent');
  504    const body=document.getElementById('trades-body');
  505    if(!trades||!trades.length){body.innerHTML='<tr><td colspan="10" class="empty">Aucun trade</td></tr>';return}
  506    body.innerHTML=trades.map(t=>{
  507      const pnl=t.pnl;const cls=pnl===null?'':(pnl>=0?'pos':'neg');const isOpen=t.status==='open';
  508      return`<tr><td><strong>${t.symbol}</strong></td><td><span class="tag tag-${t.side}">${t.side.toUpperCase()}</span></td><td>${fmt(t.entry_price)}</td><td>${isOpen?'<span class="tag tag-open">OUVERT</span>':fmt(t.exit_price)}</td><td>${t.qty}</td><td class="${cls}">${pnl!==null?(pnl>=0?'+':'')+'$'+Math.abs(pnl).toFixed(2):'—'}</td><td class="${cls}">${t.pnl_pct!==null?fmtPct(t.pnl_pct):'—'}</td><td>${fmtDur(t.hold_duration_min)}</td><td style="color:var(--muted)">${t.close_reason||'—'}</td><td><span class="tag ${isOpen?'tag-open':(pnl>=0?'tag-buy':'tag-sell')}">${t.status}</span></td></tr>`;
  509    }).join('');
  510  }
  511  async function updateDecisions(){
  512    const d=await fetchJSON('/api/decisions/recent');
  513    const c=document.getElementById('decisions-container');
  514    if(!d||!d.length){c.innerHTML='<div class="empty">Aucune décision</div>';return}
  515    c.innerHTML=d.map(x=>`<div class="decision-item"><div class="decision-header"><span class="tag tag-${x.decision==='buy'?'buy':x.decision==='sell'?'sell':'open'}">${x.decision.toUpperCase()}</span> <strong>${x.symbol||''}</strong><span class="decision-time">${new Date(x.decided_at).toLocaleTimeString('fr-FR')}</span></div><div class="decision-reasoning" onclick="this.classList.toggle('expanded')">${x.reasoning||'—'}</div></div>`).join('');
  516  }
  517  async function updateAnalyses(){
  518    const a=await fetchJSON('/api/analyses/recent');
  519    const c=document.getElementById('analyses-container');
  520    if(!a||!a.length){c.innerHTML='<div class="empty">Aucune analyse</div>';return}
  521    c.innerHTML=a.map(x=>{
  522      const lessons=Array.isArray(x.lessons)?x.lessons:[];
  523      const col=x.outcome==='win'?'var(--green)':x.outcome==='loss'?'var(--red)':'var(--blue)';
  524      return`<div class="analysis-item"><div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:8px"><strong>${x.symbol}</strong><span style="color:${col};font-weight:700">${x.outcome.toUpperCase()} ${x.pnl?(x.pnl>=0?'+':'')+'$'+Math.abs(x.pnl).toFixed(2):''}</span></div><div class="analysis-text">${x.analysis||'—'}</div>${lessons.map(l=>`<div class="lesson">${l}</div>`).join('')}</div>`;
  525    }).join('');
  526  }
  527  async function refreshAll(){
  528    await Promise.all([updateStats(),updateOpenTrades(),updateTradesHistory(),updateDecisions(),updateAnalyses()]);
  529    const bar=document.getElementById('refresh-progress');
  530    bar.style.transition='none';bar.style.width='0%';
  531    requestAnimationFrame(()=>{bar.style.transition=`width ${REFRESH}ms linear`;bar.style.width='100%'});
  532  }
  533  refreshAll();
  534  setInterval(refreshAll,REFRESH);
  535  </script>
  536  </body>
  537  </html>"""

    1  import os
    2  
    3  # Anthropic
    4  ANTHROPIC_API_KEY = os.getenv("ANTHROPIC_API_KEY", "")
    5  
    6  # Alpaca
    7  ALPACA_API_KEY = os.getenv("ALPACA_API_KEY", "")
    8  ALPACA_SECRET_KEY = os.getenv("ALPACA_SECRET_KEY", "")
    9  ALPACA_BASE_URL = "https://paper-api.alpaca.markets"
   10  
   11  # Trading rules
   12  MAX_LEVERAGE = 3
   13  MAX_POSITION_PCT = 0.30
   14  GLOBAL_STOP_LOSS_PCT = 0.20
   15  TRADE_STOP_LOSS_PCT = 0.05
   16  MAX_POSITIONS = 5
   17  
   18  # Trailing stop distances — LONG positions (fraction below highest price)
   19  TRAILING_STOP_CRYPTO = 0.03   # 3% for crypto longs
   20  TRAILING_STOP_STOCK  = 0.05   # 5% for stocks/ETFs longs
   21  
   22  # Trailing stop distances — SHORT positions (fraction above lowest price)
   23  TRAILING_STOP_SHORT_CRYPTO = 0.03  # 3% for crypto shorts (paper only)
   24  TRAILING_STOP_SHORT_STOCK  = 0.06  # 6% for stocks/ETF shorts
   25  
   26  # Short selling rules
   27  MAX_SHORT_SIZE_PCT   = 0.15   # Max 15% of portfolio per short position
   28  SHORT_ENTRY_RSI_MIN  = 70     # RSI must be above this to short
   29  SHORT_ENTRY_CONF_MAX = 0.30   # Claude confidence must be below this
   30  
   31  # Partial profit taking
   32  PARTIAL_PROFIT_PCT   = 0.03   # Take partial profits at +3% unrealised gain
   33  PARTIAL_PROFIT_RATIO = 0.50   # Sell / cover this fraction of the position (50%)
   34  
   35  # Universe
   36  CRYPTO_SYMBOLS   = ["BTC/USD", "ETH/USD", "SOL/USD", "AVAX/USD", "DOGE/USD", "XRP/USD", "LINK/USD", "SHIB/USD", "MATIC/USD"]
   37  STOCK_SYMBOLS    = ["AAPL", "NVDA", "TSLA", "META", "GOOGL", "MSFT", "AMD"]
   38  ETF_SYMBOLS      = ["QQQ", "SPY", "ARKK"]
   39  # Fixed blue-chip list always evaluated every cycle regardless of top movers
   40  BLUECHIP_SYMBOLS = ["AAPL", "NVDA", "TSLA", "META", "GOOGL", "MSFT", "AMD", "QQQ", "SPY"]
   41  ALL_SYMBOLS      = CRYPTO_SYMBOLS + STOCK_SYMBOLS + ETF_SYMBOLS
   42  
   43  # Loop speeds
   44  LOOP_INTERVAL_SECONDS      = 300   # Slow loop: full synthesis + movers refresh
   45  FAST_LOOP_INTERVAL_SECONDS = 30    # Fast loop: position stops + score triggers
   46  INITIAL_CAPITAL = 1000.0

FILE: trading-agent/broker.py  (79 lines)

    1  import logging
    2  import alpaca_trade_api as tradeapi
    3  import config
    4  
    5  logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
    6  
    7  class AlpacaBroker:
    8      def __init__(self):
    9          self.api = tradeapi.REST(
   10              config.ALPACA_API_KEY,
   11              config.ALPACA_SECRET_KEY,
   12              config.ALPACA_BASE_URL
   13          )
   14          logger.info("✅ Alpaca broker connected")
   15  
   16      def get_account(self):
   17          try:
   18              return self.api.get_account()
   19          except Exception as e:
   20              logger.error(f"get_account error: {e}")
   21              return None
   22  
   23      def get_portfolio_value(self):
   24          account = self.get_account()
   25          if account:
   26              return float(account.portfolio_value)
   27          return config.INITIAL_CAPITAL
   28  
   29      def get_positions(self):
   30          try:
   31              return self.api.list_positions()
   32          except Exception as e:
   33              logger.error(f"get_positions error: {e}")
   34              return []
   35  
   36      def get_bars(self, symbol, timeframe="1Min", limit=50):
   37          try:
   38              is_crypto = "/" in symbol
   39              if is_crypto:
   40                  bars = self.api.get_crypto_bars(symbol, timeframe, limit=limit).df
   41              else:
   42                  bars = self.api.get_bars(symbol, timeframe, limit=limit).df
   43              return bars
   44          except Exception as e:
   45              logger.error(f"get_bars error for {symbol}: {e}")
   46              return None
   47  
   48      def place_order(self, symbol, qty, side, stop_loss=None, take_profit=None):
   49          try:
   50              order = self.api.submit_order(
   51                  symbol=symbol,
   52                  qty=qty,
   53                  side=side,
   54                  type="market",
   55                  time_in_force="gtc"
   56              )
   57              logger.info(f"✅ Order placed: {side} {qty} {symbol}")
   58              return order
   59          except Exception as e:
   60              logger.error(f"place_order error: {e}")
   61              return None
   62  
   63      def close_position(self, symbol):
   64          try:
   65              self.api.close_position(symbol)
   66              logger.info(f"✅ Position closed: {symbol}")
   67              return True
   68          except Exception as e:
   69              logger.error(f"close_position error: {e}")
   70              return False
   71  
   72      def close_all_positions(self):
   73          try:
   74              self.api.close_all_positions()
   75              logger.info("✅ All positions closed")
   76              return True
   77          except Exception as e:
   78              logger.error(f"close_all_positions error: {e}")
   79              return False


================================================================================
FILE: trading-agent/risk.py  (97 lines)
================================================================================

    1  import logging
    2  import config
    3  
    4  logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
    5  
    6  # Score tiers: (min_score_inclusive, position_pct, trailing_stop_pct)
    7  # Evaluated top-down; first match wins.
    8  SCORE_TIERS = [
    9      (90, 0.40, 0.02),
   10      (80, 0.30, 0.03),
   11      (70, 0.20, 0.04),
   12      (60, 0.15, 0.05),
   13  ]
   14  
   15  MAX_POSITION_PCT    = 0.40   # absolute hard cap — no single long > 40%
   16  SHORT_POSITION_PCT  = 0.15   # all short entries fixed at 15%
   17  LOW_VOLUME_CAP_PCT  = 0.10   # daily volume < LOW_VOLUME_THRESHOLD → cap at 10%
   18  LOW_VOLUME_THRESHOLD = 100_000
   19  
   20  
   21  class RiskManager:
   22      def __init__(self, broker):
   23          self.broker = broker
   24  
   25      def get_position_size_by_score(self, symbol, price, opp_score, volume=None):
   26          """
   27          Returns (qty, pct, trail_pct) based on opportunity score tier.
   28  
   29          Tier mapping:
   30            score 90-100 → 40% position, 2% trailing stop
   31            score 80-89  → 30% position, 3% trailing stop
   32            score 70-79  → 20% position, 4% trailing stop
   33            score 60-69  → 15% position, 5% trailing stop
   34  
   35          Low-volume override: if daily volume < 100,000, cap at 10% regardless.
   36          Hard cap: never exceed 40%.
   37          """
   38          portfolio = self.broker.get_portfolio_value()
   39  
   40          # Default to lowest tier (60-69)
   41          pct, trail_pct = 0.15, 0.05
   42          for min_score, tier_pct, tier_trail in SCORE_TIERS:
   43              if opp_score >= min_score:
   44                  pct, trail_pct = tier_pct, tier_trail
   45                  break
   46  
   47          # Low-volume override
   48          is_low_volume = volume is not None and volume < LOW_VOLUME_THRESHOLD
   49          if is_low_volume:
   50              original_pct = pct
   51              pct = min(pct, LOW_VOLUME_CAP_PCT)
   52              logger.info(
   53                  f"⚠️ {symbol} low volume ({volume:,}) — position capped at "
   54                  f"{pct*100:.0f}% (was {original_pct*100:.0f}% for score {opp_score})"
   55              )
   56  
   57          # Hard cap
   58          pct = min(pct, MAX_POSITION_PCT)
   59  
   60          amount = portfolio * pct
   61          qty = amount / price
   62          return round(qty, 4), pct, trail_pct
   63  
   64      def get_short_position_size(self, symbol, price):
   65          """All short positions are fixed at 15% of portfolio."""
   66          portfolio = self.broker.get_portfolio_value()
   67          amount = portfolio * SHORT_POSITION_PCT
   68          qty = amount / price
   69          return round(qty, 4), SHORT_POSITION_PCT
   70  
   71      def check_global_stop_loss(self):
   72          portfolio = self.broker.get_portfolio_value()
   73          loss_pct = (config.INITIAL_CAPITAL - portfolio) / config.INITIAL_CAPITAL
   74          if loss_pct >= config.GLOBAL_STOP_LOSS_PCT:
   75              logger.warning(f"🔴 GLOBAL STOP LOSS triggered: -{loss_pct*100:.1f}%")
   76              return True
   77          return False
   78  
   79      def check_max_positions(self):
   80          positions = self.broker.get_positions()
   81          if len(positions) >= config.MAX_POSITIONS:
   82              logger.warning(f"⚠️ Max positions reached: {len(positions)}")
   83              return False
   84          return True
   85  
   86      def calculate_stop_loss(self, entry_price, side):
   87          if side == "buy":
   88              return round(entry_price * (1 - config.TRADE_STOP_LOSS_PCT), 4)
   89          else:
   90              return round(entry_price * (1 + config.TRADE_STOP_LOSS_PCT), 4)
   91  
   92      def can_trade(self):
   93          if self.check_global_stop_loss():
   94              return False
   95          if not self.check_max_positions():
   96              return False
   97          return True

FILE: trading-agent/strategy.py  (479 lines)

    1  """
    2  strategy.py — Stratégies de trading avancées
    3  Gapper scanner, momentum, breakout, mean reversion, crypto 24/7
    4  """
    5  import logging
    6  from datetime import datetime, timezone, time
    7  import pytz
    8  import numpy as np
    9  
   10  logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
   11  
   12  ET = pytz.timezone("America/New_York")
   13  
   14  
   15  # ─── HORAIRES DE MARCHÉ ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   16  
   17  def get_market_session() -> str:
   18      """
   19      Retourne la session de marché actuelle.
   20      pre_market / open / mid_day / power_hour / closed
   21      """
   22      now_et = datetime.now(ET)
   23      t = now_et.time()
   24      weekday = now_et.weekday()
   25  
   26      if weekday >= 5:
   27          return "weekend"
   28  
   29      if time(4, 0) <= t < time(9, 30):
   30          return "pre_market"
   31      elif time(9, 30) <= t < time(11, 0):
   32          return "open"        # ⭐ Meilleure fenêtre — gappers + momentum
   33      elif time(11, 0) <= t < time(15, 0):
   34          return "mid_day"     # Volume faible — éviter
   35      elif time(15, 0) <= t < time(16, 0):
   36          return "power_hour"  # 2ème meilleure fenêtre
   37      elif time(16, 0) <= t < time(20, 0):
   38          return "after_hours"
   39      else:
   40          return "closed"
   41  
   42  
   43  def is_good_stock_window() -> bool:
   44      """True si on est dans une bonne fenêtre pour trader les stocks."""
   45      session = get_market_session()
   46      return session in ["open", "power_hour"]
   47  
   48  
   49  def is_crypto_good_hours() -> bool:
   50      """
   51      Crypto trade 24/7 mais évite 2h-6h UTC (volume mort).
   52      """
   53      hour_utc = datetime.now(timezone.utc).hour
   54      return not (2 <= hour_utc < 6)
   55  
   56  
   57  def get_session_context() -> dict:
   58      """Retourne le contexte de session pour le prompt Claude."""
   59      session = get_market_session()
   60      now_et = datetime.now(ET)
   61  
   62      context = {
   63          "session": session,
   64          "time_et": now_et.strftime("%H:%M ET"),
   65          "day": now_et.strftime("%A"),
   66          "good_for_stocks": is_good_stock_window(),
   67          "good_for_crypto": is_crypto_good_hours(),
   68      }
   69  
   70      context["instructions"] = {
   71          "pre_market": "Pre-market: observe gappers, prepare watchlist, no entry yet.",
   72          "open": "PRIME TIME 9:30-11h: Focus on gappers +20%. Momentum and breakout entries. Be aggressive.",
   73          "mid_day": "Mid-day: low volume, choppy. Reduce position sizes. Prefer crypto.",
   74          "power_hour": "Power hour 15-16h: good volatility returns. Look for end-of-day momentum.",
   75          "after_hours": "After-hours: crypto only. Stocks illiquid.",
   76          "closed": "Market closed: crypto only.",
   77          "weekend": "Weekend: crypto only, markets closed.",
   78      }.get(session, "")
   79  
   80      return context
   81  
   82  
   83  # ─── INDICATEURS TECHNIQUES ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
   84  
   85  def compute_indicators(prices: list, volumes: list) -> dict:
   86      """
   87      Calcule tous les indicateurs techniques nécessaires.
   88      Retourne un dict complet pour le prompt Claude.
   89      """
   90      if len(prices) < 20:
   91          return {"error": "Not enough data"}
   92  
   93      p = np.array(prices, dtype=float)
   94      v = np.array(volumes, dtype=float)
   95  
   96      # ── Prix ──
   97      current = float(p[-1])
   98      prev_close = float(p[-2])
   99      change_pct = ((current - prev_close) / prev_close) * 100
  100  
  101      # ── Moyennes mobiles ──
  102      sma20 = float(np.mean(p[-20:]))
  103      sma9  = float(np.mean(p[-9:])) if len(p) >= 9 else sma20
  104      ema12 = _ema(p, 12)
  105      ema26 = _ema(p, 26)
  106  
  107      # ── MACD ──
  108      macd = ema12 - ema26
  109      # Signal = EMA9 du MACD (approximation)
  110      macd_signal = macd * 0.9  # simplification
  111      macd_hist = macd - macd_signal
  112  
  113      # ── RSI ──
  114      rsi = _rsi(p, 14)
  115  
  116      # ── Bollinger Bands ──
  117      bb_mid  = sma20
  118      bb_std  = float(np.std(p[-20:]))
  119      bb_up   = bb_mid + 2 * bb_std
  120      bb_low  = bb_mid - 2 * bb_std
  121      bb_pct  = (current - bb_low) / (bb_up - bb_low) * 100 if (bb_up - bb_low) > 0 else 50
  122  
  123      # ── Volume ──
  124      avg_vol    = float(np.mean(v[-20:]))
  125      curr_vol   = float(v[-1])
  126      vol_ratio  = curr_vol / avg_vol if avg_vol > 0 else 1
  127  
  128      # ── Momentum ──
  129      momentum_5  = ((current - p[-5])  / p[-5])  * 100 if len(p) >= 5  else 0
  130      momentum_10 = ((current - p[-10]) / p[-10]) * 100 if len(p) >= 10 else 0
  131  
  132      # ── Support / Résistance ──
  133      high_20 = float(np.max(p[-20:]))
  134      low_20  = float(np.min(p[-20:]))
  135      near_resistance = current >= high_20 * 0.98
  136      near_support    = current <= low_20  * 1.02
  137  
  138      # ── ATR (Average True Range) — volatilité ──
  139      atr = _atr(p, 14)
  140      atr_pct = (atr / current) * 100
  141  
  142      return {
  143          "current_price":    round(current, 4),
  144          "change_pct":       round(change_pct, 2),
  145          "sma9":             round(sma9, 4),
  146          "sma20":            round(sma20, 4),
  147          "above_sma20":      current > sma20,
  148          "macd":             round(float(macd), 4),
  149          "macd_signal":      round(float(macd_signal), 4),
  150          "macd_bullish":     macd > macd_signal,
  151          "rsi":              round(rsi, 1),
  152          "rsi_oversold":     rsi < 30,
  153          "rsi_overbought":   rsi > 70,
  154          "bb_pct":           round(bb_pct, 1),
  155          "bb_squeeze":       bb_std < (sma20 * 0.01),
  156          "volume_ratio":     round(vol_ratio, 2),
  157          "high_volume":      vol_ratio > 2.0,
  158          "momentum_5":       round(float(momentum_5), 2),
  159          "momentum_10":      round(float(momentum_10), 2),
  160          "near_resistance":  near_resistance,
  161          "near_support":     near_support,
  162          "high_20":          round(high_20, 4),
  163          "low_20":           round(low_20, 4),
  164          "atr_pct":          round(atr_pct, 2),
  165          "high_volatility":  atr_pct > 2.0,
  166      }
  167  
  168  
  169  def _ema(prices: np.ndarray, period: int) -> float:
  170      """Calcule l'EMA d'une série de prix."""
  171      if len(prices) < period:
  172          return float(np.mean(prices))
  173      k = 2 / (period + 1)
  174      ema = float(np.mean(prices[:period]))
  175      for price in prices[period:]:
  176          ema = float(price) * k + ema * (1 - k)
  177      return ema
  178  
  179  
  180  def _rsi(prices: np.ndarray, period: int = 14) -> float:
  181      """Calcule le RSI."""
  182      if len(prices) < period + 1:
  183          return 50.0
  184      deltas = np.diff(prices)
  185      gains  = np.where(deltas > 0, deltas, 0)
  186      losses = np.where(deltas < 0, -deltas, 0)
  187      avg_gain = np.mean(gains[-period:])
  188      avg_loss = np.mean(losses[-period:])
  189      if avg_loss == 0:
  190          return 100.0
  191      rs = avg_gain / avg_loss
  192      return 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))
  193  
  194  
  195  def _atr(prices: np.ndarray, period: int = 14) -> float:
  196      """Calcule l'ATR (Average True Range)."""
  197      if len(prices) < 2:
  198          return 0.0
  199      trs = [abs(prices[i] - prices[i-1]) for i in range(1, len(prices))]
  200      return float(np.mean(trs[-period:]))
  201  
  202  
  203  # ─── DÉTECTION DE PATTERNS ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  204  
  205  def detect_patterns(indicators: dict, session: str) -> dict:
  206      """
  207      Détecte les patterns de trading et retourne les opportunités.
  208      """
  209      patterns = []
  210      score = 0  # Score d'opportunité global
  211  
  212      rsi       = indicators.get("rsi", 50)
  213      macd_bull = indicators.get("macd_bullish", False)
  214      above_sma = indicators.get("above_sma20", False)
  215      vol_ratio = indicators.get("volume_ratio", 1)
  216      bb_pct    = indicators.get("bb_pct", 50)
  217      mom5      = indicators.get("momentum_5", 0)
  218      near_res  = indicators.get("near_resistance", False)
  219      near_sup  = indicators.get("near_support", False)
  220      change    = indicators.get("change_pct", 0)
  221      high_vol  = indicators.get("high_volatility", False)
  222  
  223      # ── GAPPER (stock en forte hausse à l'ouverture) ──
  224      if change > 10 and vol_ratio > 3 and session == "open":
  225          patterns.append("GAPPER")
  226          score += 40
  227  
  228      # ── MOMENTUM ──
  229      if mom5 > 2 and macd_bull and above_sma and vol_ratio > 1.5:
  230          patterns.append("MOMENTUM_BULL")
  231          score += 25
  232      elif mom5 < -2 and not macd_bull and not above_sma and vol_ratio > 1.5:
  233          patterns.append("MOMENTUM_BEAR")
  234          score += 20
  235  
  236      # ── BREAKOUT ──
  237      if near_res and vol_ratio > 2 and macd_bull:
  238          patterns.append("BREAKOUT")
  239          score += 30
  240      elif near_sup and vol_ratio > 2 and not macd_bull:
  241          patterns.append("BREAKDOWN")
  242          score += 20
  243  
  244      # ── MEAN REVERSION ──
  245      if rsi < 25 and near_sup:
  246          patterns.append("OVERSOLD_REVERSAL")
  247          score += 20
  248      elif rsi > 75 and near_res:
  249          patterns.append("OVERBOUGHT_REVERSAL")
  250          score += 15
  251  
  252      # ── SCALP (volume élevé + volatilité) ──
  253      if vol_ratio > 3 and high_vol:
  254          patterns.append("SCALP_OPPORTUNITY")
  255          score += 10
  256  
  257      # ── CONSOLIDATION (éviter) ──
  258      if vol_ratio < 0.5 and abs(mom5) < 0.5:
  259          patterns.append("CONSOLIDATING")
  260          score -= 20
  261  
  262      return {
  263          "patterns":   patterns,
  264          "score":      max(0, score),
  265          "is_opportunity": score >= 25,
  266          "best_pattern":   patterns[0] if patterns else "NONE",
  267          "suggested_action": _suggest_action(patterns, score),
  268      }
  269  
  270  
  271  def compute_opportunity_score(indicators: dict, patterns: dict) -> int:
  272      """
  273      Score DIRECTIONNEL 0-100 :
  274        > 60  → signal haussier clair    → Claude appelé (candidat long)
  275        < 30  → signal baissier clair    → Claude appelé (candidat short)
  276        30-60 → ambigu / neutre          → Claude skippé (pas de coût API)
  277  
  278      Part d'un score neutre de 50, puis ajoute/retire des points selon la
  279      direction des indicateurs techniques. Le volume amplifie la direction.
  280      """
  281      rsi          = indicators.get("rsi", 50)
  282      macd_bullish = indicators.get("macd_bullish", True)
  283      above_sma20  = indicators.get("above_sma20", True)
  284      momentum_5   = indicators.get("momentum_5", 0.0)
  285      vol_ratio    = indicators.get("volume_ratio", 1.0)
  286      bb_pct       = indicators.get("bb_pct", 50.0)
  287      near_sup     = indicators.get("near_support", False)
  288      near_res     = indicators.get("near_resistance", False)
  289      pattern_act  = patterns.get("suggested_action", "hold")
  290      pattern_sc   = patterns.get("score", 0)
  291  
  292      score = 50  # point de départ neutre
  293  
  294      # ── RSI : oversold = haussier, overbought = baissier (±18 pts) ────────
  295      if rsi < 25:
  296          score += 18
  297      elif rsi < 30:
  298          score += 12
  299      elif rsi < 40:
  300          score += 6
  301      elif rsi > 75:
  302          score -= 18
  303      elif rsi > 70:
  304          score -= 12
  305      elif rsi > 60:
  306          score -= 6
  307  
  308      # ── MACD : bullish = haussier, bearish = baissier (±8 pts) ───────────
  309      score += 8 if macd_bullish else -8
  310  
  311      # ── SMA20 : au-dessus = haussier, en-dessous = baissier (±6 pts) ─────
  312      score += 6 if above_sma20 else -6
  313  
  314      # ── Momentum 5 bars : positif = haussier (max ±10 pts) ───────────────
  315      mom_pts = max(-10, min(10, int(momentum_5 * 3)))
  316      score += mom_pts
  317  
  318      # ── Volume : amplifie la direction courante (max ±8 pts) ─────────────
  319      if vol_ratio >= 2.0:
  320          vol_amp = 8
  321      elif vol_ratio >= 1.5:
  322          vol_amp = 4
  323      else:
  324          vol_amp = 0
  325      if score > 50:
  326          score += vol_amp
  327      elif score < 50:
  328          score -= vol_amp
  329  
  330      # ── Bollinger %B : extrêmes confirment la direction (±8 pts) ─────────
  331      if bb_pct < 15:
  332          score += 8
  333      elif bb_pct < 25:
  334          score += 5
  335      elif bb_pct > 85:
  336          score -= 8
  337      elif bb_pct > 75:
  338          score -= 5
  339  
  340      # ── Support / Résistance : contexte directionnel (±3 pts) ────────────
  341      if near_sup:
  342          score += 3
  343      if near_res:
  344          score -= 3
  345  
  346      # ── Pattern détecté (±8 pts) ─────────────────────────────────────────
  347      if pattern_act == "buy" and pattern_sc > 0:
  348          score += min(8, pattern_sc // 5)
  349      elif pattern_act == "sell" and pattern_sc > 0:
  350          score -= min(8, pattern_sc // 5)
  351  
  352      return max(0, min(100, score))
  353  
  354  
  355  def _suggest_action(patterns: list, score: int) -> str:
  356      """Suggère une action basée sur les patterns détectés."""
  357      if not patterns or score < 25:
  358          return "hold"
  359      buy_patterns  = {"GAPPER", "MOMENTUM_BULL", "BREAKOUT", "OVERSOLD_REVERSAL", "SCALP_OPPORTUNITY"}
  360      sell_patterns = {"MOMENTUM_BEAR", "BREAKDOWN", "OVERBOUGHT_REVERSAL"}
  361      buy_count  = sum(1 for p in patterns if p in buy_patterns)
  362      sell_count = sum(1 for p in patterns if p in sell_patterns)
  363      if buy_count > sell_count:
  364          return "buy"
  365      elif sell_count > buy_count:
  366          return "sell"
  367      return "hold"
  368  
  369  
  370  # ─── PROMPT ENRICHI POUR CLAUDE ───────────────────────────────────────────────
  371  
  372  def build_strategy_prompt(
  373      symbol: str,
  374      indicators: dict,
  375      patterns: dict,
  376      session_ctx: dict,
  377      memory_context: str = "",
  378      market_context: str = "",
  379  ) -> str:
  380      """
  381      Construit un prompt complet pour Claude avec tout le contexte stratégique.
  382      C'est ce prompt qui fait la vraie différence vs un agent basique.
  383      """
  384      is_crypto = "/" in symbol
  385      asset_type = "CRYPTO (24/7)" if is_crypto else "STOCK (NYSE/Nasdaq)"
  386  
  387      return f"""You are an expert day trader with 10 years experience. Make a precise trading decision.
  388  
  389  ## Asset
  390  - Symbol: {symbol} ({asset_type})
  391  - Session: {session_ctx['session']} ({session_ctx['time_et']})
  392  - Session guidance: {session_ctx['instructions']}
  393  
  394  ## Technical Indicators
  395  - Price: ${indicators.get('current_price')} ({indicators.get('change_pct'):+.2f}% change)
  396  - RSI: {indicators.get('rsi')} {'🔴 OVERBOUGHT' if indicators.get('rsi_overbought') else '🟢 OVERSOLD' if indicators.get('rsi_oversold') else ''}
  397  - MACD: {'🟢 BULLISH' if indicators.get('macd_bullish') else '🔴 BEARISH'}
  398  - Above SMA20: {indicators.get('above_sma20')}
  399  - Volume ratio vs average: {indicators.get('volume_ratio')}x {'⚡ HIGH VOLUME' if indicators.get('high_volume') else ''}
  400  - Momentum 5 bars: {indicators.get('momentum_5'):+.2f}%
  401  - Bollinger %B: {indicators.get('bb_pct'):.0f}% {'(near top)' if indicators.get('bb_pct',50)>80 else '(near bottom)' if indicators.get('bb_pct',50)<20 else ''}
  402  - Volatility (ATR%): {indicators.get('atr_pct'):.2f}% {'⚡ HIGH' if indicators.get('high_volatility') else ''}
  403  - Near resistance: {indicators.get('near_resistance')} | Near support: {indicators.get('near_support')}
  404  
  405  ## Detected Patterns
  406  - Patterns: {', '.join(patterns.get('patterns', ['NONE']))}
  407  - Opportunity score: {patterns.get('score')}/100
  408  - Suggested action: {patterns.get('suggested_action').upper()}
  409  
  410  ## Strategy Rules by Session
  411  {'- PRIME TIME: Prioritize GAPPERS (+20% at open with high volume). Enter momentum early, exit before 11h.' if session_ctx['session'] == 'open' else ''}
  412  {'- MID-DAY: Low conviction trades only. Tight stops. Prefer crypto.' if session_ctx['session'] == 'mid_day' else ''}
  413  {'- POWER HOUR: End-of-day momentum. Watch for reversals.' if session_ctx['session'] == 'power_hour' else ''}
  414  {'- CRYPTO: Mean reversion on dips. Momentum on breakouts. No PDT rule.' if is_crypto else ''}
  415  
  416  ## Multi-Strategy Framework
  417  - MOMENTUM: Enter if price + volume confirm trend. RSI 40-70 range ideal.
  418  - BREAKOUT: Enter on high-volume break of 20-bar high. Volume must be 2x+ average.
  419  - MEAN REVERSION: Enter on RSI<30 near support. Quick 2-5% target.
  420  - GAPPER: Stock up 20%+ at open with 3x+ volume = highest priority opportunity.
  421  - SCALP: Only if volume ratio >3x AND high volatility. Tight 1-2% target.
  422  
  423  ## Risk Rules (NON-NEGOTIABLE)
  424  - Max position: 30% of capital
  425  - Stop loss: -5% per trade
  426  - Take profit: +10% (or +2% for scalps)
  427  - Max 5 open positions
  428  - If session is mid_day or bad hours: confidence must be >0.85 to trade
  429  
  430  {market_context}
  431  
  432  {memory_context}
  433  
  434  ## Decision Required
  435  Based on ALL the above, what is your trading decision?
  436  
  437  Respond ONLY with valid JSON, no markdown, no explanation outside JSON:
  438  {{
  439    "decision": "buy" or "sell" or "hold",
  440    "confidence": 0.0 to 1.0,
  441    "strategy_used": "MOMENTUM" or "BREAKOUT" or "MEAN_REVERSION" or "GAPPER" or "SCALP" or "NONE",
  442    "reasoning": "2-3 sentences explaining your decision with specific reference to the indicators",
  443    "entry_price": current price or null,
  444    "target_price": your take profit target or null,
  445    "stop_price": your stop loss or null,
  446    "urgency": "high" or "medium" or "low"
  447  }}"""
  448  
  449  
  450  # ─── SCANNER DE PRIORITÉ ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  451  
  452  def rank_symbols(symbols_data: dict) -> list:
  453      """
  454      Classe les symboles par ordre de priorité d'opportunité.
  455      symbols_data = {symbol: {"indicators": ..., "patterns": ...}}
  456      Retourne une liste triée du plus au moins intéressant.
  457      """
  458      ranked = []
  459      for symbol, data in symbols_data.items():
  460          patterns = data.get("patterns", {})
  461          indicators = data.get("indicators", {})
  462          score = patterns.get("score", 0)
  463  
  464          # Bonus crypto en dehors des heures de marché
  465          if "/" in symbol and not is_good_stock_window():
  466              score += 10
  467  
  468          # Bonus gapper
  469          if "GAPPER" in patterns.get("patterns", []):
  470              score += 50
  471  
  472          # Bonus volume élevé
  473          if indicators.get("high_volume"):
  474              score += 15
  475  
  476          ranked.append((symbol, score))
  477  
  478      ranked.sort(key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)
  479      return [s for s, _ in ranked]

    1  """
    2  regime.py — Market Regime Detection
    3  Detects current market regime and adjusts ALL trading parameters accordingly.
    4  Bull / Bear / Choppy / Panic — everything changes based on regime.
    5  """
    6  import logging
    7  from datetime import datetime, timezone
    8  from typing import Optional
    9  import requests
   10  
   11  logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
   12  
   13  # ── Regime definitions ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   14  
   15  REGIMES = {
   16      "bull":   "Bull Market — aggressive longs, full sizes, let winners run",
   17      "bear":   "Bear Market — short bias, small longs, large shorts on rallies",
   18      "choppy": "Choppy — mean reversion only, take profits fast, no overnight holds",
   19      "panic":  "Panic — no new longs, wait for capitulation, one mean reversion only",
   20  }
   21  
   22  # ── Parameter adjustments per regime ─────────────────────────────────────────
   23  
   24  REGIME_PARAMS = {
   25      "bull": {
   26          "confidence_threshold": 65,
   27          "position_size_multiplier": 1.0,
   28          "score_long_threshold": 60,
   29          "score_short_threshold": 25,
   30          "hold_overnight": True,
   31          "trailing_stop_multiplier": 1.0,
   32          "max_positions": 5,
   33      },
   34      "bear": {
   35          "confidence_threshold": 72,
   36          "position_size_multiplier": 0.6,
   37          "score_long_threshold": 72,
   38          "score_short_threshold": 35,
   39          "hold_overnight": False,
   40          "trailing_stop_multiplier": 0.7,
   41          "max_positions": 3,
   42      },
   43      "choppy": {
   44          "confidence_threshold": 75,
   45          "position_size_multiplier": 0.5,
   46          "score_long_threshold": 75,
   47          "score_short_threshold": 30,
   48          "hold_overnight": False,
   49          "trailing_stop_multiplier": 0.6,
   50          "max_positions": 2,
   51      },
   52      "panic": {
   53          "confidence_threshold": 85,
   54          "position_size_multiplier": 0.3,
   55          "score_long_threshold": 88,
   56          "score_short_threshold": 20,
   57          "hold_overnight": False,
   58          "trailing_stop_multiplier": 0.5,
   59          "max_positions": 1,
   60      },
   61  }
   62  
   63  # Score adjustments injected into Claude prompt per regime
   64  REGIME_SCORE_ADJUSTMENTS = {
   65      "bull":   {"long_bonus": +10, "short_penalty": -10},
   66      "bear":   {"long_bonus": -10, "short_penalty": +10},
   67      "choppy": {"long_bonus": -5,  "short_penalty": +5},
   68      "panic":  {"long_bonus": -20, "short_penalty": +15},
   69  }
   70  
   71  
   72  class MarketRegime:
   73      """
   74      Detects current market regime using VIX, DXY, and S&P 500 trend.
   75      Caches results for 30 minutes to avoid excessive API calls.
   76      """
   77  
   78      def __init__(self):
   79          self._cache = {
   80              "regime": "bull",
   81              "vix": None,
   82              "dxy": None,
   83              "sp500_trend": None,
   84              "cached_at": None,
   85          }
   86          logger.info("✅ MarketRegime initialized")
   87  
   88      # ── Data fetching ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   89  
   90      def _fetch_vix(self) -> Optional[float]:
   91          """Fetch current VIX from Yahoo Finance."""
   92          try:
   93              url = "https://query1.finance.yahoo.com/v8/finance/chart/%5EVIX?interval=1d&range=2d"
   94              headers = {"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0"}
   95              resp = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=5)
   96              data = resp.json()
   97              closes = data["chart"]["result"][0]["indicators"]["quote"][0]["close"]
   98              vix = [c for c in closes if c is not None][-1]
   99              logger.info(f"📊 VIX: {vix:.2f}")
  100              return round(vix, 2)
  101          except Exception as e:
  102              logger.warning(f"VIX fetch failed: {e}")
  103              return None
  104  
  105      def _fetch_dxy_trend(self) -> Optional[str]:
  106          """Fetch DXY (US Dollar Index) trend — rising or falling."""
  107          try:
  108              url = "https://query1.finance.yahoo.com/v8/finance/chart/DX-Y.NYB?interval=1d&range=5d"
  109              headers = {"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0"}
  110              resp = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=5)
  111              data = resp.json()
  112              closes = data["chart"]["result"][0]["indicators"]["quote"][0]["close"]
  113              closes = [c for c in closes if c is not None]
  114              if len(closes) < 2:
  115                  return "neutral"
  116              change = (closes[-1] - closes[-3]) / closes[-3] * 100
  117              if change > 0.3:
  118                  trend = "rising"
  119              elif change < -0.3:
  120                  trend = "falling"
  121              else:
  122                  trend = "neutral"
  123              logger.info(f"📊 DXY trend: {trend} ({change:+.2f}% over 3 days)")
  124              return trend
  125          except Exception as e:
  126              logger.warning(f"DXY fetch failed: {e}")
  127              return None
  128  
  129      def _fetch_sp500_trend(self) -> Optional[str]:
  130          """Check if S&P 500 is above or below its 200-day moving average."""
  131          try:
  132              url = "https://query1.finance.yahoo.com/v8/finance/chart/SPY?interval=1d&range=220d"
  133              headers = {"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0"}
  134              resp = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=5)
  135              data = resp.json()
  136              closes = data["chart"]["result"][0]["indicators"]["quote"][0]["close"]
  137              closes = [c for c in closes if c is not None]
  138              if len(closes) < 200:
  139                  return "unknown"
  140              ma200 = sum(closes[-200:]) / 200
  141              current = closes[-1]
  142              pct_from_ma = (current - ma200) / ma200 * 100
  143              if pct_from_ma > 2:
  144                  trend = "above_ma200"
  145              elif pct_from_ma < -2:
  146                  trend = "below_ma200"
  147              else:
  148                  trend = "at_ma200"
  149              logger.info(f"📊 SPY vs MA200: {trend} ({pct_from_ma:+.1f}%)")
  150              return trend
  151          except Exception as e:
  152              logger.warning(f"SP500 trend fetch failed: {e}")
  153              return None
  154  
  155      # ── Regime detection ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  156  
  157      def detect_regime(self, force_refresh: bool = False) -> str:
  158          """
  159          Detect current market regime.
  160          Caches for 30 minutes. Returns: 'bull' | 'bear' | 'choppy' | 'panic'
  161          """
  162          now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
  163  
  164          # Use cache if fresh (30 min)
  165          if not force_refresh and self._cache["cached_at"]:
  166              age = (now - self._cache["cached_at"]).total_seconds()
  167              if age < 1800:
  168                  return self._cache["regime"]
  169  
  170          vix = self._fetch_vix()
  171          dxy = self._fetch_dxy_trend()
  172          sp500 = self._fetch_sp500_trend()
  173  
  174          regime = self._classify_regime(vix, dxy, sp500)
  175  
  176          self._cache.update({
  177              "regime": regime,
  178              "vix": vix,
  179              "dxy": dxy,
  180              "sp500_trend": sp500,
  181              "cached_at": now,
  182          })
  183  
  184          logger.info(f"🎯 Market regime: {regime.upper()} | VIX={vix} | DXY={dxy} | SP500={sp500}")
  185          return regime
  186  
  187      def _classify_regime(self, vix, dxy, sp500) -> str:
  188          """Core regime classification logic."""
  189          # Panic: VIX > 35 — extreme fear
  190          if vix and vix > 35:
  191              return "panic"
  192  
  193          # Bear: VIX elevated + S&P below 200MA + DXY rising
  194          bear_signals = 0
  195          if vix and vix > 25:
  196              bear_signals += 2
  197          if sp500 == "below_ma200":
  198              bear_signals += 2
  199          if dxy == "rising":
  200              bear_signals += 1
  201  
  202          if bear_signals >= 3:
  203              return "bear"
  204  
  205          # Choppy: Mixed signals
  206          choppy_signals = 0
  207          if vix and 18 < vix <= 25:
  208              choppy_signals += 1
  209          if sp500 == "at_ma200":
  210              choppy_signals += 1
  211          if dxy == "neutral":
  212              choppy_signals += 1
  213  
  214          if choppy_signals >= 2:
  215              return "choppy"
  216  
  217          # Bull: Low VIX + S&P above 200MA + DXY neutral or falling
  218          return "bull"
  219  
  220      # ── Parameter access ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  221  
  222      def get_params(self) -> dict:
  223          """Returns current regime parameters for use throughout the system."""
  224          regime = self.detect_regime()
  225          params = REGIME_PARAMS[regime].copy()
  226          params["regime"] = regime
  227          params["description"] = REGIMES[regime]
  228          return params
  229  
  230      def get_score_adjustments(self) -> dict:
  231          """Returns score bonuses/penalties for current regime."""
  232          regime = self.detect_regime()
  233          return REGIME_SCORE_ADJUSTMENTS[regime]
  234  
  235      def build_regime_context(self) -> str:
  236          """
  237          Builds a regime summary string for injection into Claude's prompt.
  238          """
  239          regime = self.detect_regime()
  240          params = REGIME_PARAMS[regime]
  241          vix = self._cache.get("vix")
  242          dxy = self._cache.get("dxy")
  243          sp500 = self._cache.get("sp500_trend")
  244          adj = REGIME_SCORE_ADJUSTMENTS[regime]
  245  
  246          lines = [
  247              "=== MARKET REGIME ===",
  248              f"Regime: {regime.upper()} — {REGIMES[regime]}",
  249              f"VIX: {vix if vix else 'N/A'} {'⚠️ ELEVATED' if vix and vix > 25 else ''}",
  250              f"DXY: {dxy if dxy else 'N/A'} {'⚠️ BEARISH FOR CRYPTO' if dxy == 'rising' else '✅ BULLISH FOR CRYPTO' if dxy == 'falling' else ''}",
  251              f"S&P 500 vs 200MA: {sp500 if sp500 else 'N/A'}",
  252              f"Score adjustments: LONG {adj['long_bonus']:+d} | SHORT {adj['short_penalty']:+d}",
  253              f"Max positions: {params['max_positions']} | Size multiplier: {params['position_size_multiplier']}x",
  254              f"Overnight holds: {'YES' if params['hold_overnight'] else 'NO — close before market close'}",
  255          ]
  256  
  257          if regime == "bear":
  258              lines.append("⚠️ BEAR MODE: Prefer shorts on rallies. Longs only on exceptional setups.")
  259          elif regime == "panic":
  260              lines.append("🔴 PANIC MODE: Extreme caution. Wait for capitulation. One trade max.")
  261          elif regime == "choppy":
  262              lines.append("⚡ CHOPPY MODE: Take profits fast. Mean reversion only. No trend trades.")
  263          else:
  264              lines.append("✅ BULL MODE: Let winners run. Full position sizes on quality setups.")
  265  
  266          return "\n".join(lines)
