    1  """
    2  scanner.py — Dynamic Top Movers + News Sentiment
    3  """
    4  import logging
    5  import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET
    6  from datetime import datetime, timezone
    7  import requests
    8  import alpaca_trade_api as tradeapi
    9  import config
   10  
   11  logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
   12  
   13  ECONOMIC_EVENTS = [
   14      {"date": "2026-04-02", "event": "Fed Meeting"},
   15      {"date": "2026-04-03", "event": "Jobs Report (NFP)"},
   16      {"date": "2026-04-14", "event": "CPI Inflation"},
   17      {"date": "2026-04-29", "event": "Fed Meeting"},
   18      {"date": "2026-05-08", "event": "Jobs Report"},
   19      {"date": "2026-05-13", "event": "CPI Inflation"},
   20      {"date": "2026-06-17", "event": "Fed Meeting"},
   21  ]
   22  
   23  # Confirmed Q1/Q2 2026 earnings dates — update as IRs announce
   24  EARNINGS_DATES = {
   25      "TSLA":  "2026-04-22",
   26      "GOOGL": "2026-04-29",
   27      "MSFT":  "2026-04-30",
   28      "META":  "2026-04-30",
   29      "AAPL":  "2026-05-01",
   30      "AMD":   "2026-05-06",
   31      "NVDA":  "2026-05-28",
   32  }
   33  
   34  NEWS_FEEDS = [
   35      "https://feeds.marketwatch.com/marketwatch/topstories/",
   36      "https://search.cnbc.com/rs/search/combinedcms/view.xml?partnerId=wrss01&id=100003114",
   37      "https://news.google.com/rss/search?q=stock+market+economy+fed&hl=en-US&gl=US&ceid=US:en",
   38  ]
   39  
   40  RSS_HEADERS = {
   41      "User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (compatible; TradingAgent/1.0; +https://alpaca.markets)"
   42  }
   43  
   44  BULLISH_KEYWORDS = ["rate cut", "fed pivot", "strong jobs", "beat expectations",
   45      "record high", "bull market", "stimulus", "better than expected", "upgrade"]
   46  
   47  BEARISH_KEYWORDS = ["tariff", "trade war", "recession", "rate hike", "layoffs",
   48      "miss expectations", "downgrade", "inflation surge", "trump tariff",
   49      "china trade", "worse than expected", "hawkish"]
   50  
   51  HIGH_ALERT_KEYWORDS = ["trump", "federal reserve", "emergency rate",
   52      "war", "sanctions", "default", "collapse", "crisis"]
   53  
   54  # Only keep headlines relevant to financial markets — excludes personal finance,
   55  # tax advice, lifestyle articles, etc.
   56  FINANCE_FILTER_KEYWORDS = [
   57      "stock", "market", "share", "equity", "index", "dow", "nasdaq", "s&p", "spy",
   58      "fed", "federal reserve", "interest rate", "rate cut", "rate hike", "powell",
   59      "earnings", "revenue", "profit", "quarter", "ipo", "merger", "acquisition",
   60      "crypto", "bitcoin", "ethereum", "blockchain", "coin",
   61      "tariff", "trade war", "sanction", "import duty", "export",
   62      "inflation", "cpi", "pce", "gdp", "recession", "jobs report", "unemployment",
   63      "oil", "gold", "commodity", "bond", "treasury", "yield", "debt",
   64      "dollar", "currency", "forex", "yuan", "yen", "euro",
   65      "wall street", "hedge fund", "bank", "jpmorgan", "goldman", "morgan stanley",
   66      "apple", "nvidia", "tesla", "meta", "google", "amazon", "microsoft", "intel",
   67      "tech stock", "semiconductor", "chip", "ai stock",
   68      "economy", "economic", "fiscal", "monetary", "deficit",
   69      "opec", "china trade", "supply chain", "manufacturing",
   70      "rally", "selloff", "correction", "bull market", "bear market",
   71      "war", "sanctions", "geopolit", "trump", "biden", "white house policy",
   72  ]
   73  
   74  class MarketScanner:
   75      def __init__(self):
   76          self.api = tradeapi.REST(
   77              config.ALPACA_API_KEY,
   78              config.ALPACA_SECRET_KEY,
   79              config.ALPACA_BASE_URL
   80          )
   81          self._news_cache = {"headlines": [], "sentiment": "neutral", "cached_at": None}
   82          self._movers_cache = {"symbols": [], "cached_at": None}
   83          logger.info("✅ MarketScanner initialized")
   84  
   85      def get_top_movers(self, top_n=6):
   86          now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
   87          if self._movers_cache["cached_at"]:
   88              age = (now - self._movers_cache["cached_at"]).total_seconds()
   89              if age < 900 and self._movers_cache["symbols"]:
   90                  return self._movers_cache["symbols"]
   91          try:
   92              assets = self.api.list_assets(status="active", asset_class="us_equity")
   93              tradeable = [a for a in assets if a.tradable and a.fractionable]
   94              symbols = [a.symbol for a in tradeable[:500]]
   95              snapshots = self.api.get_snapshots(symbols)
   96              gappers = []
   97              movers  = []
   98              for symbol, snap in snapshots.items():
   99                  try:
  100                      if not snap.daily_bar or not snap.prev_daily_bar:
  101                          continue
  102                      prev       = snap.prev_daily_bar.close
  103                      curr       = snap.daily_bar.close
  104                      prev_vol   = snap.prev_daily_bar.volume or 1
  105                      volume     = snap.daily_bar.volume
  106                      if prev <= 0:
  107                          continue
  108                      change_pct   = ((curr - prev) / prev) * 100
  109                      volume_ratio = round(volume / prev_vol, 1) if prev_vol > 0 else 0
  110                      is_microcap  = 0.50 <= curr <= 10.0
  111  
  112                      # Qualify as a mover:
  113                      # - Standard:  |change| ≥ 3% AND volume > 50 000
  114                      # - Micro/small cap ($0.50–$10): volume must exceed 500 000 (higher bar)
  115                      if is_microcap:
  116                          qualifies = abs(change_pct) >= 3 and volume > 500_000
  117                      else:
  118                          qualifies = abs(change_pct) >= 3 and volume > 50_000
  119  
  120                      if not qualifies:
  121                          continue
  122  
  123                      entry = {
  124                          "symbol":       symbol,
  125                          "price":        round(curr, 4),
  126                          "change_pct":   round(change_pct, 2),
  127                          "volume":       volume,
  128                          "volume_ratio": volume_ratio,
  129                          "direction":    "up" if change_pct > 0 else "down",
  130                          "is_gapper":    False,
  131                          "is_microcap":  is_microcap,
  132                      }
  133  
  134                      # GAPPER ALERT: >50% gain on >5× average volume
  135                      if change_pct >= 50 and volume_ratio >= 5:
  136                          entry["is_gapper"] = True
  137                          logger.info(
  138                              f"🚨 GAPPER ALERT: {symbol} +{change_pct:.1f}% "
  139                              f"volume={volume_ratio}x — potential 100-200% move"
  140                          )
  141                          gappers.append(entry)
  142                      else:
  143                          movers.append(entry)
  144  
  145                  except Exception:
  146                      continue
  147  
  148              # Sort each bucket by magnitude; gappers always win
  149              gappers.sort(key=lambda x: x["change_pct"], reverse=True)
  150              movers.sort(key=lambda x: abs(x["change_pct"]), reverse=True)
  151  
  152              # Gappers all included; regular movers capped at top_n
  153              top = gappers + movers[:top_n]
  154              self._movers_cache = {"symbols": top, "cached_at": now}
  155  
  156              gap_labels   = [f"🚨{m['symbol']} +{m['change_pct']:.1f}% {m['volume_ratio']}x" for m in gappers]
  157              mover_labels = [f"{m['symbol']} {m['change_pct']:+.1f}%" for m in movers[:top_n]]
  158              if gap_labels:
  159                  logger.info(f"🚨 GAPPERS: {gap_labels}")
  160              logger.info(f"🔥 Top movers: {mover_labels}")
  161              return top
  162          except Exception as e:
  163              logger.error(f"get_top_movers error: {e}")
  164              return []
  165  
  166      def get_dynamic_watchlist(self):
  167          from strategy import is_good_stock_window
  168          seen = set()
  169          watchlist = []
  170  
  171          def _add(symbols):
  172              for s in symbols:
  173                  if s not in seen:
  174                      seen.add(s)
  175                      watchlist.append(s)
  176  
  177          if is_good_stock_window():
  178              movers = self.get_top_movers(top_n=6)
  179  
  180              # Split movers into gappers (highest priority) and regular movers
  181              gapper_symbols = [m["symbol"] for m in movers if m.get("is_gapper")]
  182              regular_symbols = [m["symbol"] for m in movers if not m.get("is_gapper")]
  183  
  184              _add(gapper_symbols)          # 1. GAPPERS — absolute priority
  185              _add(regular_symbols)         # 2. Regular top movers
  186              _add(config.BLUECHIP_SYMBOLS) # 3. Blue chips — always present
  187  
  188          _add(config.CRYPTO_SYMBOLS)       # 4. Crypto — always present
  189  
  190          gappers_in = [s for s in watchlist if s in {m["symbol"] for m in self._movers_cache.get("symbols", []) if m.get("is_gapper")}]
  191          bc_in_list  = [s for s in config.BLUECHIP_SYMBOLS if s in seen]
  192          mover_only  = [s for s in watchlist if s not in config.BLUECHIP_SYMBOLS and s not in config.CRYPTO_SYMBOLS and s not in gappers_in]
  193          logger.info(
  194              f"📋 Watchlist ({len(watchlist)}): "
  195              f"gappers={gappers_in} | "
  196              f"movers={mover_only} | "
  197              f"bluechips={bc_in_list} | "
  198              f"crypto={[s for s in watchlist if s in config.CRYPTO_SYMBOLS]}"
  199          )
  200          return watchlist
  201  
  202      def fetch_news_headlines(self):
  203          now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
  204          if self._news_cache["cached_at"]:
  205              age = (now - self._news_cache["cached_at"]).total_seconds()
  206              if age < 600:
  207                  return self._news_cache["headlines"]
  208          headlines = []
  209          for feed_url in NEWS_FEEDS:
  210              try:
  211                  resp = requests.get(feed_url, timeout=8, headers=RSS_HEADERS)
  212                  if resp.status_code != 200:
  213                      logger.warning(f"RSS {resp.status_code}: {feed_url[:60]}")
  214                      continue
  215                  root = ET.fromstring(resp.content)
  216                  fetched = 0
  217                  for item in root.findall(".//item"):
  218                      title = item.find("title")
  219                      if title is not None and title.text:
  220                          text = title.text.strip()
  221                          # Google News wraps titles in CDATA — clean angle-bracket artefacts
  222                          text_lower = text.lower()
  223                          is_finance = any(kw in text_lower for kw in FINANCE_FILTER_KEYWORDS)
  224                          if text and "<" not in text and is_finance:
  225                              headlines.append(text)
  226                              fetched += 1
  227                      if fetched >= 5:
  228                          break
  229                  logger.debug(f"RSS OK ({fetched} headlines): {feed_url[:60]}")
  230              except Exception as e:
  231                  logger.warning(f"RSS error ({feed_url[:40]}): {e}")
  232          self._news_cache["headlines"] = headlines
  233          self._news_cache["cached_at"] = now
  234          return headlines
  235  
  236      def analyze_sentiment(self):
  237          headlines = self.fetch_news_headlines()
  238          if not headlines:
  239              return {"sentiment": "neutral", "score": 0, "alerts": []}
  240          score = 0
  241          alerts = []
  242          text = " ".join(headlines).lower()
  243          for kw in BULLISH_KEYWORDS:
  244              if kw in text:
  245                  score += 1
  246          for kw in BEARISH_KEYWORDS:
  247              if kw in text:
  248                  score -= 1
  249          for kw in HIGH_ALERT_KEYWORDS:
  250              if kw in text:
  251                  alerts.append(f"⚡ HIGH ALERT: '{kw.upper()}' detected in headlines")
  252          if score >= 3: sentiment = "very_bullish"
  253          elif score >= 1: sentiment = "bullish"
  254          elif score <= -3: sentiment = "very_bearish"
  255          elif score <= -1: sentiment = "bearish"
  256          else: sentiment = "neutral"
  257          logger.info(f"📰 Sentiment: {sentiment} (score: {score})")
  258          ts = datetime.now(timezone.utc).strftime("%H:%M UTC")
  259          return {"sentiment": sentiment, "score": score, "alerts": alerts, "headlines": headlines[:3], "ts": ts}
  260  
  261      def check_economic_calendar(self):
  262          today = datetime.now(timezone.utc).strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
  263          for event in ECONOMIC_EVENTS:
  264              if event["date"] == today:
  265                  return {"event": event["event"], "timing": "today",
  266                      "note": f"⚡ {event['event']} TODAY — high volatility expected"}
  267          return {"event": None, "note": ""}
  268  
  269      def get_earnings_alerts(self, symbols=None):
  270          """
  271          Return earnings alerts for stocks within ±1 day of their earnings date.
  272            type='earnings_day'  → reports TODAY (skip the stock)
  273            type='pre_earnings'  → reports in 1–2 days (cut position to 10%)
  274            type='post_earnings' → reported yesterday (watch for gap play)
  275          """
  276          from datetime import date as date_cls
  277          today = datetime.now(timezone.utc).date()
  278          alerts = []
  279          for symbol, date_str in EARNINGS_DATES.items():
  280              if symbols and symbol not in symbols:
  281                  continue
  282              edate     = datetime.strptime(date_str, "%Y-%m-%d").date()
  283              days_away = (edate - today).days
  284              if days_away == 0:
  285                  alerts.append({"symbol": symbol, "days_away": 0,  "type": "earnings_day"})
  286              elif 1 <= days_away <= 2:
  287                  alerts.append({"symbol": symbol, "days_away": days_away, "type": "pre_earnings"})
  288              elif days_away == -1:
  289                  alerts.append({"symbol": symbol, "days_away": -1, "type": "post_earnings"})
  290          return alerts
  291  
  292      def build_market_context(self, symbol=None):
  293          sentiment = self.analyze_sentiment()
  294          calendar  = self.check_economic_calendar()
  295          movers    = self.get_top_movers(top_n=6)
  296          earnings  = self.get_earnings_alerts()
  297  
  298          lines = ["=== MARKET INTELLIGENCE ==="]
  299          emoji = {"very_bullish":"🚀","bullish":"🟢","neutral":"⚪","bearish":"🔴","very_bearish":"💀"}
  300          lines.append(f"📰 NEWS: {emoji.get(sentiment['sentiment'],'⚪')} {sentiment['sentiment'].upper()} (score: {sentiment['score']})")
  301          for alert in sentiment.get("alerts", []):
  302              lines.append(f"  {alert}")
  303          if calendar["event"]:
  304              lines.append(f"📅 CALENDAR: {calendar['note']}")
  305  
  306          # Earnings proximity warnings — passed to Claude so it can factor in volatility
  307          for ea in earnings:
  308              if ea["type"] == "earnings_day":
  309                  lines.append(
  310                      f"🚨 EARNINGS DAY: {ea['symbol']} reports TODAY — "
  311                      f"DO NOT ENTER any position, risk is too high"
  312                  )
  313              elif ea["type"] == "pre_earnings":
  314                  lines.append(
  315                      f"⚠️ EARNINGS ALERT: {ea['symbol']} reports in {ea['days_away']} day(s) — "
  316                      f"expect high volatility, reduce position size to 10% max"
  317                  )
  318              elif ea["type"] == "post_earnings":
  319                  lines.append(
  320                      f"📈 POST-EARNINGS: {ea['symbol']} reported yesterday — "
  321                      f"if gapping up >5% on high volume, treat as priority gapper (score 90+, up to 40% position)"
  322                  )
  323  
  324          if movers:
  325              lines.append("🔥 TOP MOVERS:")
  326              for m in movers[:6]:
  327                  vol_str = f" vol={m.get('volume_ratio','')}x" if m.get("volume_ratio") else ""
  328                  tag     = " 🚨 GAPPER — prioritize, potential 100-200% move" if m.get("is_gapper") else ""
  329                  lines.append(f"  {'↑' if m['direction']=='up' else '↓'} {m['symbol']}: {m['change_pct']:+.1f}%{vol_str}{tag}")
  330          if symbol:
  331              sm = next((m for m in movers if m["symbol"] == symbol), None)
  332              if sm:
  333                  if sm.get("is_gapper"):
  334                      lines.append(
  335                          f"🚨 {symbol} IS A CONFIRMED GAPPER: {sm['change_pct']:+.1f}% "
  336                          f"volume={sm.get('volume_ratio','')}x average — "
  337                          f"score this 90+, use max position size, set tight trailing stop"
  338                      )
  339                  else:
  340                      lines.append(f"⭐ {symbol} IS A TOP MOVER: {sm['change_pct']:+.1f}%")
  341          if sentiment["sentiment"] in ["very_bullish", "bullish"]:
  342              lines.append("💡 Conditions favorable for LONG positions")
  343          elif sentiment["sentiment"] in ["very_bearish", "bearish"]:
  344              lines.append("💡 Conditions favorable for SHORT positions — tighten stops on longs")
  345          else:
  346              lines.append("💡 Neutral market — stick to technical signals only")
  347          return "\n".join(lines)


================================================================================
FILE: trading-agent/synthesis.py  (163 lines)
================================================================================

    1  """
    2  synthesis.py — Master Scoring Engine
    3  Combines ALL intelligence layers into one final conviction score.
    4  This runs BEFORE every Claude API call.
    5  Only calls Claude when final score crosses the threshold.
    6  """
    7  import logging
    8  from news_intelligence import NewsIntelligence
    9  
   10  logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
   11  
   12  # Score thresholds
   13  LONG_THRESHOLD      = 60
   14  SHORT_THRESHOLD     = 30
   15  CONFIDENCE_MINIMUM  = 70
   16  
   17  
   18  class SynthesisEngine:
   19  
   20      def __init__(self, regime, correlations, geometry, scanner):
   21          self.regime       = regime
   22          self.correlations = correlations
   23          self.geometry     = geometry
   24          self.scanner      = scanner   # kept for non-news uses (movers cache, etc.)
   25          self.news         = NewsIntelligence()
   26          logger.info("✅ SynthesisEngine initialized — all layers connected")
   27  
   28      def run(
   29          self,
   30          symbol: str,
   31          base_score: float,
   32          opens: list,
   33          highs: list,
   34          lows: list,
   35          closes: list,
   36          volumes: list,
   37          open_positions: list,
   38          side: str = "long",
   39      ) -> dict:
   40          """
   41          Master pre-trade analysis.
   42          Returns final score, full context string, and stop/target levels.
   43          Only proceed to Claude if final score crosses threshold.
   44          """
   45  
   46          # ── Layer 1: Market Regime ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   47          regime_params   = self.regime.get_params()
   48          regime_name     = regime_params["regime"]
   49          regime_adj      = self.regime.get_score_adjustments()
   50          regime_context  = self.regime.build_regime_context()
   51  
   52          long_threshold   = regime_params["score_long_threshold"]
   53          short_threshold  = regime_params["score_short_threshold"]
   54          confidence_min   = regime_params["confidence_threshold"]
   55          size_multiplier  = regime_params["position_size_multiplier"]
   56  
   57          # ── Layer 2: Correlations ──────────────────────────────────────────────
   58          # refresh_prices uses 5-min cache; parent cycle already warmed it for all symbols
   59          changes      = self.correlations.refresh_prices([symbol])
   60          dxy_trend    = self.regime._cache.get("dxy") or "neutral"
   61          is_crypto    = "/" in symbol
   62  
   63          corr_conflict = self.correlations.check_correlation_conflict(symbol, open_positions)
   64          rel_strength  = self.correlations.detect_relative_strength(symbol, changes)
   65          dxy_impact    = (
   66              self.correlations.get_dxy_crypto_adjustment(dxy_trend)
   67              if is_crypto else {"adjustment": 0, "reason": "N/A"}
   68          )
   69          corr_context  = self.correlations.build_correlation_context(
   70              symbol, open_positions, changes, dxy_trend
   71          )
   72  
   73          # ── Layer 3: Geometry ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
   74          geo         = self.geometry.build_geometry_context(
   75              symbol, opens, highs, lows, closes, volumes, side
   76          )
   77          geo_context = geo["context"]
   78  
   79          # ── Layer 4: News Intelligence (Tier 1-4 classification) ─────────────────
   80          # Replaces simple scanner keyword detection with full tiered analysis:
   81          # Tier 1 = market-moving (±25), Tier 2 = directional (±12-15),
   82          # Tier 3 = contextual (±6), + Trump direction signal + earnings whisper
   83          news_result  = self.news.analyze(symbol)
   84          news_adj     = max(-35, min(35, news_result["total_score_adjustment"]))
   85          news_context = news_result["context"]
   86  
   87          # ── Final Score Calculation ────────────────────────────────────────────
   88          regime_score_adj = (
   89              regime_adj["long_bonus"] if side == "long" else regime_adj["short_penalty"]
   90          )
   91  
   92          final_score = (
   93              base_score
   94              + regime_score_adj
   95              + rel_strength["score_adjustment"]
   96              + (dxy_impact["adjustment"] if is_crypto else 0)
   97              + corr_conflict.get("score_adjustment", 0)
   98              + geo["score_adjustment"]
   99              + news_adj
  100          )
  101          final_score = max(0, min(100, final_score))
  102  
  103          # ── Decision ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  104          if side == "long":
  105              should_call_claude = final_score >= long_threshold
  106              decision_reason    = (
  107                  f"LONG score {final_score:.0f} "
  108                  f"{'≥' if should_call_claude else '<'} threshold {long_threshold}"
  109              )
  110          else:
  111              should_call_claude = final_score <= short_threshold
  112              decision_reason    = (
  113                  f"SHORT score {final_score:.0f} "
  114                  f"{'≤' if should_call_claude else '>'} threshold {short_threshold}"
  115              )
  116  
  117          # ── Build Master Context for Claude ───────────────────────────────────
  118          score_breakdown = (
  119              f"Base: {base_score:.0f} | "
  120              f"Regime: {regime_score_adj:+.0f} | "
  121              f"RelStr: {rel_strength['score_adjustment']:+.0f} | "
  122              f"DXY: {dxy_impact['adjustment']:+.0f} | "
  123              f"Corr: {corr_conflict.get('score_adjustment', 0):+.0f} | "
  124              f"Geo: {geo['score_adjustment']:+.0f} | "
  125              f"News: {news_adj:+.0f} | "
  126              f"FINAL: {final_score:.0f}"
  127          )
  128  
  129          synthesis_lines = [
  130              "=== SYNTHESIS SCORE ===",
  131              score_breakdown,
  132              f"Decision: {decision_reason}",
  133          ]
  134  
  135          full_context = "\n\n".join([
  136              regime_context,
  137              corr_context,
  138              geo_context,
  139              news_context,          # full Tier 1-4 classification from NewsIntelligence
  140              "\n".join(synthesis_lines),
  141          ])
  142  
  143          logger.info(
  144              f"🧠 SYNTHESIS {symbol} {side.upper()}: {score_breakdown} | "
  145              f"{'→ CALLING CLAUDE' if should_call_claude else '→ SKIPPED'}"
  146          )
  147  
  148          return {
  149              "final_score":       final_score,
  150              "should_call_claude": should_call_claude,
  151              "decision_reason":   decision_reason,
  152              "score_breakdown":   score_breakdown,
  153              "full_context":      full_context,
  154              "stop_loss":         geo.get("stop_loss"),
  155              "take_profit":       geo.get("take_profit"),
  156              "stop_pct":          geo.get("stop_pct"),
  157              "target_pct":        geo.get("target_pct"),
  158              "risk_reward":       geo.get("risk_reward"),
  159              "size_multiplier":   size_multiplier,
  160              "confidence_minimum": confidence_min,
  161              "regime":            regime_name,
  162              "patterns":          geo.get("patterns_detected", []),
  163          }


================================================================================
FILE: trading-agent/correlations.py  (338 lines)

    1  """
    2  correlations.py — Inter-Asset Correlation Intelligence
    3  Detects correlation breakdowns, relative strength signals, and beta-adjusted sizing.
    4  The most powerful edge most retail bots completely miss.
    5  """
    6  import logging
    7  from datetime import datetime, timezone
    8  from typing import Optional
    9  import requests
   10  
   11  logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
   12  
   13  # ── Correlation matrix (static knowledge) ────────────────────────────────────
   14  
   15  # Expected correlation direction between asset pairs
   16  # 1.0 = perfectly correlated, -1.0 = perfectly inverse
   17  CORRELATION_MATRIX = {
   18      ("BTC/USD", "ETH/USD"):   0.88,
   19      ("BTC/USD", "SOL/USD"):   0.82,
   20      ("BTC/USD", "AVAX/USD"):  0.80,
   21      ("BTC/USD", "DOGE/USD"):  0.75,
   22      ("BTC/USD", "LINK/USD"):  0.78,
   23      ("BTC/USD", "XRP/USD"):   0.72,
   24      ("ETH/USD", "SOL/USD"):   0.85,
   25      ("BTC/USD", "QQQ"):       0.72,
   26      ("BTC/USD", "SPY"):       0.65,
   27      ("NVDA",    "AMD"):       0.80,
   28      ("NVDA",    "QQQ"):       0.75,
   29      ("TSLA",    "BTC/USD"):   0.60,
   30      ("AAPL",    "QQQ"):       0.85,
   31      ("META",    "GOOGL"):     0.78,
   32  }
   33  
   34  # Beta coefficients (how much more volatile vs BTC or NASDAQ)
   35  BETA = {
   36      "BTC/USD":  1.0,
   37      "ETH/USD":  1.1,
   38      "SOL/USD":  1.8,
   39      "AVAX/USD": 2.0,
   40      "DOGE/USD": 2.5,
   41      "LINK/USD": 1.9,
   42      "XRP/USD":  1.7,
   43      "SHIB/USD": 3.0,
   44      "TSLA":     1.5,
   45      "NVDA":     1.8,
   46      "AMD":      1.6,
   47      "META":     1.3,
   48      "GOOGL":    1.1,
   49      "AAPL":     1.0,
   50      "MSFT":     1.0,
   51      "QQQ":      1.0,
   52      "SPY":      0.8,
   53      "ARKK":     2.2,
   54  }
   55  
   56  # Sector groupings — never hold more than 2 from same sector
   57  SECTORS = {
   58      "crypto_large":    ["BTC/USD", "ETH/USD"],
   59      "crypto_mid":      ["SOL/USD", "AVAX/USD", "LINK/USD", "XRP/USD"],
   60      "crypto_meme":     ["DOGE/USD", "SHIB/USD"],
   61      "semis":           ["NVDA", "AMD"],
   62      "big_tech":        ["AAPL", "MSFT", "GOOGL", "META"],
   63      "etf_broad":       ["QQQ", "SPY"],
   64      "etf_speculative": ["ARKK"],
   65      "ev_disruptive":   ["TSLA"],
   66  }
   67  
   68  
   69  class CorrelationIntelligence:
   70      """
   71      Monitors inter-asset correlations in real-time.
   72      Detects breakdowns (relative strength signals) and enforces diversification.
   73      """
   74  
   75      # Expose module-level dict for use via self.CORRELATION_MATRIX
   76      CORRELATION_MATRIX = CORRELATION_MATRIX
   77  
   78      def __init__(self):
   79          self._price_cache: dict = {}
   80          self._cache_time: Optional[datetime] = None
   81          logger.info("✅ CorrelationIntelligence initialized")
   82  
   83      # ── Price fetching ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   84  
   85      def _fetch_current_change(self, symbol: str) -> Optional[float]:
   86          """Fetch today's % change for a symbol via Yahoo Finance."""
   87          try:
   88              yf_symbol = symbol.replace("/", "-")
   89              url = f"https://query1.finance.yahoo.com/v8/finance/chart/{yf_symbol}?interval=1d&range=2d"
   90              headers = {"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0"}
   91              resp = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=5)
   92              data = resp.json()
   93              closes = data["chart"]["result"][0]["indicators"]["quote"][0]["close"]
   94              closes = [c for c in closes if c is not None]
   95              if len(closes) < 2:
   96                  return None
   97              change = (closes[-1] - closes[-2]) / closes[-2] * 100
   98              return round(change, 3)
   99          except Exception:
  100              return None
  101  
  102      def refresh_prices(self, symbols: list) -> dict:
  103          """
  104          Fetch % change for a list of symbols.
  105          Caches for 5 minutes.
  106          """
  107          now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
  108          if self._cache_time:
  109              age = (now - self._cache_time).total_seconds()
  110              if age < 300 and self._price_cache:
  111                  return self._price_cache
  112  
  113          changes = {}
  114          for sym in symbols:
  115              chg = self._fetch_current_change(sym)
  116              if chg is not None:
  117                  changes[sym] = chg
  118  
  119          self._price_cache = changes
  120          self._cache_time = now
  121          logger.info(f"📊 Correlation prices refreshed: {len(changes)} symbols")
  122          return changes
  123  
  124      # ── Relative strength detection ───────────────────────────────────────────
  125  
  126      def detect_relative_strength(self, symbol: str, changes: dict) -> dict:
  127          """
  128          Detect if a symbol is showing relative strength or weakness vs correlated peers.
  129  
  130          BULLISH signal: Asset holds flat or rises while correlated peers fall.
  131          BEARISH signal: Asset falls while correlated peers rise.
  132  
  133          This is one of the highest-conviction signals in trading.
  134          """
  135          if symbol not in changes:
  136              return {"signal": "neutral", "score_adjustment": 0, "reason": "No price data"}
  137  
  138          asset_change = changes[symbol]
  139          correlated_peers = []
  140  
  141          # Find correlated peers
  142          for (a, b), corr in CORRELATION_MATRIX.items():
  143              if corr >= 0.7:  # Only strong correlations
  144                  if a == symbol and b in changes:
  145                      correlated_peers.append((b, changes[b], corr))
  146                  elif b == symbol and a in changes:
  147                      correlated_peers.append((a, changes[a], corr))
  148  
  149          if not correlated_peers:
  150              return {"signal": "neutral", "score_adjustment": 0, "reason": "No correlated peers available"}
  151  
  152          avg_peer_change = sum(c for _, c, _ in correlated_peers) / len(correlated_peers)
  153          divergence = asset_change - avg_peer_change
  154  
  155          # Relative strength threshold: asset outperforms peers by >1.5%
  156          if divergence > 1.5:
  157              signal = "relative_strength_bullish"
  158              score_adjustment = +20
  159              reason = f"{symbol} +{asset_change:.1f}% vs peers avg {avg_peer_change:.1f}% — strong buyer absorption"
  160          elif divergence > 0.8:
  161              signal = "mild_strength"
  162              score_adjustment = +10
  163              reason = f"{symbol} outperforming peers by {divergence:.1f}%"
  164          elif divergence < -1.5:
  165              signal = "relative_weakness_bearish"
  166              score_adjustment = -20
  167              reason = f"{symbol} {asset_change:.1f}% vs peers avg {avg_peer_change:.1f}% — selling pressure"
  168          elif divergence < -0.8:
  169              signal = "mild_weakness"
  170              score_adjustment = -10
  171              reason = f"{symbol} underperforming peers by {abs(divergence):.1f}%"
  172          else:
  173              signal = "neutral"
  174              score_adjustment = 0
  175              reason = f"{symbol} moving in line with peers"
  176  
  177          return {
  178              "signal": signal,
  179              "score_adjustment": score_adjustment,
  180              "reason": reason,
  181              "asset_change": asset_change,
  182              "peer_avg_change": round(avg_peer_change, 3),
  183              "divergence": round(divergence, 3),
  184              "peers": [(p, round(c, 3)) for p, c, _ in correlated_peers],
  185          }
  186  
  187      # ── DXY impact for crypto ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
  188  
  189      def get_dxy_crypto_adjustment(self, dxy_trend: str) -> dict:
  190          """
  191          DXY trend impact on crypto longs.
  192          Rising DXY = bad for crypto. Falling DXY = good for crypto.
  193          """
  194          if dxy_trend == "rising":
  195              return {
  196                  "adjustment": -15,
  197                  "reason": "DXY rising — historically bearish for crypto (inverse correlation -75%)",
  198              }
  199          elif dxy_trend == "falling":
  200              return {
  201                  "adjustment": +10,
  202                  "reason": "DXY falling — historically bullish for crypto",
  203              }
  204          return {"adjustment": 0, "reason": "DXY neutral"}
  205  
  206      # ── Correlation filter for open positions ─────────────────────────────────
  207  
  208      def check_correlation_conflict(self, new_symbol: str, open_positions: list) -> dict:
  209          """
  210          Check if opening a new position would create dangerous correlation overlap
  211          with existing open positions.
  212          Returns warning if conflict detected.
  213          """
  214          if not open_positions:
  215              return {"conflict": False, "reason": "No open positions"}
  216  
  217          conflicts = []
  218          for open_sym in open_positions:
  219              corr = self.CORRELATION_MATRIX.get(
  220                  (new_symbol, open_sym),
  221                  self.CORRELATION_MATRIX.get((open_sym, new_symbol), 0)
  222              )
  223              if corr >= 0.80:
  224                  conflicts.append((open_sym, corr))
  225  
  226          # Check sector overlap
  227          new_sector = self._get_sector(new_symbol)
  228          sector_count = sum(
  229              1 for s in open_positions
  230              if self._get_sector(s) == new_sector and new_sector != "unknown"
  231          )
  232  
  233          if conflicts:
  234              worst = max(conflicts, key=lambda x: x[1])
  235              return {
  236                  "conflict": True,
  237                  "score_adjustment": -20,
  238                  "reason": (
  239                      f"High correlation conflict: {new_symbol} vs {worst[0]} "
  240                      f"({worst[1]:.0%} corr). Diversify."
  241                  ),
  242                  "conflicts": conflicts,
  243              }
  244  
  245          if sector_count >= 2:
  246              return {
  247                  "conflict": True,
  248                  "score_adjustment": -10,
  249                  "reason": f"Sector concentration: already holding {sector_count} {new_sector} positions.",
  250              }
  251  
  252          return {"conflict": False, "score_adjustment": 0, "reason": "No correlation conflicts"}
  253  
  254      def _get_sector(self, symbol: str) -> str:
  255          for sector, symbols in SECTORS.items():
  256              if symbol in symbols:
  257                  return sector
  258          return "unknown"
  259  
  260      # ── Beta-adjusted position sizing ─────────────────────────────────────────
  261  
  262      def get_beta_adjusted_size(self, symbol: str, base_size_pct: float, regime: str) -> float:
  263          """
  264          Adjust position size based on asset beta and current regime.
  265          High beta assets get smaller positions in bear/choppy regimes.
  266          High beta assets get normal positions in bull regime.
  267          """
  268          beta = BETA.get(symbol, 1.0)
  269  
  270          if regime in ["bear", "choppy"]:
  271              if beta > 2.0:
  272                  adjusted = base_size_pct * 0.4
  273                  logger.info(f"⚠️ {symbol} beta={beta} in {regime} regime → size reduced to {adjusted:.1f}%")
  274              elif beta > 1.5:
  275                  adjusted = base_size_pct * 0.6
  276              elif beta > 1.2:
  277                  adjusted = base_size_pct * 0.8
  278              else:
  279                  adjusted = base_size_pct
  280          elif regime == "panic":
  281              adjusted = base_size_pct * 0.3
  282          else:
  283              # Bull regime: full size, slight bonus for high beta (more upside)
  284              if beta > 1.5:
  285                  adjusted = min(base_size_pct * 1.1, 40.0)  # Cap at 40%
  286              else:
  287                  adjusted = base_size_pct
  288  
  289          return round(adjusted, 1)
  290  
  291      # ── Context for Claude prompt ─────────────────────────────────────────────
  292  
  293      def build_correlation_context(
  294          self,
  295          symbol: str,
  296          open_positions: list,
  297          changes: dict,
  298          dxy_trend: str = "neutral"
  299      ) -> str:
  300          """
  301          Build a correlation intelligence summary for Claude's prompt.
  302          """
  303          rel_strength   = self.detect_relative_strength(symbol, changes)
  304          corr_conflict  = self.check_correlation_conflict(symbol, open_positions)
  305          dxy_impact     = self.get_dxy_crypto_adjustment(dxy_trend)
  306  
  307          is_crypto = "/" in symbol
  308  
  309          lines = ["=== CORRELATION INTELLIGENCE ==="]
  310  
  311          # Relative strength
  312          signal = rel_strength["signal"]
  313          emoji = "🟢" if "bullish" in signal else "🔴" if "bearish" in signal else "⚪"
  314          lines.append(f"Relative strength: {emoji} {signal.upper()}")
  315          lines.append(f"  → {rel_strength['reason']}")
  316          if rel_strength.get("peers"):
  317              peer_str = ", ".join([f"{p}: {c:+.1f}%" for p, c in rel_strength["peers"][:3]])
  318              lines.append(f"  Peers: {peer_str}")
  319  
  320          # DXY impact (crypto only)
  321          if is_crypto and dxy_impact["adjustment"] != 0:
  322              lines.append(f"DXY impact: {dxy_impact['reason']}")
  323  
  324          # Correlation conflicts
  325          if corr_conflict["conflict"]:
  326              lines.append(f"⚠️ CORRELATION CONFLICT: {corr_conflict['reason']}")
  327          else:
  328              lines.append("✅ No correlation conflicts with open positions")
  329  
  330          # Score summary
  331          total_adj = (
  332              rel_strength["score_adjustment"]
  333              + (dxy_impact["adjustment"] if is_crypto else 0)
  334              + corr_conflict.get("score_adjustment", 0)
  335          )
  336          lines.append(f"Total correlation score adjustment: {total_adj:+d}")
  337  
  338          return "\n".join(lines)

    1  """
    2  geometry.py — Geometric & Candlestick Analysis
    3  Support/resistance detection, candlestick patterns, chart patterns, ATR-based stops.
    4  Transforms arbitrary % stops into technically anchored levels.
    5  """
    6  import logging
    7  import numpy as np
    8  
    9  logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
   10  
   11  
   12  class GeometryAnalysis:
   13  
   14      def __init__(self):
   15          logger.info("✅ GeometryAnalysis initialized")
   16  
   17      # ── ATR Calculation ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   18  
   19      def calculate_atr(self, highs: list, lows: list, closes: list, period: int = 14) -> float:
   20          """Calculate Average True Range over given period."""
   21          if len(closes) < period + 1:
   22              return 0.0
   23          true_ranges = []
   24          for i in range(1, len(closes)):
   25              tr = max(
   26                  highs[i] - lows[i],
   27                  abs(highs[i] - closes[i - 1]),
   28                  abs(lows[i] - closes[i - 1])
   29              )
   30              true_ranges.append(tr)
   31          atr = sum(true_ranges[-period:]) / period
   32          return round(atr, 6)
   33  
   34      # ── Support & Resistance ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
   35  
   36      def find_support_resistance(
   37          self,
   38          closes: list,
   39          highs: list,
   40          lows: list,
   41          lookback: int = 50
   42      ) -> dict:
   43          """
   44          Identify key support and resistance levels using swing highs/lows.
   45          Score each level by how many times it has been tested.
   46          """
   47          if len(closes) < lookback:
   48              lookback = len(closes)
   49  
   50          recent_closes = closes[-lookback:]
   51          recent_highs  = highs[-lookback:]
   52          recent_lows   = lows[-lookback:]
   53          current_price = closes[-1]
   54  
   55          swing_highs = []
   56          swing_lows  = []
   57  
   58          for i in range(2, len(recent_highs) - 2):
   59              if recent_highs[i] > recent_highs[i-1] and recent_highs[i] > recent_highs[i+1]:
   60                  swing_highs.append(recent_highs[i])
   61              if recent_lows[i] < recent_lows[i-1] and recent_lows[i] < recent_lows[i+1]:
   62                  swing_lows.append(recent_lows[i])
   63  
   64          # Round numbers as additional levels
   65          magnitude = 10 ** (len(str(int(current_price))) - 2)
   66          round_levels = [
   67              round(current_price / magnitude) * magnitude * i / 10
   68              for i in range(8, 13)
   69          ]
   70  
   71          supports    = [l for l in swing_lows   if l < current_price * 0.999]
   72          resistances = [h for h in swing_highs  if h > current_price * 1.001]
   73  
   74          nearest_support    = max(supports)    if supports    else current_price * 0.97
   75          nearest_resistance = min(resistances) if resistances else current_price * 1.03
   76  
   77          support_score = min(5, sum(
   78              1 for l in swing_lows
   79              if abs(l - nearest_support) / nearest_support < 0.005
   80          ))
   81          resistance_score = min(5, sum(
   82              1 for h in swing_highs
   83              if abs(h - nearest_resistance) / nearest_resistance < 0.005
   84          ))
   85  
   86          return {
   87              "current_price":           current_price,
   88              "nearest_support":         round(nearest_support, 6),
   89              "nearest_resistance":      round(nearest_resistance, 6),
   90              "support_score":           support_score,
   91              "resistance_score":        resistance_score,
   92              "support_distance_pct":    round((current_price - nearest_support)    / current_price * 100, 2),
   93              "resistance_distance_pct": round((nearest_resistance - current_price) / current_price * 100, 2),
   94              "swing_highs":             sorted(swing_highs, reverse=True)[:3],
   95              "swing_lows":              sorted(swing_lows,  reverse=True)[:3],
   96          }
   97  
   98      # ── ATR-Based Stop Calculation ────────────────────────────────────────────
   99  
  100      def calculate_atr_stop(
  101          self,
  102          entry_price: float,
  103          atr: float,
  104          side: str,
  105          support: float = None,
  106          resistance: float = None,
  107      ) -> dict:
  108          """
  109          Calculate stop loss and take profit using ATR + support/resistance.
  110          Stop is placed 0.3% beyond the nearest technical level.
  111          Take profit = 2x the stop distance (1:2 minimum risk/reward).
  112          """
  113          if side == "long":
  114              if support and (entry_price - support) / entry_price < 0.04:
  115                  stop_price = support * 0.997
  116              else:
  117                  stop_price = entry_price - (1.0 * atr)
  118  
  119              stop_distance = entry_price - stop_price
  120              target_price  = entry_price + (2.0 * stop_distance)
  121              stop_pct      = round(stop_distance  / entry_price * 100, 2)
  122              target_pct    = round((target_price  - entry_price) / entry_price * 100, 2)
  123  
  124          else:  # short
  125              if resistance and (resistance - entry_price) / entry_price < 0.04:
  126                  stop_price = resistance * 1.003
  127              else:
  128                  stop_price = entry_price + (1.0 * atr)
  129  
  130              stop_distance = stop_price - entry_price
  131              target_price  = entry_price - (2.0 * stop_distance)
  132              stop_pct      = round(stop_distance  / entry_price * 100, 2)
  133              target_pct    = round((entry_price   - target_price) / entry_price * 100, 2)
  134  
  135          return {
  136              "entry":       round(entry_price, 6),
  137              "stop":        round(stop_price,  6),
  138              "target":      round(target_price, 6),
  139              "stop_pct":    stop_pct,
  140              "target_pct":  target_pct,
  141              "risk_reward": round(target_pct / stop_pct, 2) if stop_pct > 0 else 0,
  142              "atr":         round(atr, 6),
  143          }
  144  
  145      # ── Candlestick Patterns ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
  146  
  147      def detect_candlestick_patterns(
  148          self,
  149          opens: list,
  150          highs: list,
  151          lows: list,
  152          closes: list,
  153          volumes: list = None
  154      ) -> dict:
  155          """
  156          Detect the 5 most important single-candle patterns + 2 multi-candle patterns.
  157          Returns detected patterns with score adjustments.
  158          """
  159          if len(closes) < 3:
  160              return {"patterns": [], "score_adjustment": 0}
  161  
  162          patterns  = []
  163          score_adj = 0
  164  
  165          o, h, l, c = opens[-1], highs[-1], lows[-1], closes[-1]
  166          body         = abs(c - o)
  167          upper_wick   = h - max(o, c)
  168          lower_wick   = min(o, c) - l
  169          candle_range = h - l
  170  
  171          if candle_range == 0:
  172              return {"patterns": [], "score_adjustment": 0}
  173  
  174          # ── Hammer ──
  175          if (lower_wick >= 2 * body and
  176                  upper_wick <= body * 0.3 and
  177                  c > o and body > 0):
  178              patterns.append({
  179                  "name": "HAMMER", "direction": "bullish", "score_adj": +15,
  180                  "note": "Strong reversal signal — buyers absorbed selling pressure"
  181              })
  182              score_adj += 15
  183  
  184          # ── Shooting Star ──
  185          elif (upper_wick >= 2 * body and
  186                lower_wick <= body * 0.3 and
  187                c < o and body > 0):
  188              patterns.append({
  189                  "name": "SHOOTING_STAR", "direction": "bearish", "score_adj": -15,
  190                  "note": "Strong reversal signal — sellers overwhelmed buyers"
  191              })
  192              score_adj -= 15
  193  
  194          # ── Doji ──
  195          elif body <= candle_range * 0.1:
  196              patterns.append({
  197                  "name": "DOJI", "direction": "neutral", "score_adj": -5,
  198                  "note": "Indecision — wait for next candle confirmation"
  199              })
  200              score_adj -= 5
  201  
  202          # ── Pin Bar ──
  203          elif (lower_wick >= 3 * body or upper_wick >= 3 * body):
  204              direction = "bullish" if lower_wick >= 3 * body else "bearish"
  205              adj = +20 if direction == "bullish" else -20
  206              patterns.append({
  207                  "name": "PIN_BAR", "direction": direction, "score_adj": adj,
  208                  "note": "Strong price rejection — trade opposite to the long wick"
  209              })
  210              score_adj += adj
  211  
  212          # ── Bullish Engulfing ──
  213          if (len(closes) >= 2 and
  214                  opens[-2] > closes[-2] and
  215                  c > o and
  216                  o < closes[-2] and
  217                  c > opens[-2]):
  218              patterns.append({
  219                  "name": "BULLISH_ENGULFING", "direction": "bullish", "score_adj": +20,
  220                  "note": "Buyers completely absorbed previous sellers — strong reversal"
  221              })
  222              score_adj += 20
  223  
  224          # ── Bearish Engulfing ──
  225          elif (len(closes) >= 2 and
  226                closes[-2] > opens[-2] and
  227                c < o and
  228                o > closes[-2] and
  229                c < opens[-2]):
  230              patterns.append({
  231                  "name": "BEARISH_ENGULFING", "direction": "bearish", "score_adj": -20,
  232                  "note": "Sellers completely absorbed previous buyers — strong reversal"
  233              })
  234              score_adj -= 20
  235  
  236          # ── Three White Soldiers ──
  237          if (len(closes) >= 3 and
  238                  closes[-1] > closes[-2] > closes[-3] and
  239                  opens[-1]  > opens[-2]  > opens[-3]  and
  240                  closes[-1] > opens[-1] and
  241                  closes[-2] > opens[-2] and
  242                  closes[-3] > opens[-3]):
  243              patterns.append({
  244                  "name": "THREE_WHITE_SOLDIERS", "direction": "bullish", "score_adj": +25,
  245                  "note": "Strong momentum continuation — three consecutive green candles"
  246              })
  247              score_adj += 25
  248  
  249          # ── Three Black Crows ──
  250          elif (len(closes) >= 3 and
  251                closes[-1] < closes[-2] < closes[-3] and
  252                opens[-1]  < opens[-2]  < opens[-3]  and
  253                closes[-1] < opens[-1] and
  254                closes[-2] < opens[-2] and
  255                closes[-3] < opens[-3]):
  256              patterns.append({
  257                  "name": "THREE_BLACK_CROWS", "direction": "bearish", "score_adj": -25,
  258                  "note": "Strong bearish momentum — three consecutive red candles"
  259              })
  260              score_adj -= 25
  261  
  262          # Volume confirmation boost
  263          if volumes and len(volumes) >= 2:
  264              avg_vol = sum(volumes[-10:]) / len(volumes[-10:]) if len(volumes) >= 10 else volumes[-1]
  265              if volumes[-1] > avg_vol * 1.5 and patterns:
  266                  patterns[-1]["note"] += " (VOLUME CONFIRMED ✅)"
  267                  score_adj += 10
  268              elif volumes[-1] < avg_vol * 0.7 and patterns:
  269                  patterns[-1]["note"] += " (low volume — less reliable ⚠️)"
  270                  score_adj -= 5
  271  
  272          return {
  273              "patterns":      patterns,
  274              "score_adjustment": score_adj,
  275              "latest_candle": {
  276                  "open": o, "high": h, "low": l, "close": c,
  277                  "body_pct":  round(body / candle_range * 100, 1),
  278                  "direction": "green" if c >= o else "red"
  279              }
  280          }
  281  
  282      # ── Chart Pattern Detection ───────────────────────────────────────────────
  283  
  284      def detect_chart_patterns(
  285          self,
  286          closes: list,
  287          highs: list,
  288          lows: list,
  289          volumes: list = None,
  290          lookback: int = 30
  291      ) -> dict:
  292          """
  293          Detect Bull/Bear Flag and Double Top/Bottom patterns.
  294          """
  295          if len(closes) < lookback:
  296              return {"patterns": [], "score_adjustment": 0}
  297  
  298          patterns  = []
  299          score_adj = 0
  300  
  301          recent_closes = closes[-lookback:]
  302          recent_highs  = highs[-lookback:]
  303          recent_lows   = lows[-lookback:]
  304          mid           = lookback // 2
  305  
  306          first_half_change  = (recent_closes[mid] - recent_closes[0])  / recent_closes[0]  * 100
  307          second_half_change = (recent_closes[-1]  - recent_closes[mid]) / recent_closes[mid] * 100
  308  
  309          # ── Bull Flag ──
  310          if first_half_change > 5 and -3 < second_half_change < 1:
  311              patterns.append({
  312                  "name": "BULL_FLAG", "direction": "bullish", "score_adj": +20,
  313                  "note":       f"Bull flag: +{first_half_change:.1f}% flagpole then consolidation. Breakout imminent.",
  314                  "entry":      "Break above flag high with volume",
  315                  "target_pct": f"+{first_half_change:.0f}% (flagpole height)"
  316              })
  317              score_adj += 20
  318  
  319          # ── Bear Flag ──
  320          elif first_half_change < -5 and -1 < second_half_change < 3:
  321              patterns.append({
  322                  "name": "BEAR_FLAG", "direction": "bearish", "score_adj": -20,
  323                  "note":       f"Bear flag: {first_half_change:.1f}% drop then weak bounce. Breakdown imminent.",
  324                  "entry":      "Break below flag low with volume",
  325                  "target_pct": f"{first_half_change:.0f}% (flagpole height)"
  326              })
  327              score_adj -= 20
  328  
  329          # ── Double Top ──
  330          if len(recent_highs) >= 20:
  331              top1_idx = recent_highs.index(max(recent_highs[:mid]))
  332              top2_idx = mid + recent_highs[mid:].index(max(recent_highs[mid:]))
  333              top1, top2 = recent_highs[top1_idx], recent_highs[top2_idx]
  334  
  335              if (abs(top1 - top2) / top1 < 0.02 and
  336                      top1_idx != top2_idx and
  337                      recent_closes[-1] < top2 * 0.98):
  338                  valley = min(recent_closes[top1_idx:top2_idx]) if top1_idx < top2_idx else 0
  339                  patterns.append({
  340                      "name": "DOUBLE_TOP", "direction": "bearish", "score_adj": -25,
  341                      "note":  f"Double top at ~${top1:.2f}. Price failing to break resistance twice.",
  342                      "entry": f"Short on break below ${valley:.2f}",
  343                  })
  344                  score_adj -= 25
  345  
  346          # ── Double Bottom ──
  347          if len(recent_lows) >= 20:
  348              bot1_idx = recent_lows.index(min(recent_lows[:mid]))
  349              bot2_idx = mid + recent_lows[mid:].index(min(recent_lows[mid:]))
  350              bot1, bot2 = recent_lows[bot1_idx], recent_lows[bot2_idx]
  351  
  352              if (abs(bot1 - bot2) / bot1 < 0.02 and
  353                      bot1_idx != bot2_idx and
  354                      recent_closes[-1] > bot2 * 1.02):
  355                  peak = max(recent_closes[bot1_idx:bot2_idx]) if bot1_idx < bot2_idx else 0
  356                  patterns.append({
  357                      "name": "DOUBLE_BOTTOM", "direction": "bullish", "score_adj": +25,
  358                      "note":  f"Double bottom at ~${bot1:.2f}. Strong support held twice.",
  359                      "entry": f"Long on break above ${peak:.2f}",
  360                  })
  361                  score_adj += 25
  362  
  363          return {"patterns": patterns, "score_adjustment": score_adj}
  364  
  365      # ── Volume Analysis ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  366  
  367      def analyze_volume(self, volumes: list, period: int = 20) -> dict:
  368          """
  369          Analyze volume relative to average.
  370          Returns confirmation signal and score adjustment.
  371          """
  372          if not volumes or len(volumes) < 5:
  373              return {"signal": "unknown", "score_adjustment": 0, "ratio": 1.0}
  374  
  375          avg_vol     = sum(volumes[-period:]) / min(period, len(volumes))
  376          current_vol = volumes[-1]
  377          ratio       = round(current_vol / avg_vol, 2) if avg_vol > 0 else 1.0
  378  
  379          if ratio >= 3.0:
  380              return {
  381                  "signal": "climax_volume", "score_adjustment": 0, "ratio": ratio,
  382                  "note": f"⚡ CLIMAX VOLUME ({ratio:.1f}x avg) — potential exhaustion/reversal, not continuation"
  383              }
  384          elif ratio >= 1.5:
  385              return {
  386                  "signal": "high_volume", "score_adjustment": +15, "ratio": ratio,
  387                  "note": f"✅ High volume confirmation ({ratio:.1f}x avg)"
  388              }
  389          elif ratio < 0.7:
  390              return {
  391                  "signal": "low_volume", "score_adjustment": -10, "ratio": ratio,
  392                  "note": f"⚠️ Low volume ({ratio:.1f}x avg) — signal less reliable"
  393              }
  394          else:
  395              return {
  396                  "signal": "normal_volume", "score_adjustment": 0, "ratio": ratio,
  397                  "note": f"Volume normal ({ratio:.1f}x avg)"
  398              }
  399  
  400      # ── Master Context Builder ────────────────────────────────────────────────
  401  
  402      def build_geometry_context(
  403          self,
  404          symbol: str,
  405          opens: list,
  406          highs: list,
  407          lows: list,
  408          closes: list,
  409          volumes: list = None,
  410          side: str = "long"
  411      ) -> dict:
  412          """
  413          Master function — runs all geometric analysis and returns:
  414          - Combined score adjustment
  415          - ATR-based stop/target levels
  416          - Full context string for Claude's prompt
  417          """
  418          if len(closes) < 10:
  419              return {
  420                  "context":          "Insufficient price history for geometric analysis",
  421                  "score_adjustment": 0,
  422                  "stop_loss":        None,
  423                  "take_profit":      None,
  424              }
  425  
  426          atr           = self.calculate_atr(highs, lows, closes)
  427          current_price = closes[-1]
  428          atr_pct       = round(atr / current_price * 100, 3) if current_price > 0 else 0
  429  
  430          sr      = self.find_support_resistance(closes, highs, lows)
  431          candles = self.detect_candlestick_patterns(opens, highs, lows, closes, volumes)
  432          charts  = self.detect_chart_patterns(closes, highs, lows, volumes)
  433          vol     = (
  434              self.analyze_volume(volumes)
  435              if volumes
  436              else {"signal": "unknown", "score_adjustment": 0, "ratio": 1.0}
  437          )
  438  
  439          stops = self.calculate_atr_stop(
  440              entry_price=current_price,
  441              atr=atr,
  442              side=side,
  443              support=sr["nearest_support"]    if side == "long"  else None,
  444              resistance=sr["nearest_resistance"] if side == "short" else None,
  445          )
  446  
  447          total_score_adj = (
  448              candles["score_adjustment"] +
  449              charts["score_adjustment"]  +
  450              vol["score_adjustment"]
  451          )
  452  
  453          if side == "long"  and sr["support_score"]    >= 3:
  454              total_score_adj += 15
  455          elif side == "short" and sr["resistance_score"] >= 3:
  456              total_score_adj += 15
  457  
  458          lines = [f"=== GEOMETRIC ANALYSIS: {symbol} ==="]
  459          lines.append(f"Price: ${current_price:.4f} | ATR: ${atr:.4f} ({atr_pct:.2f}%)")
  460          lines.append(
  461              f"Support: ${sr['nearest_support']:.4f} (-{sr['support_distance_pct']:.2f}%) "
  462              f"score={sr['support_score']}/5"
  463          )
  464          lines.append(
  465              f"Resistance: ${sr['nearest_resistance']:.4f} (+{sr['resistance_distance_pct']:.2f}%) "
  466              f"score={sr['resistance_score']}/5"
  467          )
  468  
  469          if candles["patterns"]:
  470              for p in candles["patterns"]:
  471                  emoji = "🟢" if p["direction"] == "bullish" else "🔴" if p["direction"] == "bearish" else "⚪"
  472                  lines.append(f"Candle: {emoji} {p['name']} — {p['note']}")
  473          else:
  474              lines.append("Candle: No significant pattern detected")
  475  
  476          if charts["patterns"]:
  477              for p in charts["patterns"]:
  478                  emoji = "🟢" if p["direction"] == "bullish" else "🔴"
  479                  lines.append(f"Chart: {emoji} {p['name']} — {p['note']}")
  480  
  481          lines.append(f"Volume: {vol.get('note', 'N/A')}")
  482          lines.append(
  483              f"ATR Stop ({side.upper()}): entry=${stops['entry']:.4f} | "
  484              f"stop=${stops['stop']:.4f} (-{stops['stop_pct']:.2f}%) | "
  485              f"target=${stops['target']:.4f} (+{stops['target_pct']:.2f}%) | "
  486              f"R:R={stops['risk_reward']:.1f}x"
  487          )
  488          lines.append(f"Geometry score adjustment: {total_score_adj:+d}")
  489  
  490          return {
  491              "context":           "\n".join(lines),
  492              "score_adjustment":  total_score_adj,
  493              "stop_loss":         stops["stop"],
  494              "take_profit":       stops["target"],
  495              "stop_pct":          stops["stop_pct"],
  496              "target_pct":        stops["target_pct"],
  497              "risk_reward":       stops["risk_reward"],
  498              "atr":               atr,
  499              "support":           sr["nearest_support"],
  500              "resistance":        sr["nearest_resistance"],
  501              "patterns_detected": [p["name"] for p in candles["patterns"] + charts["patterns"]],
  502          }

    1  import { Router, type IRouter } from "express";
    2  import { existsSync } from "fs";
    3  import Database from "better-sqlite3";
    4  
    5  const router: IRouter = Router();
    6  
    7  const DB_PATH =
    8    process.env["TRADING_DB_PATH"] ??
    9    "/home/runner/workspace/trading-agent/trading_memory.db";
   10  
   11  function getDb(): Database.Database | null {
   12    if (!existsSync(DB_PATH)) {
   13      console.warn("[trading] DB not found at:", DB_PATH);
   14      return null;
   15    }
   16    try {
   17      return new Database(DB_PATH, { readonly: true });
   18    } catch (e) {
   19      console.error("[trading] Failed to open DB:", e);
   20      return null;
   21    }
   22  }
   23  
   24  router.get("/status", (_req, res) => {
   25    const db = getDb();
   26    let trades: unknown[] = [];
   27    let stats = { total_trades: 0, db_connected: false };
   28  
   29    if (db) {
   30      try {
   31        trades = db
   32          .prepare(
   33            `SELECT symbol, side as action, entry_price as price, qty,
   34             entry_at as timestamp, pnl, status, close_reason
   35             FROM trades ORDER BY entry_at DESC LIMIT 50`,
   36          )
   37          .all();
   38        const row = db
   39          .prepare("SELECT COUNT(*) as count FROM trades")
   40          .get() as { count: number };
   41        stats = { total_trades: row.count, db_connected: true };
   42        db.close();
   43      } catch (e) {
   44        console.error("[trading] status query error:", e);
   45        try { db.close(); } catch { /* ignore */ }
   46      }
   47    }
   48  
   49    res.json({
   50      agent: "running",
   51      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
   52      db_connected: stats.db_connected,
   53      total_trades: stats.total_trades,
   54      recent_trades: trades,
   55    });
   56  });
   57  
   58  router.get("/decisions", (_req, res) => {
   59    const db = getDb();
   60    let decisions: unknown[] = [];
   61    let connected = false;
   62  
   63    if (db) {
   64      try {
   65        decisions = db
   66          .prepare(
   67            `SELECT symbol, decision, confidence, reasoning, market_data, decided_at
   68             FROM agent_decisions
   69             ORDER BY decided_at DESC LIMIT 60`,
   70          )
   71          .all();
   72        connected = true;
   73        db.close();
   74      } catch (e) {
   75        console.error("[trading] decisions query error:", e);
   76        try { db.close(); } catch { /* ignore */ }
   77      }
   78    }
   79  
   80    res.json({ db_connected: connected, decisions });
   81  });
   82  
   83  router.get("/partial-profits", (_req, res) => {
   84    const db = getDb();
   85    if (!db) {
   86      res.json({ partial_profits: {} });
   87      return;
   88    }
   89    try {
   90      const rows = db
   91        .prepare(
   92          `SELECT symbol, SUM(ABS(pnl)) as secured_pnl, COUNT(*) as count
   93           FROM trades
   94           WHERE close_reason = 'partial_profit' AND pnl IS NOT NULL
   95           GROUP BY symbol`,
   96        )
   97        .all() as { symbol: string; secured_pnl: number; count: number }[];
   98      const result: Record<string, { secured_pnl: number; count: number }> = {};
   99      rows.forEach(r => { result[r.symbol] = { secured_pnl: r.secured_pnl, count: r.count }; });
  100      db.close();
  101      res.json({ partial_profits: result });
  102    } catch (e) {
  103      console.error("[trading] partial-profits query error:", e);
  104      try { db.close(); } catch { /* ignore */ }
  105      res.json({ partial_profits: {} });
  106    }
  107  });
  108  
  109  const ALPACA_BASE = "https://paper-api.alpaca.markets";
  110  const ALPACA_KEY  = process.env["ALPACA_API_KEY"]  ?? "";
  111  const ALPACA_SEC  = process.env["ALPACA_SECRET_KEY"] ?? "";
  112  
  113  router.get("/positions", async (_req, res) => {
  114    try {
  115      const r = await fetch(`${ALPACA_BASE}/v2/positions`, {
  116        headers: {
  117          "APCA-API-KEY-ID":     ALPACA_KEY,
  118          "APCA-API-SECRET-KEY": ALPACA_SEC,
  119        },
  120      });
  121      if (!r.ok) {
  122        res.json({ positions: [], error: `Alpaca HTTP ${r.status}` });
  123        return;
  124      }
  125      const raw = (await r.json()) as Record<string, string>[];
  126      const positions = raw.map(p => ({
  127        symbol:          p.symbol,
  128        side:            p.side,
  129        qty:             parseFloat(p.qty),
  130        entry_price:     parseFloat(p.avg_entry_price),
  131        current_price:   parseFloat(p.current_price),
  132        market_value:    parseFloat(p.market_value),
  133        unrealized_pl:   parseFloat(p.unrealized_pl),
  134        unrealized_plpc: parseFloat(p.unrealized_plpc) * 100,
  135        cost_basis:      parseFloat(p.cost_basis),
  136      }));
  137      res.json({ positions });
  138    } catch (err) {
  139      res.json({ positions: [], error: String(err) });
  140    }
  141  });
  142  
  143  const FLASK_BASE = "http://localhost:5000";
  144  
  145  async function proxyFlask(url: string, fallback: unknown) {
  146    try {
  147      const r = await fetch(url);
  148      if (!r.ok) return fallback;
  149      return await r.json();
  150    } catch {
  151      return fallback;
  152    }
  153  }
  154  
  155  router.get("/movers", async (_req, res) => {
  156    res.json(await proxyFlask(`${FLASK_BASE}/api/movers`, { movers: [], error: "scanner unavailable" }));
  157  });
  158  
  159  router.get("/sentiment", async (_req, res) => {
  160    res.json(await proxyFlask(`${FLASK_BASE}/api/sentiment`, { sentiment: "neutral", score: 0, headlines: [], alerts: [] }));
  161  });
  162  
  163  router.get("/calendar", async (_req, res) => {
  164    res.json(await proxyFlask(`${FLASK_BASE}/api/calendar`, { event: null, note: "" }));
  165  });
  166  
  167  router.get("/stats", async (_req, res) => {
  168    res.json(await proxyFlask(`${FLASK_BASE}/api/stats`, {
  169      total_trades: 0, win_rate: 0, profit_factor: 0,
  170      total_pnl: 0, max_drawdown: 0, best_asset: null, asset_pnl: {}
  171    }));
  172  });
  173  
  174  router.get("/regime", async (_req, res) => {
  175    res.json(await proxyFlask(`${FLASK_BASE}/api/regime`, { regime: "UNKNOWN" }));
  176  });
  177  
  178  router.get("/stops", async (_req, res) => {
  179    res.json(await proxyFlask(`${FLASK_BASE}/api/stops`, { stops: {} }));
  180  });
  181  
  182  router.get("/account", async (_req, res) => {
  183    res.json(await proxyFlask(`${FLASK_BASE}/api/account`, {
  184      equity: 0, cash: 0, buying_power: 0, portfolio_value: 0, last_equity: 0
  185    }));
  186  });
  187  
  188  router.get("/closed-today", async (req, res) => {
  189    const period = (req.query.period as string) || "today";
  190    res.json(await proxyFlask(`${FLASK_BASE}/api/closed-today?period=${period}`, { closed: [], date: "" }));
  191  });
  192  
  193  router.get("/analysis", async (_req, res) => {
  194    res.json(await proxyFlask(`${FLASK_BASE}/api/analysis`, {}));

    1  import { useEffect, useState, useCallback } from "react";
