   24  // ── Interfaces ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   25  interface Trade {
   26    symbol: string; action: string; price: number; qty: number;
   27    timestamp: string; pnl: number | null; status: string; close_reason: string | null;
   28  }
   29  interface Decision {
   30    symbol: string; decision: string; confidence: number;
   31    reasoning: string; market_data?: string; decided_at: string;
   32  }
   33  interface Status {
   34    agent: string; timestamp: string; db_connected: boolean;
   35    total_trades: number; recent_trades: Trade[];
   36  }
   37  interface Position {
   38    symbol: string; side: string; qty: number;
   39    entry_price: number; current_price: number;
   40    market_value: number; unrealized_pl: number; unrealized_plpc: number;
   41    cost_basis: number;
   42  }
   43  interface Mover { symbol: string; price: number; change_pct: number; direction: "up" | "down"; }
   44  interface SentimentResponse { sentiment: string; score: number; headlines?: string[]; alerts?: string[]; ts?: string; }
   45  interface RegimeResponse { regime: string; params?: Record<string, unknown>; context?: string; }
   46  interface StatsResponse {
   47    total_trades: number; win_rate: number; profit_factor: number;
   48    total_pnl: number; max_drawdown: number; best_asset: string | null; asset_pnl: Record<string, number>;
   49  }
   50  interface PartialProfits { [symbol: string]: { secured_pnl: number; count: number } }
   51  interface Stops { [symbol: string]: number }
   52  interface AccountResponse {
   53    equity: number; cash: number; buying_power: number;
   54    portfolio_value: number; last_equity: number;
   55  }
   56  interface ClosedTodayItem {
   57    symbol: string; pnl: number; trade_count: number;
   58    qty_sold: number; last_exit: string; reasons: string;
   59  }
   60  
   61  type Page = "HOME" | "MARKET" | "SIGNALS" | "TRADES" | "ANALYSIS";
   62  type ClosedPeriod = "today" | "week" | "month" | "ytd" | "all";
   63  
   64  interface AnalysisData {
   65    total_trades: number; winning_trades: number; losing_trades: number;
   66    win_rate: number; profit_factor: number; expectancy: number;
   67    gross_win: number; gross_loss: number; total_pnl: number;
   68    avg_win: number; avg_loss: number; avg_hold_min: number;
   69    avg_trades_per_day: number;
   70    best_trade:  { symbol: string; pnl: number; reason: string } | null;
   71    worst_trade: { symbol: string; pnl: number; reason: string } | null;
   72    current_streak: { type: string; count: number } | null;
   73    max_win_streak: number; max_loss_streak: number;
   74    daily_pnl: { date: string; pnl: number; trades: number }[];
   75    by_asset:  { symbol: string; pnl: number; trades: number; avg_pnl: number; avg_hold_min: number }[];
   76    by_reason: { reason: string; trades: number; pnl: number }[];
   77  }
   78  
   79  // ── Helpers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   80  function fmtTime(s: string) {
   81    const d = new Date(s.includes("T") ? s : s.replace(" ", "T") + "Z");
   82    return d.toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: "2-digit", minute: "2-digit" });
   83  }
   84  function fmtDateTime(s: string) {
   85    const d = new Date(s.includes("T") ? s : s.replace(" ", "T") + "Z");
   86    return d.toLocaleString([], { month: "short", day: "numeric", hour: "2-digit", minute: "2-digit" });
   87  }
   88  function fmtPrice(n: number) {
   89    if (n >= 1000) return n.toLocaleString("en-US", { minimumFractionDigits: 2, maximumFractionDigits: 2 });
   90    if (n >= 1)    return n.toFixed(2);
   91    return n.toFixed(4);
   92  }
   93  function fmtPnl(n: number) {
   94    const abs = Math.abs(n);
   95    const str = abs >= 1 ? abs.toFixed(2) : abs >= 0.01 ? abs.toFixed(3) : abs.toFixed(4);
   96    return (n >= 0 ? "+" : "-") + "$" + str;
   97  }
   98  function fmtPct(n: number) { return (n >= 0 ? "+" : "") + n.toFixed(2) + "%"; }
   99  function daysUntil(dateStr: string) {
  100    const diff = Math.round((new Date(dateStr + "T12:00:00Z").getTime() - Date.now()) / 86400_000);
  101    if (diff < 0)   return `${Math.abs(diff)}d ago`;
  102    if (diff === 0) return "today";
  103    if (diff === 1) return "tomorrow";
  104    return `in ${diff}d`;
  105  }
  106  
  107  function inferHeadlineTier(text: string): 1 | 2 | 3 {
  108    const t = text.toLowerCase();
  109    const t1 = ["fed rate cut", "rate hike", "bank failure", "default", "war declaration", "nuclear", "circuit breaker", "flash crash", "cpi beat", "jobs miss", "gdp miss", "recession"];
  110    const t2 = ["fed dovish", "fed hawkish", "tariff", "trade war", "earnings", "guidance", "layoffs", "bankruptcy", "sec investigation", "fed pivot", "rate cut"];
  111    if (t1.some(k => t.includes(k))) return 1;
  112    if (t2.some(k => t.includes(k))) return 2;
  113    return 3;
  114  }
  115  
  116  function parseSynthesisBreakdown(reasoning: string) {
  117    const m = reasoning.match(/Breakdown: Base: (-?\d+) \| Regime: ([+-]?\d+) \| RelStr: ([+-]?\d+) \| DXY: ([+-]?\d+) \| Corr: ([+-]?\d+) \| Geo: ([+-]?\d+) \| News: ([+-]?\d+) \| FINAL: (\d+)/);
  118    if (!m) return null;
  119    return { base: +m[1], regime: +m[2], relStr: +m[3], dxy: +m[4], corr: +m[5], geo: +m[6], news: +m[7], final: +m[8] };
  120  }
  121  
  122  function parseRegimeFromReasoning(reasoning: string): string {
  123    const m = reasoning.match(/\b(BEAR_MARKET|BULL_MARKET|CHOPPY|TRENDING_BULL|TRENDING_BEAR|VOLATILE)\b/);
  124    if (m) return m[1].replace("_MARKET", "").replace("TRENDING_", "TRENDING ");
  125    if (reasoning.toLowerCase().includes("bear")) return "BEAR";
  126    if (reasoning.toLowerCase().includes("bull")) return "BULL";
  127    return "—";
  128  }
  129  
  130  function parsePatternsFromMarketData(md?: string): string[] {
  131    if (!md) return [];
  132    try {
  133      const parsed = JSON.parse(md);
  134      return (parsed.patterns_detected ?? parsed.patterns ?? []) as string[];
  135    } catch { return []; }
  136  }
  137  
  138  function regimeBadgeStyle(regime: string): { bg: string; text: string; emoji: string } {
  139    const r = regime.toUpperCase();
  140    if (r.includes("BEAR")) return { bg: "bg-red-900/60 border-red-700",   text: "text-red-400",   emoji: "🔴" };
  141    if (r.includes("BULL")) return { bg: "bg-emerald-900/60 border-emerald-700", text: "text-emerald-400", emoji: "🟢" };
  142    return { bg: "bg-yellow-900/60 border-yellow-700", text: "text-yellow-400", emoji: "🟡" };
  143  }
  144  
  145  // ── Shared Small Components ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
  146  function DecisionBadge({ decision }: { decision: string }) {
  147    const d = decision.toUpperCase();
  148    const cls = d === "BUY"  ? "bg-emerald-900/70 text-emerald-400 border-emerald-700" :
  149                d === "SELL" ? "bg-red-900/70 text-red-400 border-red-700" :
  150                               "bg-slate-700/70 text-slate-400 border-slate-600";
  151    return <span className={`inline-block px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-xs font-bold border ${cls}`}>{d}</span>;
  152  }
  153  
  154  function TierBadge({ tier }: { tier: 1 | 2 | 3 }) {
  155    const cls = tier === 1 ? "bg-red-900/60 text-red-400 border-red-700" :
  156                tier === 2 ? "bg-amber-900/60 text-amber-400 border-amber-700" :
  157                             "bg-slate-700/60 text-slate-500 border-slate-600";
  158    return <span className={`text-[9px] font-bold border rounded px-1 py-0 ${cls}`}>T{tier}</span>;
  159  }
  160  
  161  function SideBadge({ side }: { side: string }) {
  162    const isLong = side.toLowerCase() === "long" || side.toLowerCase() === "buy";
  163    return (
  164      <span className={`text-[10px] font-bold px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded border ${isLong ? "bg-emerald-900/50 text-emerald-400 border-emerald-700" : "bg-red-900/50 text-red-400 border-red-700"}`}>
  165        {isLong ? "LONG" : "SHORT"}
  166      </span>
  167    );
  168  }

  170  // ── Top Navigation Bar ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  171  function TopNav({ activePage, setActivePage, regime, portfolioValue, portfolioDelta, positionsCount, lastRefresh, error }: {
  172    activePage: Page; setActivePage: (p: Page) => void;
  173    regime: string; portfolioValue: number; portfolioDelta: number;
  174    positionsCount: number; lastRefresh: Date; error: boolean;
  175  }) {
  176    const rb   = regimeBadgeStyle(regime);
  177    const tabs: Page[] = ["HOME", "MARKET", "SIGNALS", "TRADES", "ANALYSIS"];
  178    const pPos = portfolioDelta >= 0;
  179  
  180    return (
  181      <nav className="fixed top-0 left-0 right-0 z-50 bg-slate-900/95 backdrop-blur-sm border-b border-slate-800 h-14 flex items-center px-3 gap-2 sm:gap-4">
  182        {/* Brand */}
  183        <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 flex-shrink-0">
  184          <span className="text-sky-400 font-bold text-sm sm:text-base">⚡ Jim Bot</span>
  185          <span className={`hidden sm:inline-flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] font-bold px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded border ${rb.bg} ${rb.text}`}>
  186            {rb.emoji} {regime === "UNKNOWN" ? "—" : regime.replace("_MARKET","").replace("TRENDING_","")}
  187          </span>
  188        </div>
  189  
  190        {/* Portfolio value */}
  191        <div className="flex-shrink-0 hidden sm:block">
  192          <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-600 leading-none">Portfolio</div>
  193          <div className={`text-sm font-bold leading-tight ${pPos ? "text-emerald-400" : "text-red-400"}`}>
  194            ${portfolioValue.toFixed(0)}
  195            <span className="text-[10px] font-semibold ml-1 opacity-80">({fmtPct(portfolioDelta)})</span>
  196          </div>
  197        </div>
  198  
  199        {/* Mobile portfolio */}
  200        <div className={`flex-shrink-0 sm:hidden text-sm font-bold ${pPos ? "text-emerald-400" : "text-red-400"}`}>
  201          ${portfolioValue.toFixed(0)}
  202        </div>
  203  
  204        {/* Tabs */}
  205        <div className="flex items-center gap-0 flex-1 justify-center">
  206          {tabs.map(tab => (
  207            <button
  208              key={tab}
  209              onClick={() => setActivePage(tab)}
  210              className={`px-2 sm:px-4 py-1.5 text-xs sm:text-sm font-semibold rounded transition-colors ${activePage === tab ? "bg-sky-600/20 text-sky-400" : "text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-300"}`}
  211            >
  212              {tab}
  213            </button>
  214          ))}
  215        </div>
  216  
  217        {/* Right info */}
  218        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-shrink-0 text-right">
  219          <div className="hidden sm:flex items-center gap-1.5">
  220            <span className="text-[10px] text-slate-600">{positionsCount} pos</span>
  221            <span className={`w-2 h-2 rounded-full ${error ? "bg-red-400" : "bg-emerald-400"}`} title={error ? "Error" : "Running"} />
  222          </div>
  223          <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-600 hidden sm:block">{lastRefresh.toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: "2-digit", minute: "2-digit" })}</div>
  224        </div>
  225      </nav>
  226    );
  227  }
