  229  // ── HOME PAGE ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  230  function PositionRow({ pos, decisions, partialProfits, stops, totalPortfolio }: {
  231    pos: Position; decisions: Decision[];
  232    partialProfits: PartialProfits; stops: Stops; totalPortfolio: number;
  233  }) {
  234    const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(false);
  235    const pnl     = pos.unrealized_pl;
  236    const pnlPct  = pos.unrealized_plpc;
  237    const isPos   = pnl >= 0;
  238    const secured = partialProfits[pos.symbol]?.secured_pnl ?? 0;
  239    const stopVal = stops[pos.symbol] ?? (pos.side === "long"
  240      ? pos.current_price * 0.95
  241      : pos.current_price * 1.03);
  242    const sizePct = (pos.cost_basis / Math.max(totalPortfolio, INITIAL_CAPITAL)) * 100;
  243    const latestDec = decisions.find(d => d.symbol === pos.symbol || d.symbol === pos.symbol.replace("/",""));
  244    const breakdown = latestDec ? parseSynthesisBreakdown(latestDec.reasoning) : null;
  245    const patterns  = latestDec ? parsePatternsFromMarketData(latestDec.market_data) : [];
  246    const ticker    = pos.symbol.replace("/USD","");
  247  
  248    return (
  249      <>
  250        <tr
  251          className={`border-l-2 cursor-pointer hover:bg-slate-800/60 transition-colors ${isPos ? "border-emerald-600/70" : "border-red-600/70"}`}
  252          onClick={() => setExpanded(v => !v)}
  253        >
  254          <td className="px-3 py-2.5">
  255            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
  256              <span className="font-bold text-white text-sm">{ticker}</span>
  257              <SideBadge side={pos.side} />
  258            </div>
  259          </td>
  260          <td className="px-3 py-2.5 text-xs text-slate-300 font-mono">${fmtPrice(pos.entry_price)}</td>
  261          <td className="px-3 py-2.5 text-xs text-slate-200 font-mono">${fmtPrice(pos.current_price)}</td>
  262          <td className="px-3 py-2.5">
  263            <div className={`text-xs font-bold ${isPos ? "text-emerald-400" : "text-red-400"}`}>{fmtPnl(pnl)}</div>
  264            <div className={`text-[10px] ${isPos ? "text-emerald-500" : "text-red-500"}`}>{fmtPct(pnlPct)}</div>
  265          </td>
  266          <td className="px-3 py-2.5">
  267            {secured > 0
  268              ? <span className="text-[10px] font-semibold bg-emerald-900/40 border border-emerald-700/50 text-emerald-400 rounded px-1.5 py-0.5">✅ +${secured.toFixed(2)}</span>
  269              : <span className="text-[10px] text-slate-700">—</span>}
  270          </td>
  271          <td className="px-3 py-2.5 text-xs font-mono text-amber-400">${fmtPrice(stopVal)}</td>
  272          <td className="px-3 py-2.5 text-xs text-slate-400">{sizePct.toFixed(1)}%</td>
  273          <td className="px-3 py-2.5 text-slate-600 text-xs">{expanded ? "▲" : "▼"}</td>
  274        </tr>
  275        {expanded && (
  276          <tr className={`border-l-2 ${isPos ? "border-emerald-600/40" : "border-red-600/40"}`}>
  277            <td colSpan={8} className="px-4 pb-4 pt-1 bg-slate-800/40">
  278              <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 gap-4 mt-2">
  279                {/* Position details */}
  280                <div className="space-y-2">
  281                  <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 uppercase tracking-wider font-semibold mb-1">Position Details</div>
  282                  {[
  283                    ["Qty",        pos.qty.toString()],
  284                    ["Cost Basis", "$" + fmtPrice(pos.cost_basis)],
  285                    ["Market Val", "$" + fmtPrice(pos.market_value)],
  286                    ["~Stop",      "$" + fmtPrice(stopVal)],
  287                    ["Size %",     sizePct.toFixed(1) + "% of portfolio"],
  288                  ].map(([k, v]) => (
  289                    <div key={k} className="flex justify-between text-xs">
  290                      <span className="text-slate-500">{k}</span>
  291                      <span className="text-slate-300 font-mono">{v}</span>
  292                    </div>
  293                  ))}
  294                  {patterns.length > 0 && (
  295                    <div className="flex items-center gap-1 flex-wrap mt-1">
  296                      {patterns.map(p => (
  297                        <span key={p} className="text-[9px] bg-violet-900/40 text-violet-400 border border-violet-700/50 rounded px-1.5 py-0.5">{p}</span>
  298                      ))}
  299                    </div>
  300                  )}
  301                </div>
  302                {/* Score breakdown + Claude reasoning */}
  303                <div>
  304                  {breakdown && (
  305                    <div className="mb-2">
  306                      <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 uppercase tracking-wider font-semibold mb-1">Synthesis Score</div>
  307                      <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-1">
  308                        {[
  309                          ["Base", breakdown.base],
  310                          ["Regime", breakdown.regime],
  311                          ["RelStr", breakdown.relStr],
  312                          ["DXY", breakdown.dxy],
  313                          ["Corr", breakdown.corr],
  314                          ["Geo", breakdown.geo],
  315                          ["News", breakdown.news],
  316                          ["FINAL", breakdown.final],
  317                        ].map(([label, val]) => (
  318                          <div key={label as string} className={`text-center rounded p-1 ${label === "FINAL" ? "bg-sky-900/40 col-span-2" : "bg-slate-800"}`}>
  319                            <div className="text-[8px] text-slate-600 uppercase">{label as string}</div>
  320                            <div className={`text-xs font-bold ${typeof val === "number" && val > 0 ? "text-emerald-400" : typeof val === "number" && val < 0 ? "text-red-400" : "text-slate-300"}`}>
  321                              {typeof val === "number" && label !== "Base" && label !== "FINAL" && val > 0 ? "+" : ""}{val}
  322                            </div>
  323                          </div>
  324                        ))}
  325                      </div>
  326                    </div>
  327                  )}
  328                  {latestDec && (
  329                    <div>
  330                      <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 uppercase tracking-wider font-semibold mb-1">
  331                        Claude — {fmtDateTime(latestDec.decided_at)}
  332                      </div>
  333                      <div className="bg-slate-900/60 rounded p-2 max-h-28 overflow-y-auto border-l-2 border-sky-700/40">
  334                        <p className="text-[10px] text-slate-400 leading-relaxed whitespace-pre-wrap">
  335                          {latestDec.reasoning.replace(/Breakdown:.*$/m, "").trim().slice(0, 400)}
  336                          {latestDec.reasoning.length > 400 ? "…" : ""}
  337                        </p>
  338                      </div>
  339                    </div>
  340                  )}
  341                </div>
  342              </div>
  343            </td>
  344          </tr>
  345        )}
  346      </>
  347    );
  348  }
  349  
  350  function ReasonBadge({ reasons }: { reasons: string }) {
  351    const r = reasons.toLowerCase();
  352    if (r.includes("partial"))  return <span className="text-[9px] bg-sky-900/40 text-sky-400 border border-sky-700/40 rounded px-1.5 py-0.5">partial</span>;
  353    if (r.includes("stop"))     return <span className="text-[9px] bg-red-900/40 text-red-400 border border-red-700/40 rounded px-1.5 py-0.5">stop</span>;
  354    if (r.includes("target"))   return <span className="text-[9px] bg-emerald-900/40 text-emerald-400 border border-emerald-700/40 rounded px-1.5 py-0.5">target</span>;
  355    return <span className="text-[9px] bg-slate-700/40 text-slate-500 border border-slate-600/40 rounded px-1.5 py-0.5">{reasons.split(",")[0]}</span>;
  356  }
  357  
  358  function EquityCurve({ data }: { data: { date: string; pnl: number }[] }) {
  359    if (data.length < 2) return null;
  360    let cum = 0;
  361    const points = data.map(d => { cum += d.pnl; return cum; });
  362    const maxV = Math.max(...points.map(Math.abs), 0.01);
  363    const W = 400; const H = 64;
  364    const xs = points.map((_, i) => (i / Math.max(points.length - 1, 1)) * W);
  365    const ys = points.map(p => H / 2 - (p / maxV) * (H / 2 - 5));
  366    const pathD = xs.map((x, i) => `${i === 0 ? "M" : "L"} ${x.toFixed(1)} ${ys[i].toFixed(1)}`).join(" ");
  367    const areaD = `${pathD} L ${W} ${H / 2} L 0 ${H / 2} Z`;
  368    const lastVal = points[points.length - 1];
  369    const col = lastVal >= 0 ? "#10b981" : "#ef4444";
  370    const gradId = `eq-${data.length}`;
  371    return (
  372      <svg viewBox={`0 0 ${W} ${H}`} width="100%" height={H} preserveAspectRatio="none">
  373        <defs>
  374          <linearGradient id={gradId} x1="0" y1="0" x2="0" y2="1">
  375            <stop offset="0%" stopColor={col} stopOpacity="0.25" />
  376            <stop offset="100%" stopColor={col} stopOpacity="0" />
  377          </linearGradient>
  378        </defs>
  379        <line x1={0} y1={H / 2} x2={W} y2={H / 2} stroke="#334155" strokeWidth="1" />
  380        <path d={areaD} fill={`url(#${gradId})`} />
  381        <path d={pathD} stroke={col} strokeWidth="1.5" fill="none" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round" />
  382        {xs.map((x, i) => (
  383          <circle key={i} cx={x} cy={ys[i]} r="2" fill={col} opacity="0.7" />
  384        ))}
  385      </svg>
  386    );
  387  }
  388  
  389  // ── ANALYSIS PAGE ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  390  function StatCard({ label, value, sub, color }: { label: string; value: string; sub?: string; color?: string }) {
  391    return (
  392      <div className="bg-slate-800 rounded-xl p-4 border border-slate-700/50">
  393        <div className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wider text-slate-500 font-semibold mb-1">{label}</div>
  394        <div className={`text-xl font-bold font-mono ${color ?? "text-white"}`}>{value}</div>
  395        {sub && <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-600 mt-0.5">{sub}</div>}
  396      </div>
  397    );
  398  }
  399  
  400  function AnalysisPage({ data }: { data: AnalysisData | null }) {
  401    if (!data || data.total_trades === 0) {
  402      return (
  403        <div className="p-6 flex items-center justify-center min-h-[300px]">
  404          <div className="text-slate-600 text-sm">No closed trades yet — analysis will appear once the first trade closes.</div>
  405        </div>
  406      );
  407    }
  408  
  409    const pfLabel   = data.profit_factor === 999 ? "∞" : data.profit_factor.toFixed(2);
  410    const exSign    = data.expectancy >= 0 ? "+" : "";
  411    const holdLabel = data.avg_hold_min >= 60
  412      ? `${(data.avg_hold_min / 60).toFixed(1)}h`
  413      : `${data.avg_hold_min.toFixed(0)}m`;
  414    const streakCol = data.current_streak?.type === "win" ? "text-emerald-400" : "text-red-400";
  415    const streakLbl = data.current_streak
  416      ? `${data.current_streak.count} ${data.current_streak.type} streak`
  417      : "—";
  418  
  419    const maxAssetPnl = Math.max(...data.by_asset.map(a => Math.abs(a.pnl)), 0.01);
  420  
  421    return (
  422      <div className="p-4 sm:p-6 space-y-6">
  423        <h2 className="text-base font-bold text-white">Performance Analysis</h2>
  424  
  425        {/* ── KPI Row 1 ─────────────────────────────────────────────── */}
  426        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-4 gap-3">
  427          <StatCard label="Win Rate"      value={`${data.win_rate.toFixed(1)}%`}
  428            sub={`${data.winning_trades}W / ${data.losing_trades}L`}
  429            color={data.win_rate >= 50 ? "text-emerald-400" : "text-red-400"} />
  430          <StatCard label="Profit Factor" value={pfLabel}
  431            sub={`Gross win $${data.gross_win.toFixed(2)}`}
  432            color={data.profit_factor >= 1 ? "text-emerald-400" : "text-red-400"} />
  433          <StatCard label="Expectancy"    value={`${exSign}$${data.expectancy.toFixed(4)}`}
  434            sub="avg $ per trade"
  435            color={data.expectancy >= 0 ? "text-sky-400" : "text-red-400"} />
  436          <StatCard label="Avg Hold"      value={holdLabel}
  437            sub={`${data.avg_trades_per_day.toFixed(1)} trades/day`} />
  438        </div>
  439  
  440        {/* ── KPI Row 2 ─────────────────────────────────────────────── */}
  441        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-4 gap-3">
  442          <StatCard label="Total Trades"  value={`${data.total_trades}`}
  443            sub={`${data.avg_trades_per_day.toFixed(1)} per active day`} />
  444          <StatCard label="Best Trade"
  445            value={data.best_trade ? `+$${data.best_trade.pnl.toFixed(4)}` : "—"}
  446            sub={data.best_trade?.symbol}  color="text-emerald-400" />
  447          <StatCard label="Worst Trade"
  448            value={data.worst_trade ? `$${data.worst_trade.pnl.toFixed(4)}` : "—"}
  449            sub={data.worst_trade?.symbol} color={data.worst_trade && data.worst_trade.pnl < 0 ? "text-red-400" : "text-emerald-400"} />
  450          <StatCard label="Win Streak"    value={streakLbl}
  451            sub={`Max: ${data.max_win_streak}W / ${data.max_loss_streak}L`}
  452            color={streakCol} />
  453        </div>
  454  
  455        {/* ── P&L by Asset ──────────────────────────────────────────── */}
  456        <div className="bg-slate-800 rounded-xl border border-slate-700/50 overflow-hidden">
  457          <div className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-slate-700/50">
  458            <span className="text-sm font-bold text-white">P&L by Asset</span>
  459          </div>
  460          <div className="p-4 space-y-3">
  461            {data.by_asset.map(a => {
  462              const isPos  = a.pnl >= 0;
  463              const barPct = (Math.abs(a.pnl) / maxAssetPnl) * 100;
  464              return (
  465                <div key={a.symbol}>
  466                  <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-1">
  467                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
  468                      <span className="text-sm font-bold text-white">{a.symbol.replace("/USD", "")}</span>
  469                      <span className="text-[10px] text-slate-500">{a.trades} trades · avg {a.avg_hold_min >= 60 ? `${(a.avg_hold_min/60).toFixed(1)}h` : `${a.avg_hold_min.toFixed(0)}m`}</span>
  470                    </div>
  471                    <div className="text-right">
  472                      <span className={`text-sm font-bold font-mono ${isPos ? "text-emerald-400" : "text-red-400"}`}>
  473                        {isPos ? "+" : ""}${a.pnl.toFixed(4)}
  474                      </span>
  475                      <span className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 ml-2">avg {isPos ? "+" : ""}${a.avg_pnl.toFixed(4)}</span>
  476                    </div>
  477                  </div>
  478                  <div className="h-1.5 bg-slate-700 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
  479                    <div
  480                      className={`h-full rounded-full transition-all ${isPos ? "bg-emerald-500/70" : "bg-red-500/70"}`}
  481                      style={{ width: `${barPct}%` }}
  482                    />
  483                  </div>
  484                </div>
  485              );
  486            })}
  487          </div>
  488        </div>
  489  
  490        {/* ── Win / Loss Profile ────────────────────────────────────── */}
  491        <div className="bg-slate-800 rounded-xl border border-slate-700/50 overflow-hidden">
  492          <div className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-slate-700/50">
  493            <span className="text-sm font-bold text-white">Win / Loss Profile</span>
  494          </div>
  495          <div className="p-4 space-y-3">
  496            <div>
  497              <div className="flex justify-between text-xs mb-1">
  498                <span className="text-emerald-400 font-semibold">Avg Win</span>
  499                <span className="text-emerald-400 font-mono font-bold">+${data.avg_win.toFixed(4)}</span>
  500              </div>
  501              <div className="h-2 bg-slate-700 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
  502                <div className="h-full bg-emerald-500/70 rounded-full"
  503                  style={{ width: `${Math.min((data.avg_win / Math.max(data.avg_win, Math.abs(data.avg_loss || 0.0001))) * 100, 100)}%` }} />
  504              </div>
  505            </div>
  506            {data.avg_loss !== 0 && (
  507              <div>
  508                <div className="flex justify-between text-xs mb-1">
  509                  <span className="text-red-400 font-semibold">Avg Loss</span>
  510                  <span className="text-red-400 font-mono font-bold">${data.avg_loss.toFixed(4)}</span>
  511                </div>
  512                <div className="h-2 bg-slate-700 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
  513                  <div className="h-full bg-red-500/70 rounded-full"
  514                    style={{ width: `${Math.min((Math.abs(data.avg_loss) / Math.max(data.avg_win, Math.abs(data.avg_loss))) * 100, 100)}%` }} />
  515                </div>
  516              </div>
  517            )}
  518            <div className="flex justify-between text-xs text-slate-500 pt-1 border-t border-slate-700/40">
  519              <span>
  520                Reward/Risk <span className="text-white font-semibold">
  521                  {data.avg_loss !== 0 ? (data.avg_win / Math.abs(data.avg_loss)).toFixed(2) : "∞"}x
  522                </span>
  523              </span>
  524              <span>
  525                Expectancy <span className={`font-semibold ${data.expectancy >= 0 ? "text-emerald-400" : "text-red-400"}`}>
  526                  {data.expectancy >= 0 ? "+" : ""}${data.expectancy.toFixed(4)}
  527                </span>
  528              </span>
  529            </div>
  530          </div>
  531        </div>
  532  
  533        {/* ── Equity Curve ──────────────────────────────────────────── */}
  534        {data.daily_pnl.length >= 2 && (
  535          <div className="bg-slate-800 rounded-xl border border-slate-700/50 overflow-hidden">
  536            <div className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-slate-700/50 flex items-center justify-between">
  537              <span className="text-sm font-bold text-white">Equity Curve</span>
  538              <span className={`text-sm font-bold font-mono ${data.total_pnl >= 0 ? "text-emerald-400" : "text-red-400"}`}>
  539                {data.total_pnl >= 0 ? "+" : ""}${data.total_pnl.toFixed(4)} cumulative
  540              </span>
  541            </div>
  542            <div className="p-4">
  543              <EquityCurve data={data.daily_pnl} />
  544            </div>
  545          </div>
  546        )}
  547  
  548        {/* ── Close Reason + Daily P&L side-by-side ─────────────────── */}
  549        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
  550          {/* Close Reasons */}
  551          <div className="bg-slate-800 rounded-xl border border-slate-700/50 overflow-hidden">
  552            <div className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-slate-700/50">
  553              <span className="text-sm font-bold text-white">Exit Reasons</span>
  554            </div>
  555            <div className="p-3 space-y-2">
  556              {data.by_reason.map(r => (
  557                <div key={r.reason} className="flex items-center justify-between">
  558                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
  559                    <ReasonBadge reasons={r.reason} />
  560                    <span className="text-xs text-slate-400">{r.trades} trades</span>
  561                  </div>
  562                  <span className={`text-xs font-mono font-bold ${r.pnl >= 0 ? "text-emerald-400" : "text-red-400"}`}>
  563                    {r.pnl >= 0 ? "+" : ""}${r.pnl.toFixed(4)}
  564                  </span>
  565                </div>
  566              ))}
  567            </div>
  568          </div>
  569  
  570          {/* Daily P&L */}
  571          <div className="bg-slate-800 rounded-xl border border-slate-700/50 overflow-hidden">
  572            <div className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-slate-700/50">
  573              <span className="text-sm font-bold text-white">Daily P&L</span>
  574            </div>
  575            <div className="divide-y divide-slate-700/30">
  576              {data.daily_pnl.length === 0 ? (
  577                <div className="p-4 text-xs text-slate-600">No data</div>
  578              ) : data.daily_pnl.map(d => (
  579                <div key={d.date} className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2">
  580                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
  581                    <span className="text-xs text-slate-400">{d.date}</span>
  582                    <span className="text-[10px] text-slate-600">{d.trades} trades</span>
  583                  </div>
  584                  <span className={`text-xs font-mono font-bold ${d.pnl >= 0 ? "text-emerald-400" : "text-red-400"}`}>
  585                    {d.pnl >= 0 ? "+" : ""}${d.pnl.toFixed(4)}
  586                  </span>
  587                </div>
  588              ))}
  589            </div>
  590          </div>
  591        </div>
  592      </div>
  593    );
  594  }
  595  
  596  // ── TRADES PAGE ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  597  function TradesPage({ positions, decisions, partialProfits, stops, totalPortfolio, closedToday, closedPeriod, setClosedPeriod }: {
  598    positions: Position[]; decisions: Decision[];
  599    partialProfits: PartialProfits; stops: Stops; totalPortfolio: number;
  600    closedToday: ClosedTodayItem[];
  601    closedPeriod: ClosedPeriod; setClosedPeriod: (p: ClosedPeriod) => void;
  602  }) {
  603    const closedTotalPnl      = (closedToday ?? []).reduce((s, c) => s + c.pnl, 0);
  604    const unrealizedTotalPos  = positions.reduce((s, p) => s + p.unrealized_pl, 0);
  605    const securedTotalPos     = Object.values(partialProfits).reduce((s, p) => s + p.secured_pnl, 0);
  606    const allocatedTotalPct   = positions.reduce((s, p) => s + p.cost_basis, 0) / Math.max(totalPortfolio, INITIAL_CAPITAL) * 100;
  607    const PERIODS: { key: ClosedPeriod; label: string }[] = [
  608      { key: "today", label: "Today" },
  609      { key: "week",  label: "Week"  },
  610      { key: "month", label: "Month" },
  611      { key: "ytd",   label: "YTD"   },
  612      { key: "all",   label: "All"   },
  613    ];
  614  
  615    return (
  616      <div className="p-4 sm:p-6 space-y-5">
  617        <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
  618          <h2 className="text-base font-bold text-white">Open Positions</h2>
  619          <span className="text-xs text-slate-600">{positions.length} active</span>
  620        </div>
  621        {positions.length === 0 ? (
  622          <div className="bg-slate-800/50 rounded-xl p-10 text-center text-slate-600 text-sm">
  623            No open positions
  624          </div>
  625        ) : (
  626          <div className="bg-slate-800 rounded-xl overflow-hidden border border-slate-700/50">
  627            <div className="overflow-x-auto">
  628              <table className="w-full">
  629                <thead>
  630                  <tr className="border-b border-slate-700">
  631                    {["Asset","Entry","Current","Unrealized","Secured","~Stop","Size",""].map(h => (
  632                      <th key={h} className="px-3 py-2 text-left text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wider text-slate-500 font-semibold">{h}</th>
  633                    ))}
  634                  </tr>
  635                </thead>
  636                <tbody className="divide-y divide-slate-700/50">
  637                  {positions.map(p => (
  638                    <PositionRow key={p.symbol} pos={p} decisions={decisions}
  639                      partialProfits={partialProfits} stops={stops} totalPortfolio={totalPortfolio} />
  640                  ))}
  641                </tbody>
  642                <tfoot>
  643                  <tr className="border-t-2 border-slate-600 bg-slate-900/50">
  644                    <td className="px-3 py-2 text-[10px] text-slate-500 uppercase font-semibold tracking-wider" colSpan={2}>Total</td>
  645                    <td />
  646                    <td className="px-3 py-2">
  647                      <div className={`text-xs font-bold ${unrealizedTotalPos >= 0 ? "text-emerald-400" : "text-red-400"}`}>{fmtPnl(unrealizedTotalPos)}</div>
  648                    </td>
  649                    <td className="px-3 py-2">
  650                      {securedTotalPos > 0 && <span className="text-[10px] font-semibold text-emerald-400">✅ +${securedTotalPos.toFixed(2)}</span>}
  651                    </td>
  652                    <td />
  653                    <td className="px-3 py-2 text-xs font-semibold text-slate-400">{allocatedTotalPct.toFixed(1)}%</td>
  654                    <td />
  655                  </tr>
  656                </tfoot>
  657              </table>
  658            </div>
  659          </div>
  660        )}
  661  
  662        {/* ── Closed Trades (with period selector) ─────────────────── */}
  663        <div>
  664          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
  665            <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
  666              <h2 className="text-base font-bold text-white">Closed</h2>
  667              {/* Period pill selector */}
  668              <div className="flex items-center gap-0.5 bg-slate-800 rounded-lg p-0.5 border border-slate-700/50">
  669                {PERIODS.map(p => (
  670                  <button key={p.key} onClick={() => setClosedPeriod(p.key)}
  671                    className={`px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-semibold rounded transition-colors ${closedPeriod === p.key ? "bg-sky-600/30 text-sky-400" : "text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-300"}`}>
  672                    {p.label}
  673                  </button>
  674                ))}
  675              </div>
  676            </div>
  677            {(closedToday ?? []).length > 0 && (
  678              <span className={`text-sm font-bold font-mono ${closedTotalPnl >= 0 ? "text-emerald-400" : "text-red-400"}`}>
  679                {closedTotalPnl >= 0 ? "+" : "-"}${Math.abs(closedTotalPnl).toFixed(4)}
  680              </span>
  681            )}
  682          </div>
  683          {(closedToday ?? []).length === 0 ? (
  684            <div className="bg-slate-800/50 rounded-xl p-8 text-center text-slate-600 text-sm">
  685              No closed trades for this period
  686            </div>
  687          ) : (
  688            <div className="bg-slate-800 rounded-xl overflow-hidden border border-slate-700/50">
  689              <table className="w-full">
  690                <thead>
  691                  <tr className="border-b border-slate-700">
  692                    {["Asset","Realized P&L","# Trades","Qty Sold","Last Exit","Type"].map(h => (
  693                      <th key={h} className="px-3 py-2 text-left text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wider text-slate-500 font-semibold">{h}</th>
  694                    ))}
  695                  </tr>
  696                </thead>
  697                <tbody className="divide-y divide-slate-700/50">
  698                  {closedToday.map(c => {
  699                    const isPos = c.pnl >= 0;
  700                    return (
  701                      <tr key={c.symbol} className={`border-l-2 ${isPos ? "border-emerald-600/70" : "border-red-600/70"}`}>
  702                        <td className="px-3 py-2.5">
  703                          <span className="font-bold text-white text-sm">{c.symbol.replace("/USD","")}</span>
  704                        </td>
  705                        <td className="px-3 py-2.5">
  706                          <span className={`text-sm font-bold font-mono ${isPos ? "text-emerald-400" : "text-red-400"}`}>
  707                            {isPos ? "+" : "-"}${Math.abs(c.pnl).toFixed(4)}
  708                          </span>
  709                        </td>
  710                        <td className="px-3 py-2.5 text-xs text-slate-400">{c.trade_count}</td>
  711                        <td className="px-3 py-2.5 text-xs text-slate-400 font-mono">{c.qty_sold.toFixed(6)}</td>
  712                        <td className="px-3 py-2.5 text-xs text-slate-500">{c.last_exit ? (closedPeriod === "today" ? fmtTime(c.last_exit) : fmtDateTime(c.last_exit)) : "—"}</td>
  713                        <td className="px-3 py-2.5"><ReasonBadge reasons={c.reasons} /></td>
  714                      </tr>
  715                    );
  716                  })}
  717                </tbody>
  718              </table>
  719            </div>
  720          )}
  721        </div>
  722      </div>
  723    );
  724  }
  725  
  726  // ── MARKET PAGE ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  727  function MarketPage({ movers, sentiment, regime }: {
  728    movers: Mover[]; sentiment: SentimentResponse | null; regime: RegimeResponse | null;
  729  }) {
  730    const [calHovered, setCalHovered] = useState<string | null>(null);
  731    const [mobileSection, setMobileSection] = useState<"movers" | "calendar" | null>(null);
  732  
  733    const regimeLabel = regime?.regime ?? "UNKNOWN";
  734    const rb          = regimeBadgeStyle(regimeLabel);
  735    const sentColor   = sentiment?.sentiment?.includes("bull") ? "text-emerald-400" :
  736                        sentiment?.sentiment?.includes("bear") ? "text-red-400" : "text-slate-400";
  737    const headlines   = sentiment?.headlines ?? [];
  738    const alerts      = sentiment?.alerts ?? [];
  739    const trumpSignal = alerts.find(a => a.toLowerCase().includes("trump")) ?? null;
  740    const upcoming    = EARNINGS_CALENDAR
  741      .filter(e => { const d = new Date(e.date + "T12:00:00Z"); return d >= new Date(Date.now() - 86400_000); })
  742      .sort((a, b) => a.date.localeCompare(b.date))
  743      .slice(0, 6);
  744  
  745    return (
  746      <div className="p-4 sm:p-6">
  747        {/* Desktop: 3 equal columns */}
  748        <div className="hidden sm:grid grid-cols-3 gap-4">
  749          {/* LEFT: Top Movers */}
  750          <div className="bg-slate-800 rounded-xl border border-slate-700/50 overflow-hidden">
  751            <div className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-slate-700 flex items-center justify-between">
  752              <span className="text-xs font-bold text-slate-300 uppercase tracking-wider">Top Movers</span>
  753              <span className="text-[9px] text-slate-600">60s refresh</span>
  754            </div>
  755            <div className="p-3 space-y-1.5">
  756              {movers.length === 0
  757                ? <div className="text-xs text-slate-600 text-center py-6">Fetching movers…</div>
  758                : movers.map(m => (
  759                  <div key={m.symbol} className="flex items-center justify-between py-1.5 border-b border-slate-700/30 last:border-0">
  760                    <span className="text-sm font-bold text-white">{m.symbol.replace("/USD","")}</span>
  761                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
  762                      <span className="text-xs font-mono text-slate-400">${fmtPrice(m.price)}</span>
  763                      <span className={`text-xs font-bold ${m.direction === "up" ? "text-emerald-400" : "text-red-400"}`}>
  764                        {m.direction === "up" ? "▲" : "▼"} {Math.abs(m.change_pct).toFixed(2)}%
  765                      </span>
  766                    </div>
  767                  </div>
  768                ))}
  769            </div>
  770          </div>
  771  
  772          {/* CENTER: Market Sentiment + Regime */}
  773          <SentimentColumn sentiment={sentiment} regime={regime} headlines={headlines}
  774            trumpSignal={trumpSignal} rb={rb} regimeLabel={regimeLabel} sentColor={sentColor} />
  775  
  776          {/* RIGHT: Calendar */}
  777          <div className="bg-slate-800 rounded-xl border border-slate-700/50 overflow-hidden">
  778            <div className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-slate-700">
  779              <span className="text-xs font-bold text-slate-300 uppercase tracking-wider">Calendar</span>
  780            </div>
  781            <div className="p-3 space-y-2">
  782              <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 uppercase tracking-wider mb-1">Macro Events</div>
  783              {MACRO_EVENTS.map(e => (
  784                <div key={e.event} className="bg-slate-900/40 rounded-lg p-2.5 border border-slate-700/30">
  785                  <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
  786                    <span className="text-xs font-semibold text-slate-300">{e.event}</span>
  787                    <span className="text-[10px] text-amber-400 font-mono">{daysUntil(e.date)}</span>
  788                  </div>
  789                  <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-600 mt-0.5">{e.note}</div>
  790                </div>
  791              ))}
  792              <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 uppercase tracking-wider mt-3 mb-1">Earnings</div>
  793              {upcoming.map(e => (
  794                <div key={e.symbol}
  795                  className="bg-slate-900/40 rounded-lg p-2.5 border border-slate-700/30 cursor-pointer hover:border-amber-700/50 transition-colors"
  796                  onMouseEnter={() => setCalHovered(e.symbol)}
  797                  onMouseLeave={() => setCalHovered(null)}
  798                >
  799                  <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
  800                    <span className="text-xs font-bold text-white">{e.symbol}</span>
  801                    <span className="text-[10px] text-amber-400 font-mono">{daysUntil(e.date)}</span>
  802                  </div>
  803                  {calHovered === e.symbol && (
  804                    <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-400 mt-1 leading-snug">{e.whisper}</div>
  805                  )}
  806                </div>
  807              ))}
  808            </div>
  809          </div>
  810        </div>
  811  
  812        {/* Mobile: sentiment first, then collapsibles */}
  813        <div className="sm:hidden space-y-4">
  814          <SentimentColumn sentiment={sentiment} regime={regime} headlines={headlines}
  815            trumpSignal={trumpSignal} rb={rb} regimeLabel={regimeLabel} sentColor={sentColor} />
  816          <button className="w-full flex items-center justify-between bg-slate-800 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 border border-slate-700/50"
  817            onClick={() => setMobileSection(mobileSection === "movers" ? null : "movers")}>
  818            <span className="text-xs font-semibold text-slate-300">📊 Top Movers</span>
  819            <span className="text-slate-600">{mobileSection === "movers" ? "▲" : "▼"}</span>
  820          </button>
  821          {mobileSection === "movers" && (
  822            <div className="bg-slate-800 rounded-xl border border-slate-700/50 p-3 space-y-1.5">
  823              {movers.map(m => (
  824                <div key={m.symbol} className="flex items-center justify-between py-1.5 border-b border-slate-700/30 last:border-0">
  825                  <span className="text-sm font-bold text-white">{m.symbol.replace("/USD","")}</span>
  826                  <span className={`text-xs font-bold ${m.direction === "up" ? "text-emerald-400" : "text-red-400"}`}>
  827                    {m.direction === "up" ? "▲" : "▼"} {Math.abs(m.change_pct).toFixed(2)}%
  828                  </span>
  829                </div>
  830              ))}
  831            </div>
  832          )}
  833          <button className="w-full flex items-center justify-between bg-slate-800 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 border border-slate-700/50"
  834            onClick={() => setMobileSection(mobileSection === "calendar" ? null : "calendar")}>
  835            <span className="text-xs font-semibold text-slate-300">📅 Calendar</span>
  836            <span className="text-slate-600">{mobileSection === "calendar" ? "▲" : "▼"}</span>
  837          </button>
  838          {mobileSection === "calendar" && (
  839            <div className="bg-slate-800 rounded-xl border border-slate-700/50 p-3 space-y-2">
  840              {upcoming.map(e => (
  841                <div key={e.symbol} className="bg-slate-900/40 rounded-lg p-2.5 border border-slate-700/30"
  842                  onClick={() => setCalHovered(calHovered === e.symbol ? null : e.symbol)}>
  843                  <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
  844                    <span className="text-xs font-bold text-white">{e.symbol}</span>
  845                    <span className="text-[10px] text-amber-400">{daysUntil(e.date)}</span>
  846                  </div>
  847                  {calHovered === e.symbol && <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-400 mt-1">{e.whisper}</div>}
  848                </div>
  849              ))}
  850            </div>
  851          )}
  852        </div>
  853      </div>
  854    );
  855  }
  856  
  857  function SentimentColumn({ sentiment, regime, headlines, trumpSignal, rb, regimeLabel, sentColor }: {
  858    sentiment: SentimentResponse | null; regime: RegimeResponse | null;
  859    headlines: string[]; trumpSignal: string | null;
  860    rb: ReturnType<typeof regimeBadgeStyle>; regimeLabel: string; sentColor: string;
  861  }) {
  862    const sentimentLabel = sentiment?.sentiment?.replace("_", " ").toUpperCase() ?? "—";
  863    const params = regime?.params as Record<string, unknown> | undefined;
  864  
  865    return (
  866      <div className="bg-slate-800 rounded-xl border border-slate-700/50 overflow-hidden">
  867        <div className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-slate-700">
  868          <span className="text-xs font-bold text-slate-300 uppercase tracking-wider">Market Sentiment</span>
  869        </div>
  870        <div className="p-4 space-y-3">
  871          {/* Regime */}
  872          <div className={`flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 rounded-lg border ${rb.bg}`}>
  873            <span className="text-base">{rb.emoji}</span>
  874            <div>
  875              <div className={`text-sm font-bold ${rb.text}`}>
  876                {regimeLabel === "UNKNOWN" ? "Loading…" : regimeLabel.replace("_MARKET","").replace("TRENDING_","")}
  877              </div>
  878              <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-500">Market Regime</div>
  879            </div>
  880            {params && (
  881              <div className="ml-auto text-right">
  882                {params["vix"] !== undefined && params["vix"] !== null && (
  883                  <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-500">VIX <span className="text-slate-300">{String(params["vix"])}</span></div>
  884                )}
  885                {params["position_size_multiplier"] !== undefined && (
  886                  <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-500">Size <span className="text-slate-300">{((params["position_size_multiplier"] as number) * 100).toFixed(0)}%</span></div>
  887                )}
  888              </div>
  889            )}
  890          </div>
  891  
  892          {/* VIX Fear Gauge */}
  893          {params?.["vix"] !== undefined && params?.["vix"] !== null && (() => {
  894            const vix = params["vix"] as number;
  895            const vixColor = vix < 15 ? "text-emerald-400" : vix < 25 ? "text-yellow-400" : vix < 35 ? "text-orange-400" : "text-red-400";
  896            const barColor = vix < 15 ? "bg-emerald-500" : vix < 25 ? "bg-yellow-500" : vix < 35 ? "bg-orange-500" : "bg-red-500";
  897            const zone = vix < 15 ? "Calm" : vix < 25 ? "Normal" : vix < 35 ? "Fear" : "Panic";
  898            return (
  899              <div>
  900                <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-1.5">
  901                  <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 uppercase tracking-wider">VIX Fear Gauge</div>
  902                  <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
  903                    <span className={`text-[10px] font-semibold ${vixColor}`}>{zone}</span>
  904                    <span className={`text-xs font-bold font-mono ${vixColor}`}>{vix.toFixed(1)}</span>
  905                  </div>
  906                </div>
  907                <div className="h-2.5 bg-slate-700 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
  908                  <div className={`h-full rounded-full transition-all ${barColor}`}
  909                    style={{ width: `${Math.min(vix / 50 * 100, 100)}%` }} />
  910                </div>
  911                <div className="flex justify-between text-[8px] text-slate-600 mt-0.5">
  912                  <span>15</span><span>25</span><span>35</span><span>50+</span>
  913                </div>
  914              </div>
  915            );
  916          })()}
  917  
  918          {/* Sentiment */}
  919          <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
  920            <div>
  921              <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 uppercase tracking-wider">News Sentiment</div>
  922              <div className={`text-base font-bold ${sentColor}`}>{sentimentLabel}</div>
  923            </div>
  924            <div className="text-right">
  925              <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-500">Score</div>
  926              <div className={`text-lg font-bold font-mono ${(sentiment?.score ?? 0) >= 0 ? "text-emerald-400" : "text-red-400"}`}>
  927                {(sentiment?.score ?? 0) >= 0 ? "+" : ""}{sentiment?.score ?? "—"}
  928              </div>
  929            </div>
  930          </div>
  931  
  932          {/* Trump signal */}
  933          {trumpSignal && (
  934            <div className="bg-amber-900/20 border border-amber-700/40 rounded-lg px-3 py-2 flex items-center gap-2">
  935              <span className="text-base">🇺🇸</span>
  936              <span className="text-[11px] text-amber-300">{trumpSignal}</span>
  937            </div>
  938          )}
  939  
  940          {/* Headlines */}
  941          {headlines.length > 0 && (
  942            <div className="space-y-1.5">
  943              <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Top Headlines</div>
  944              {headlines.slice(0, 3).map((hl, i) => {
  945                const tier = inferHeadlineTier(hl);
  946                return (
  947                  <div key={i} className="flex items-start gap-1.5 py-1.5 border-b border-slate-700/30 last:border-0">
  948                    <TierBadge tier={tier} />
  949                    <span className="text-[11px] text-slate-400 leading-snug line-clamp-2">{hl}</span>
  950                  </div>
  951                );
  952              })}
  953            </div>
  954          )}
  955  
  956          {sentiment?.ts && (
  957            <div className="text-[9px] text-slate-700 text-right">Updated {fmtTime(sentiment.ts)}</div>
  958          )}
  959        </div>
  960      </div>
  961    );
  962  }
  963  
  964  // ── SIGNALS PAGE ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  965  function SignalRow({ dec }: { dec: Decision }) {
  966    const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(false);
  967    const breakdown = parseSynthesisBreakdown(dec.reasoning);
  968    const patterns  = parsePatternsFromMarketData(dec.market_data);
  969    const regimeStr = parseRegimeFromReasoning(dec.reasoning);
  970    const conf      = Math.round(dec.confidence * 100);
  971    const finalScore = breakdown?.final ?? null;
  972  
  973    return (
  974      <>
  975        <tr className="hover:bg-slate-800/50 cursor-pointer transition-colors" onClick={() => setExpanded(v => !v)}>
  976          <td className="px-3 py-2.5 text-xs text-slate-500 whitespace-nowrap">{fmtDateTime(dec.decided_at)}</td>
  977          <td className="px-3 py-2.5 font-bold text-white text-sm">{dec.symbol.replace("/USD","")}</td>
  978          <td className="px-3 py-2.5"><DecisionBadge decision={dec.decision} /></td>
  979          <td className="px-3 py-2.5">
  980            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
  981              <div className="w-16 h-1.5 bg-slate-700 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
  982                <div className={`h-full rounded-full ${conf >= 80 ? "bg-emerald-500" : conf >= 60 ? "bg-sky-500" : "bg-slate-500"}`} style={{ width: `${conf}%` }} />
  983              </div>
  984              <span className="text-xs text-slate-400">{conf}%</span>
  985            </div>
  986          </td>
  987          <td className="px-3 py-2.5 text-xs font-bold font-mono text-sky-400">{finalScore ?? "—"}</td>
  988          <td className="px-3 py-2.5">
  989            <span className={`text-[10px] font-semibold ${regimeStr.includes("BEAR") ? "text-red-400" : regimeStr.includes("BULL") ? "text-emerald-400" : "text-slate-500"}`}>
  990              {regimeStr}
  991            </span>
  992          </td>
  993          <td className="px-3 py-2.5 text-slate-600 text-xs">{expanded ? "▲" : "▼"}</td>
  994        </tr>
  995        {expanded && (
  996          <tr>
  997            <td colSpan={7} className="px-4 pb-4 pt-1 bg-slate-800/30">
  998              <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 gap-4 mt-2">
  999                {/* Score breakdown */}
 1000                {breakdown && (
 1001                  <div>
 1002                    <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 uppercase tracking-wider font-semibold mb-2">Synthesis Breakdown</div>
 1003                    <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-1">
 1004                      {[
 1005                        ["Base", breakdown.base, false],
 1006                        ["Regime", breakdown.regime, true],
 1007                        ["RelStr", breakdown.relStr, true],
 1008                        ["DXY", breakdown.dxy, true],
 1009                        ["Corr", breakdown.corr, true],
 1010                        ["Geo", breakdown.geo, true],
 1011                        ["News", breakdown.news, true],
 1012                        ["FINAL", breakdown.final, false],
 1013                      ].map(([label, val, signed]) => (
 1014                        <div key={label as string} className={`text-center rounded p-1.5 ${label === "FINAL" ? "bg-sky-900/40 col-span-2" : "bg-slate-800"}`}>
 1015                          <div className="text-[8px] text-slate-600 uppercase">{label as string}</div>
 1016                          <div className={`text-xs font-bold ${typeof val === "number" && val > 0 ? "text-emerald-400" : typeof val === "number" && val < 0 ? "text-red-400" : "text-slate-300"}`}>
 1017                            {signed && typeof val === "number" && val > 0 ? "+" : ""}{val as number}
 1018                          </div>
 1019                        </div>
 1020                      ))}
 1021                    </div>
 1022                    {patterns.length > 0 && (
 1023                      <div className="flex items-center gap-1 flex-wrap mt-2">
 1024                        <span className="text-[9px] text-slate-600">Patterns:</span>
 1025                        {patterns.map(p => (
 1026                          <span key={p} className="text-[9px] bg-violet-900/40 text-violet-400 border border-violet-700/50 rounded px-1.5 py-0.5">{p}</span>
 1027                        ))}
 1028                      </div>
 1029                    )}
 1030                  </div>
 1031                )}
 1032                {/* Claude reasoning */}
 1033                <div>
 1034                  <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 uppercase tracking-wider font-semibold mb-2">Claude Reasoning</div>
 1035                  <div className="bg-slate-900/60 rounded p-2.5 max-h-36 overflow-y-auto border-l-2 border-sky-700/40">
 1036                    <p className="text-[10px] text-slate-400 leading-relaxed whitespace-pre-wrap">
 1037                      {dec.reasoning.replace(/Breakdown:.*$/m, "").trim()}
 1038                    </p>
 1039                  </div>
 1040                </div>
 1041              </div>
 1042            </td>
 1043          </tr>
 1044        )}
 1045      </>
 1046    );
 1047  }
 1048  
 1049  function SignalsPage({ decisions }: { decisions: Decision[] }) {
 1050    const [filter,  setFilter]  = useState<"ALL" | "BUY" | "SELL" | "HOLD">("ALL");
 1051    const [showAll, setShowAll] = useState(false);
 1052  
 1053    const latestBySymbol: Record<string, Decision> = {};
 1054    decisions.forEach(d => { if (!latestBySymbol[d.symbol]) latestBySymbol[d.symbol] = d; });
 1055    const deduped  = Object.values(latestBySymbol).sort((a, b) => b.decided_at.localeCompare(a.decided_at));
 1056    const baseList = showAll ? [...decisions].sort((a, b) => b.decided_at.localeCompare(a.decided_at)) : deduped;
 1057    const filtered = filter === "ALL" ? baseList : baseList.filter(d => d.decision.toUpperCase() === filter);
 1058  
 1059    return (
 1060      <div className="p-4 sm:p-6">
 1061        {/* Filter bar */}
 1062        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-4 flex-wrap">
 1063          {(["ALL", "BUY", "SELL", "HOLD"] as const).map(f => (
 1064            <button key={f} onClick={() => setFilter(f)}
 1065              className={`px-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-semibold rounded transition-colors ${filter === f
 1066                ? f === "BUY"  ? "bg-emerald-900/50 text-emerald-400 border border-emerald-700"
 1067                : f === "SELL" ? "bg-red-900/50 text-red-400 border border-red-700"
 1068                : f === "HOLD" ? "bg-slate-700 text-slate-300 border border-slate-600"
 1069                : "bg-sky-900/40 text-sky-400 border border-sky-700"
 1070                : "text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-300 border border-transparent"}`}>
 1071              {f}
 1072            </button>
 1073          ))}
 1074          <button onClick={() => setShowAll(v => !v)}
 1075            className={`px-2.5 py-1.5 text-[10px] rounded border font-semibold transition-colors ml-1 ${showAll ? "bg-violet-900/30 text-violet-400 border-violet-700" : "text-slate-500 border-slate-700 hover:text-slate-400"}`}>
 1076            {showAll ? "History" : "Latest"}
 1077          </button>
 1078          <span className="ml-auto text-xs text-slate-600">
 1079            {filtered.length} signal{filtered.length !== 1 ? "s" : ""}{showAll ? " (full history)" : " (latest per asset)"}
 1080          </span>
 1081        </div>
 1082  
 1083        {filtered.length === 0 ? (
 1084          <div className="bg-slate-800/50 rounded-xl p-10 text-center text-slate-600 text-sm">No signals yet</div>
 1085        ) : (
 1086          <div className="bg-slate-800 rounded-xl overflow-hidden border border-slate-700/50">
 1087            <div className="overflow-x-auto">
 1088              <table className="w-full">
 1089                <thead>
 1090                  <tr className="border-b border-slate-700">
 1091                    {["Time","Asset","Signal","Confidence","Score","Regime",""].map(h => (
 1092                      <th key={h} className="px-3 py-2 text-left text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wider text-slate-500 font-semibold">{h}</th>
 1093                    ))}
 1094                  </tr>
 1095                </thead>
 1096                <tbody className="divide-y divide-slate-700/50">
 1097                  {filtered.map(d => <SignalRow key={`${d.symbol}-${d.decided_at}`} dec={d} />)}
 1098                </tbody>
 1099              </table>
 1100            </div>
 1101          </div>
 1102        )}
 1103      </div>
 1104    );
 1105  }
 1106  
 1107  // ── HOME PAGE (Performance Overview) ─────────────────────────────────────────
 1108  function DailyBarChart({ trades }: { trades: Trade[] }) {
 1109    const closed = trades.filter(t => t.pnl != null);
 1110    if (closed.length === 0) return <div className="text-xs text-slate-600 text-center py-6">No closed trades yet</div>;
 1111    const byDay: Record<string, number> = {};
 1112    closed.forEach(t => {
 1113      const d = new Date(t.timestamp.includes("T") ? t.timestamp : t.timestamp.replace(" ", "T") + "Z");
 1114      const k = d.toISOString().slice(0, 10);
 1115      byDay[k] = (byDay[k] ?? 0) + (t.pnl ?? 0);
 1116    });
 1117    const days = Object.keys(byDay).sort();
 1118    const vals = days.map(k => byDay[k]);
 1119    const maxAbs = Math.max(...vals.map(Math.abs), 0.01);
 1120    const BW = 18, GAP = 6, CH = 56, LH = 14, MY = CH / 2;
 1121    const TW = Math.max(days.length * (BW + GAP) - GAP, 260);
 1122    const SVG_H = CH + LH + 12;
 1123    const dayLabel = (k: string) => { const d = new Date(k + "T00:00:00Z"); return `${d.getDate()}/${d.getMonth()+1}`; };
 1124    return (
 1125      <div className="overflow-x-auto">
 1126        <svg viewBox={`-4 -4 ${TW + 8} ${SVG_H}`} width="100%" height={SVG_H} style={{ minWidth: `${TW}px` }} preserveAspectRatio="none">
 1127          <line x1={-4} y1={MY} x2={TW+4} y2={MY} stroke="#334155" strokeWidth="1" />
 1128          {days.map((day, i) => {
 1129            const val = vals[i];
 1130            const barH = Math.max(Math.abs(val) / maxAbs * (MY - 3), val !== 0 ? 2 : 1);
 1131            const x = i * (BW + GAP);
 1132            const y = val >= 0 ? MY - barH : MY;
 1133            const fill = val > 0 ? "#10b981" : val < 0 ? "#ef4444" : "#475569";
 1134            return (
 1135              <g key={day}>
 1136                <rect x={x} y={y} width={BW} height={barH} fill={fill} rx="1" />
 1137                <text x={x + BW/2} y={CH + LH} textAnchor="middle" fill="#475569" fontSize="7">{dayLabel(day)}</text>
 1138                {val !== 0 && <text x={x + BW/2} y={val >= 0 ? y - 2 : y + barH + 7} textAnchor="middle" fill={fill} fontSize="7" fontWeight="bold">{val >= 0 ? "+" : ""}{val.toFixed(1)}</text>}
 1139              </g>
 1140            );
 1141          })}
 1142        </svg>
 1143      </div>
 1144    );
 1145  }
 1146  
 1147  function MonthlyBarChart({ trades }: { trades: Trade[] }) {
 1148    const closed = trades.filter(t => t.pnl != null);
 1149    if (closed.length === 0) return <div className="text-xs text-slate-600 text-center py-6">No closed trades yet</div>;
 1150  
 1151    const now = new Date();
 1152    const startYear = now.getFullYear();
 1153    const allMonths: string[] = [];
 1154    for (let m = 0; m < 12; m++) {
 1155      allMonths.push(`${startYear}-${String(m+1).padStart(2,"0")}`);
 1156    }
 1157    const byMonth: Record<string, number> = {};
 1158    allMonths.forEach(k => { byMonth[k] = 0; });
 1159    closed.forEach(t => {
 1160      const d = new Date(t.timestamp.includes("T") ? t.timestamp : t.timestamp.replace(" ", "T") + "Z");
 1161      const k = `${d.getFullYear()}-${String(d.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,"0")}`;
 1162      if (k in byMonth) byMonth[k] = (byMonth[k] ?? 0) + (t.pnl ?? 0);
 1163    });
 1164    const ck     = `${now.getFullYear()}-${String(now.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,"0")}`;
 1165    const months = allMonths;
 1166    const vals   = months.map(k => byMonth[k]);
 1167  
 1168    const activeVals = vals.filter(v => v !== 0);
 1169    const maxAbs = Math.max(...activeVals.map(Math.abs), 0.01);
 1170  
 1171    const ytd: number[] = [];
 1172    let cum = 0;
 1173    vals.forEach(v => { cum += v; ytd.push(cum); });
 1174  
 1175    const BW = 22, GAP = 8, CH = 52, LH = 14, MY = CH / 2;
 1176    const TW = months.length * (BW + GAP) - GAP;
 1177    const SVG_H = CH + LH + 24;
 1178    const ML = (k: string) => ["Jan","Feb","Mar","Apr","May","Jun","Jul","Aug","Sep","Oct","Nov","Dec"][parseInt(k.split("-")[1],10)-1];
 1179  
 1180    return (
 1181      <div className="overflow-x-auto">
 1182        <svg viewBox={`-4 -18 ${TW + 8} ${SVG_H}`} width="100%" height={SVG_H} style={{ minWidth: `${Math.max(TW, 260)}px` }} preserveAspectRatio="none">
 1183          <line x1={-4} y1={MY} x2={TW+4} y2={MY} stroke="#334155" strokeWidth="1" />
 1184          {months.map((m, i) => {
 1185            const val   = vals[i];
 1186            const ytdV  = ytd[i];
 1187            const barH  = Math.max(Math.abs(val) / maxAbs * (MY - 4), val !== 0 ? 2 : 1);
 1188            const x     = i * (BW + GAP);
 1189            const y     = val >= 0 ? MY - barH : MY;
 1190            const fill  = val > 0 ? "#10b981" : val < 0 ? "#ef4444" : "#334155";
 1191            const cur   = m === ck;
 1192            const ytdFill = ytdV > 0 ? "#22d3ee" : ytdV < 0 ? "#f87171" : "#475569";
 1193            const isFuture = m > ck;
 1194            return (
 1195              <g key={m} opacity={isFuture ? 0.25 : 1}>
 1196                <rect x={x} y={y} width={BW} height={barH} fill={fill} rx="1" opacity={cur ? 0.65 : 1} />
 1197                {cur && <rect x={x} y={y} width={BW} height={barH} fill="none" stroke={fill} strokeWidth="1" rx="1" strokeDasharray="3 2" />}
 1198                <text x={x + BW/2} y={CH + LH} textAnchor="middle" fill={cur ? "#94a3b8" : "#475569"} fontSize="8">{ML(m)}</text>
 1199                {val !== 0 && (
 1200                  <text x={x + BW/2} y={val >= 0 ? y - 2 : y + barH + 7} textAnchor="middle" fill={fill} fontSize="6.5" fontWeight="bold">
 1201                    {val >= 0 ? "+" : ""}{val.toFixed(1)}
 1202                  </text>
 1203                )}
 1204                {ytdV !== 0 && !isFuture && (
 1205                  <text x={x + BW/2} y={-8} textAnchor="middle" fill={ytdFill} fontSize="6.5" fontWeight="bold">
 1206                    {ytdV >= 0 ? "+" : ""}{ytdV.toFixed(1)}
 1207                  </text>
 1208                )}
 1209              </g>
 1210            );
 1211          })}
 1212        </svg>
 1213        <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mt-1">
 1214          <div className="flex items-center gap-1"><span className="w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-cyan-400 inline-block" /><span className="text-[9px] text-slate-600">YTD running total</span></div>
 1215          <div className="text-[9px] text-slate-600 ml-auto">* current month</div>
 1216        </div>
 1217      </div>
 1218    );
 1219  }
 1220  
 1221  function HomePage({ trades, decisions, stats, positions, portfolioValue, account, analysis }: {
 1222    trades: Trade[]; decisions: Decision[];
 1223    stats: StatsResponse | null; positions: Position[]; portfolioValue: number;
 1224    account: AccountResponse | null; analysis: AnalysisData | null;
 1225  }) {
 1226    const totalReturn    = ((portfolioValue - INITIAL_CAPITAL) / INITIAL_CAPITAL) * 100;
 1227    const grossPnl       = portfolioValue - INITIAL_CAPITAL;
 1228    const now            = new Date();
 1229    const mDecisions     = decisions.filter(d => {
 1230      const dt = new Date(d.decided_at.includes("T") ? d.decided_at : d.decided_at.replace(" ", "T") + "Z");
 1231      return dt.getMonth() === now.getMonth() && dt.getFullYear() === now.getFullYear();
 1232    });
 1233    const claudeCost     = mDecisions.length * CLAUDE_COST_PER_CALL;
 1234    const totalCost      = REPLIT_MONTHLY_COST + claudeCost;
 1235    const netPnl         = grossPnl - totalCost;
 1236    const unrealizedTotal = positions.reduce((s, p) => s + p.unrealized_pl, 0);
 1237    const allocatedPct    = positions.reduce((s, p) => s + p.cost_basis, 0) / Math.max(portfolioValue, INITIAL_CAPITAL) * 100;
 1238  
 1239    const kpis = [
 1240      {
 1241        label: "Total Return",
 1242        value: (totalReturn >= 0 ? "+" : "") + totalReturn.toFixed(2) + "%",
 1243        sub: (grossPnl >= 0 ? "+" : "−") + "$" + Math.abs(grossPnl).toFixed(2),
 1244        color: totalReturn >= 0 ? "text-emerald-400" : "text-red-400",
 1245      },
 1246      {
 1247        label: "Win Rate",
 1248        value: stats ? stats.win_rate.toFixed(1) + "%" : "—",
 1249        sub: analysis ? `${analysis.winning_trades}W / ${analysis.losing_trades}L` : undefined,
 1250        color: "text-sky-400",
 1251      },
 1252      {
 1253        label: "Profit Factor",
 1254        value: stats ? (stats.profit_factor >= 999 ? "∞" : stats.profit_factor.toFixed(2)) : "—",
 1255        sub: analysis ? `$${analysis.gross_win.toFixed(2)} gross` : undefined,
 1256        color: "text-violet-400",
 1257      },
 1258      {
 1259        label: "Best Asset",
 1260        value: stats?.best_asset ?? "—",
 1261        sub: stats?.best_asset && stats.asset_pnl[stats.best_asset] !== undefined
 1262          ? `+$${(stats.asset_pnl[stats.best_asset] ?? 0).toFixed(2)}`
 1263          : undefined,
 1264        color: "text-amber-400",
 1265      },
 1266    ];
 1267  
 1268    return (
 1269      <div className="p-4 sm:p-6 space-y-5">
 1270        {/* KPI row */}
 1271        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-4 gap-3">
 1272          {kpis.map(k => (
 1273            <div key={k.label} className="bg-slate-800 rounded-xl p-4 border border-slate-700/50">
 1274              <div className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-widest text-slate-500 mb-1">{k.label}</div>
 1275              <div className={`text-2xl font-bold ${k.color}`}>{k.value}</div>
 1276              {k.sub && <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-600 mt-0.5">{k.sub}</div>}
 1277            </div>
 1278          ))}
 1279        </div>
 1280  
 1281        {/* Portfolio Snapshot strip */}
 1282        {(positions.length > 0 || account) && (
 1283          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-4 gap-3">
 1284            <div className="bg-slate-800/60 rounded-xl p-3 border border-slate-700/30">
 1285              <div className="text-[10px] uppercase text-slate-600 mb-1">Unrealized</div>
 1286              <div className={`text-base font-bold font-mono ${unrealizedTotal >= 0 ? "text-emerald-400" : "text-red-400"}`}>
 1287                {fmtPnl(unrealizedTotal)}
 1288              </div>
 1289            </div>
 1290            <div className="bg-slate-800/60 rounded-xl p-3 border border-slate-700/30">
 1291              <div className="text-[10px] uppercase text-slate-600 mb-1">Cash</div>
 1292              <div className="text-base font-bold font-mono text-slate-300">
 1293                ${account ? account.cash.toFixed(0) : "—"}
 1294              </div>
 1295            </div>
 1296            <div className="bg-slate-800/60 rounded-xl p-3 border border-slate-700/30">
 1297              <div className="text-[10px] uppercase text-slate-600 mb-1">Allocated</div>
 1298              <div className="text-base font-bold font-mono text-slate-300">
 1299                {allocatedPct.toFixed(1)}%
 1300              </div>
 1301            </div>
 1302            <div className="bg-slate-800/60 rounded-xl p-3 border border-slate-700/30">
 1303              <div className="text-[10px] uppercase text-slate-600 mb-1">Positions</div>
 1304              <div className="text-base font-bold font-mono text-slate-300">
 1305                {positions.length} open
 1306              </div>
 1307            </div>
 1308          </div>
 1309        )}
 1310  
 1311        {/* Daily P&L chart */}
 1312        <div className="bg-slate-800 rounded-xl border border-slate-700/50 overflow-hidden">
 1313          <div className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-slate-700 flex items-center justify-between">
 1314            <span className="text-xs font-bold text-slate-300 uppercase tracking-wider">Daily P&L</span>
 1315            <span className="text-xs text-slate-600">closed trades · per day</span>
 1316          </div>
 1317          <div className="p-4">
 1318            <DailyBarChart trades={trades} />
 1319          </div>
 1320        </div>
 1321  
 1322        {/* Monthly P&L chart */}
 1323        <div className="bg-slate-800 rounded-xl border border-slate-700/50 overflow-hidden">
 1324          <div className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-slate-700 flex items-center justify-between">
 1325            <span className="text-xs font-bold text-slate-300 uppercase tracking-wider">Monthly P&L</span>
 1326            <span className="text-xs text-slate-600">closed trades · by month</span>
 1327          </div>
 1328          <div className="p-4">
 1329            <MonthlyBarChart trades={trades} />
 1330          </div>
 1331        </div>
 1332  
 1333        {/* Costs */}
 1334        <div className="bg-slate-800 rounded-xl border border-slate-700/50 overflow-hidden">
 1335          <div className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-slate-700">
 1336            <span className="text-xs font-bold text-slate-300 uppercase tracking-wider">💸 Monthly Costs — {now.toLocaleString("default", { month: "long", year: "numeric" })}</span>
 1337          </div>
 1338          <div className="p-4 space-y-2 max-w-sm">
 1339            {/* Alpaca gross P&L */}
 1340            <div className="flex justify-between text-xs border-b border-slate-700 pb-2 mb-1">
 1341              <span className="text-slate-400">Gross P&L (Alpaca)</span>
 1342              <span className={`font-mono font-bold ${grossPnl >= 0 ? "text-emerald-400" : "text-red-400"}`}>
 1343                {grossPnl >= 0 ? "+" : "-"}${Math.abs(grossPnl).toFixed(2)}
 1344              </span>
 1345            </div>
 1346            {/* Costs */}
 1347            {[
 1348              ["Replit Core", `-$${REPLIT_MONTHLY_COST.toFixed(2)}`, "text-red-400"],
 1349              [`Claude API (${mDecisions.length} calls × $0.003)`, `-$${claudeCost.toFixed(3)}`, "text-red-400"],
 1350              ["Total Costs", `-$${totalCost.toFixed(2)}`, "text-red-400 font-bold"],
 1351            ].map(([label, value, cls]) => (
 1352              <div key={label as string} className={`flex justify-between text-xs ${cls as string}`}>
 1353                <span className="text-slate-400">{label as string}</span>
 1354                <span className="font-mono">{value as string}</span>
 1355              </div>
 1356            ))}
 1357            {/* Net result */}
 1358            <div className="flex justify-between text-sm border-t border-slate-700 pt-2 mt-1">
 1359              <span className="text-slate-300 font-semibold">Net P&L (after costs)</span>
 1360              <span className={`font-mono font-bold text-base ${netPnl >= 0 ? "text-emerald-400" : "text-red-400"}`}>
 1361                {netPnl >= 0 ? "+" : "-"}${Math.abs(netPnl).toFixed(2)}
 1362              </span>
 1363            </div>
 1364          </div>
 1365        </div>
 1366      </div>
 1367    );
 1368  }
 1369  
 1370  // ── App ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 1371  export default function App() {
 1372    const [activePage, setActivePage] = useState<Page>("HOME");
 1373    const [status,     setStatus]     = useState<Status | null>(null);
 1374    const [decisions,  setDecisions]  = useState<Decision[]>([]);
 1375    const [positions,  setPositions]  = useState<Position[]>([]);
 1376    const [movers,     setMovers]     = useState<Mover[]>([]);
 1377    const [sentiment,  setSentiment]  = useState<SentimentResponse | null>(null);
 1378    const [regime,     setRegime]     = useState<RegimeResponse | null>(null);
 1379    const [stats,      setStats]      = useState<StatsResponse | null>(null);
 1380    const [partialProfits, setPartialProfits] = useState<PartialProfits>({});
 1381    const [stops,      setStops]      = useState<Stops>({});
 1382    const [account,      setAccount]      = useState<AccountResponse | null>(null);
 1383    const [closedToday,  setClosedToday]  = useState<ClosedTodayItem[]>([]);
 1384    const [closedPeriod, setClosedPeriod] = useState<ClosedPeriod>("today");
 1385    const [analysis,     setAnalysis]     = useState<AnalysisData | null>(null);
 1386    const [lastRefresh,  setLastRefresh]  = useState<Date>(new Date());
 1387    const [error,        setError]        = useState(false);
 1388  
 1389    const fetchAll = useCallback(async () => {
 1390      try {
 1391        const [sRes, dRes, pRes, mRes, senRes, regRes, stRes, ppRes, stopsRes, accRes, anlRes] = await Promise.all([
 1392          fetch(`${BASE}/api/status`),
 1393          fetch(`${BASE}/api/decisions`),
 1394          fetch(`${BASE}/api/positions`),
 1395          fetch(`${BASE}/api/movers`),
 1396          fetch(`${BASE}/api/sentiment`),
 1397          fetch(`${BASE}/api/regime`),
 1398          fetch(`${BASE}/api/stats`),
 1399          fetch(`${BASE}/api/partial-profits`),
 1400          fetch(`${BASE}/api/stops`),
 1401          fetch(`${BASE}/api/account`),
 1402          fetch(`${BASE}/api/analysis`),
 1403        ]);
 1404        if (sRes.ok)     { const d = await sRes.json() as Status;   setStatus(d); }
 1405        if (dRes.ok)     { const d = await dRes.json();             setDecisions(d.decisions ?? []); }
 1406        if (pRes.ok)     { const d = await pRes.json();             setPositions(d.positions ?? []); }
 1407        if (mRes.ok)     { const d = await mRes.json();             setMovers(d.movers ?? []); }
 1408        if (senRes.ok)   setSentiment(await senRes.json() as SentimentResponse);
 1409        if (regRes.ok)   setRegime(await regRes.json() as RegimeResponse);
 1410        if (stRes.ok)    setStats(await stRes.json() as StatsResponse);
 1411        if (ppRes.ok)    { const d = await ppRes.json(); setPartialProfits(d.partial_profits ?? {}); }
 1412        if (stopsRes.ok) { const d = await stopsRes.json(); setStops(d.stops ?? {}); }
 1413        if (accRes.ok)   { const d = await accRes.json() as AccountResponse; if (d.portfolio_value > 0) setAccount(d); }
 1414        if (anlRes.ok)   { const d = await anlRes.json(); if (d.total_trades !== undefined) setAnalysis(d as AnalysisData); }
 1415        setError(false);
 1416      } catch { setError(true); }
 1417      setLastRefresh(new Date());
 1418    }, []);
 1419  
 1420    // ── Period-aware closed fetch — re-runs when period changes ────────────────
 1421    const fetchClosed = useCallback(async (period: ClosedPeriod) => {
 1422      try {
 1423        const res = await fetch(`${BASE}/api/closed-today?period=${period}`);
 1424        if (res.ok) { const d = await res.json(); setClosedToday(d.closed ?? []); }
 1425      } catch { /* silent */ }
 1426    }, []);
 1427  
 1428    useEffect(() => {
 1429      fetchAll();
 1430      const id = setInterval(fetchAll, 15_000);
 1431      return () => clearInterval(id);
 1432    }, [fetchAll]);
 1433  
 1434    // Initial + period-change fetch for closed trades
 1435    useEffect(() => { fetchClosed(closedPeriod); }, [closedPeriod, fetchClosed]);
 1436    // Also re-fetch closed on every main refresh cycle
 1437    useEffect(() => { fetchClosed(closedPeriod); }, [lastRefresh]); // eslint-disable-line
 1438  
 1439    // Derived state — use real Alpaca equity when available, fall back to computed
 1440    const unrealizedTotal = positions.reduce((s, p) => s + p.unrealized_pl, 0);
 1441    const closedPnl       = stats?.total_pnl ?? status?.recent_trades.filter(t => t.pnl != null).reduce((s,t) => s + (t.pnl ?? 0), 0) ?? 0;
 1442    const portfolioValue  = account?.portfolio_value && account.portfolio_value > 0
 1443      ? account.portfolio_value
 1444      : INITIAL_CAPITAL + closedPnl + unrealizedTotal;
 1445    const portfolioDelta  = ((portfolioValue - INITIAL_CAPITAL) / INITIAL_CAPITAL) * 100;
 1446    const allTrades       = status?.recent_trades ?? [];
 1447  
 1448    return (
 1449      <div className="min-h-screen bg-slate-900 text-slate-200">
 1450        <TopNav
 1451          activePage={activePage}
 1452          setActivePage={setActivePage}
 1453          regime={regime?.regime ?? "UNKNOWN"}
 1454          portfolioValue={portfolioValue}
 1455          portfolioDelta={portfolioDelta}
 1456          positionsCount={positions.length}
 1457          lastRefresh={lastRefresh}
 1458          error={error}
 1459        />
 1460        {/* Page content — push below fixed nav */}
 1461        <div className="pt-14">
 1462          {activePage === "HOME"     && <HomePage trades={allTrades} decisions={decisions} stats={stats} positions={positions} portfolioValue={portfolioValue} account={account} analysis={analysis} />}
 1463          {activePage === "MARKET"   && <MarketPage movers={movers} sentiment={sentiment} regime={regime} />}
 1464          {activePage === "SIGNALS"  && <SignalsPage decisions={decisions} />}
 1465          {activePage === "TRADES"   && <TradesPage positions={positions} decisions={decisions} partialProfits={partialProfits} stops={stops} totalPortfolio={portfolioValue} closedToday={closedToday} closedPeriod={closedPeriod} setClosedPeriod={setClosedPeriod} />}
 1466          {activePage === "ANALYSIS" && <AnalysisPage data={analysis} />}
 1467        </div>
 1468      </div>
 1469    );
 1470  }

  282  
  283  /**
  284   * Using the elevate system.
  285   * Automatic contrast adjustment.
  286   *
  287   * <element className="hover-elevate" />
  288   * <element className="active-elevate-2" />
  289   *
  290   * // Using the tailwind utility when a data attribute is "on"
  291   * <element className="toggle-elevate data-[state=on]:toggle-elevated" />
  292   * // Or manually controlling the toggle state
  293   * <element className="toggle-elevate toggle-elevated" />
  294   *
  295   * Elevation systems have to handle many states.
  296   * - not-hovered, vs. hovered vs. active  (three mutually exclusive states)
  297   * - toggled or not
  298   * - focused or not (this is not handled with these utilities)
  299   *
  300   * Even without handling focused or not, this is six possible combinations that
  301   * need to be distinguished from eachother visually.
  302   */
  303  @layer utilities {
  304  
  305    /* Hide ugly search cancel button in Chrome until we can style it properly */
  306    input[type="search"]::-webkit-search-cancel-button {
  307      @apply hidden;
  308    }
  309  
  310    /* Placeholder styling for contentEditable div */
  311    [contenteditable][data-placeholder]:empty::before {
  312      content: attr(data-placeholder);
  313      color: hsl(var(--muted-foreground));
  314      pointer-events: none;
  315    }
  316  
  317    /* .no-default-hover-elevate/no-default-active-elevate is an escape hatch so consumers of
  318     * buttons/badges can remove the automatic brightness adjustment on interactions
  319     * and program their own. */
  320    .no-default-hover-elevate {}
  321  
  322    .no-default-active-elevate {}
  323  
  324  
  325    /**
  326     * Toggleable backgrounds go behind the content. Hoverable/active goes on top.
  327     * This way they can stack/compound. Both will overlap the parent's borders!
  328     * So borders will be automatically adjusted both on toggle, and hover/active,
  329     * and they will be compounded.
  330     */
  331    .toggle-elevate::before,
  332    .toggle-elevate-2::before {
  333      content: "";
  334      pointer-events: none;
  335      position: absolute;
  336      inset: 0px;
  337      /*border-radius: inherit;   match rounded corners */
  338      border-radius: inherit;
  339      z-index: -1;
  340      /* sits behind content but above backdrop */
  341    }
  342  
  343    .toggle-elevate.toggle-elevated::before {
  344      background-color: var(--elevate-2);
  345    }
  346  
  347    /* If there's a 1px border, adjust the inset so that it covers that parent's border */
  348    .border.toggle-elevate::before {
  349      inset: -1px;
  350    }
  351  
  352    /* Does not work on elements with overflow:hidden! */
  353    .hover-elevate:not(.no-default-hover-elevate),
  354    .active-elevate:not(.no-default-active-elevate),
  355    .hover-elevate-2:not(.no-default-hover-elevate),
  356    .active-elevate-2:not(.no-default-active-elevate) {
  357      position: relative;
  358      z-index: 0;
  359    }
  360  
  361    .hover-elevate:not(.no-default-hover-elevate)::after,
  362    .active-elevate:not(.no-default-active-elevate)::after,
  363    .hover-elevate-2:not(.no-default-hover-elevate)::after,
  364    .active-elevate-2:not(.no-default-active-elevate)::after {
  365      content: "";
  366      pointer-events: none;
  367      position: absolute;
  368      inset: 0px;
  369      /*border-radius: inherit;   match rounded corners */
  370      border-radius: inherit;
  371      z-index: 999;
  372      /* sits in front of content */
  373    }
  374  
  375    .hover-elevate:hover:not(.no-default-hover-elevate)::after,
  376    .active-elevate:active:not(.no-default-active-elevate)::after {
  377      background-color: var(--elevate-1);
  378    }
  379  
  380    .hover-elevate-2:hover:not(.no-default-hover-elevate)::after,
  381    .active-elevate-2:active:not(.no-default-active-elevate)::after {
  382      background-color: var(--elevate-2);
  383    }
  384  
  385    /* If there's a 1px border, adjust the inset so that it covers that parent's border */
  386    .border.hover-elevate:not(.no-hover-interaction-elevate)::after,
  387    .border.active-elevate:not(.no-active-interaction-elevate)::after,
  388    .border.hover-elevate-2:not(.no-hover-interaction-elevate)::after,
  389    .border.active-elevate-2:not(.no-active-interaction-elevate)::after,
  390    .border.hover-elevate:not(.no-hover-interaction-elevate)::after {
  391      inset: -1px;
  392    }
  393  }
